					<seg id="b.GEN.50.13" type="verse">
						For his sons carried him into the land of Canaan, and buried him in the cave of the field of Machpelah, which Abraham bought with the field for a possession of a buryingplace of Ephron the Hittite, before Mamre.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.GEN.50.14" type="verse">
						And Joseph returned into Egypt, he, and his brethren, and all that went up with him to bury his father, after he had buried his father.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.GEN.50.15" type="verse">
						And when Joseph's brethren saw that their father was dead, they said, Joseph will peradventure hate us, and will certainly requite us all the evil which we did unto him.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.GEN.50.16" type="verse">
						And they sent a messenger unto Joseph, saying, Thy father did command before he died, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.GEN.50.17" type="verse">
						So shall ye say unto Joseph, Forgive, I pray thee now, the trespass of thy brethren, and their sin; for they did unto thee evil: and now, we pray thee, forgive the trespass of the servants of the God of thy father. And Joseph wept when they spake unto him.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.GEN.50.18" type="verse">
						And his brethren also went and fell down before his face; and they said, Behold, we be thy servants.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.GEN.50.19" type="verse">
						And Joseph said unto them, Fear not: for am I in the place of God?
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.GEN.50.20" type="verse">
						But as for you, ye thought evil against me; but God meant it unto good, to bring to pass, as it is this day, to save much people alive.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.GEN.50.21" type="verse">
						Now therefore fear ye not: I will nourish you, and your little ones. And he comforted them, and spake kindly unto them.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.GEN.50.22" type="verse">
						And Joseph dwelt in Egypt, he, and his father's house: and Joseph lived an hundred and ten years.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.GEN.50.23" type="verse">
						And Joseph saw Ephraim's children of the third generation: the children also of Machir the son Manasseh were brought up upon Joseph's knees.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.GEN.50.24" type="verse">
						And Joseph said unto his brethren, I die: and God will surely visit you, and bring you out of this land unto the land which he sware to Abraham, to Isaac, and to Jacob.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.GEN.50.25" type="verse">
						And Joseph took an oath of the children of Israel, saying, God will surely visit you, and ye shall carry up my bones from hence.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.GEN.50.26" type="verse">
						So Joseph died, being an hundred and ten years old: and they embalmed him, and he was put in a coffin in Egypt.
					</seg>
				</div>
			</div>
			<div id="b.EXO" type="book">
				<div id="b.EXO.1" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.EXO.1.1" type="verse">
						Now these are the names of the children of Israel, which came into Egypt; every man and his household came with Jacob.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.1.2" type="verse">
						Reuben, Simeon, Levi, and Judah,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.1.3" type="verse">
						Issachar, Zebulun, and Benjamin,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.1.4" type="verse">
						Dan, and Naphtali, Gad, and Asher.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.1.5" type="verse">
						And all the souls that came out of the loins of Jacob were seventy souls: for Joseph was in Egypt already.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.1.6" type="verse">
						And Joseph died, and all his brethren, and all that generation.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.1.7" type="verse">
						And the children of Israel were fruitful, and increased abundantly, and multiplied, and waxed exceeding mighty; and the land was filled with them.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.1.8" type="verse">
						Now there arose up a new king over Egypt, which knew not Joseph.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.1.9" type="verse">
						And he said unto his people, Behold, the people of the children of Israel are more and mightier than we:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.1.10" type="verse">
						Come on, let us deal wisely with them; lest they multiply, and it come to pass, that, when there falleth out any war, they join also unto our enemies, and fight against us, and so get them up out of the land.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.1.11" type="verse">
						Therefore they did set over them taskmasters to afflict them with their burdens. And they built for Pharaoh treasure cities, Pithom and Raamses.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.1.12" type="verse">
						But the more they afflicted them, the more they multiplied and grew. And they were grieved because of the children of Israel.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.1.13" type="verse">
						And the Egyptians made the children of Israel to serve with rigour:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.1.14" type="verse">
						And they made their lives bitter with hard bondage, in morter, and in brick, and in all manner of service in the field: all their service, wherein they made them serve, was with rigour.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.1.15" type="verse">
						And the king of Egypt spake to the Hebrew midwives, of which the name of the one was Shiphrah, and the name of the other Puah:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.1.16" type="verse">
						And he said, When ye do the office of a midwife to the Hebrew women, and see them upon the stools; if it be a son, then ye shall kill him: but if it be a daughter, then she shall live.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.1.17" type="verse">
						But the midwives feared God, and did not as the king of Egypt commanded them, but saved the men children alive.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.1.18" type="verse">
						And the king of Egypt called for the midwives, and said unto them, Why have ye done this thing, and have saved the men children alive?
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.1.19" type="verse">
						And the midwives said unto Pharaoh, Because the Hebrew women are not as the Egyptian women; for they are lively, and are delivered ere the midwives come in unto them.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.1.20" type="verse">
						Therefore God dealt well with the midwives: and the people multiplied, and waxed very mighty.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.1.21" type="verse">
						And it came to pass, because the midwives feared God, that he made them houses.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.1.22" type="verse">
						And Pharaoh charged all his people, saying, Every son that is born ye shall cast into the river, and every daughter ye shall save alive.
					</seg>
				</div>
				<div id="b.EXO.2" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.EXO.2.1" type="verse">
						And there went a man of the house of Levi, and took to wife a daughter of Levi.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.2.2" type="verse">
						And the woman conceived, and bare a son: and when she saw him that he was a goodly child, she hid him three months.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.2.3" type="verse">
						And when she could not longer hide him, she took for him an ark of bulrushes, and daubed it with slime and with pitch, and put the child therein; and she laid it in the flags by the river's brink.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.2.4" type="verse">
						And his sister stood afar off, to wit what would be done to him.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.2.5" type="verse">
						And the daughter of Pharaoh came down to wash herself at the river; and her maidens walked along by the river's side; and when she saw the ark among the flags, she sent her maid to fetch it.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.2.6" type="verse">
						And when she had opened it, she saw the child: and, behold, the babe wept. And she had compassion on him, and said, This is one of the Hebrews' children.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.2.7" type="verse">
						Then said his sister to Pharaoh's daughter, Shall I go and call to thee a nurse of the Hebrew women, that she may nurse the child for thee?
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.2.8" type="verse">
						And Pharaoh's daughter said to her, Go. And the maid went and called the child's mother.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.2.9" type="verse">
						And Pharaoh's daughter said unto her, Take this child away, and nurse it for me, and I will give thee thy wages. And the woman took the child, and nursed it.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.2.10" type="verse">
						And the child grew, and she brought him unto Pharaoh's daughter, and he became her son. And she called his name Moses: and she said, Because I drew him out of the water.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.2.11" type="verse">
						And it came to pass in those days, when Moses was grown, that he went out unto his brethren, and looked on their burdens: and he spied an Egyptian smiting an Hebrew, one of his brethren.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.2.12" type="verse">
						And he looked this way and that way, and when he saw that there was no man, he slew the Egyptian, and hid him in the sand.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.2.13" type="verse">
						And when he went out the second day, behold, two men of the Hebrews strove together: and he said to him that did the wrong, Wherefore smitest thou thy fellow?
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.2.14" type="verse">
						And he said, Who made thee a prince and a judge over us? intendest thou to kill me, as thou killedst the Egyptian? And Moses feared, and said, Surely this thing is known.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.2.15" type="verse">
						Now when Pharaoh heard this thing, he sought to slay Moses. But Moses fled from the face of Pharaoh, and dwelt in the land of Midian: and he sat down by a well.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.2.16" type="verse">
						Now the priest of Midian had seven daughters: and they came and drew water, and filled the troughs to water their father's flock.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.2.17" type="verse">
						And the shepherds came and drove them away: but Moses stood up and helped them, and watered their flock.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.2.18" type="verse">
						And when they came to Reuel their father, he said, How is it that ye are come so soon to day?
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.2.19" type="verse">
						And they said, An Egyptian delivered us out of the hand of the shepherds, and also drew water enough for us, and watered the flock.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.2.20" type="verse">
						And he said unto his daughters, And where is he? why is it that ye have left the man? call him, that he may eat bread.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.2.21" type="verse">
						And Moses was content to dwell with the man: and he gave Moses Zipporah his daughter.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.2.22" type="verse">
						And she bare him a son, and he called his name Gershom: for he said, I have been a stranger in a strange land.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.2.23" type="verse">
						And it came to pass in process of time, that the king of Egypt died: and the children of Israel sighed by reason of the bondage, and they cried, and their cry came up unto God by reason of the bondage.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.2.24" type="verse">
						And God heard their groaning, and God remembered his covenant with Abraham, with Isaac, and with Jacob.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.2.25" type="verse">
						And God looked upon the children of Israel, and God had respect unto them.
					</seg>
				</div>
				<div id="b.EXO.3" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.EXO.3.1" type="verse">
						Now Moses kept the flock of Jethro his father in law, the priest of Midian: and he led the flock to the backside of the desert, and came to the mountain of God, even to Horeb.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.3.2" type="verse">
						And the angel of the LORD appeared unto him in a flame of fire out of the midst of a bush: and he looked, and, behold, the bush burned with fire, and the bush was not consumed.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.3.3" type="verse">
						And Moses said, I will now turn aside, and see this great sight, why the bush is not burnt.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.3.4" type="verse">
						And when the LORD saw that he turned aside to see, God called unto him out of the midst of the bush, and said, Moses, Moses. And he said, Here am I.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.3.5" type="verse">
						And he said, Draw not nigh hither: put off thy shoes from off thy feet, for the place whereon thou standest is holy ground.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.3.6" type="verse">
						Moreover he said, I am the God of thy father, the God of Abraham, the God of Isaac, and the God of Jacob. And Moses hid his face; for he was afraid to look upon God.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.3.7" type="verse">
						And the LORD said, I have surely seen the affliction of my people which are in Egypt, and have heard their cry by reason of their taskmasters; for I know their sorrows;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.3.8" type="verse">
						And I am come down to deliver them out of the hand of the Egyptians, and to bring them up out of that land unto a good land and a large, unto a land flowing with milk and honey; unto the place of the Canaanites, and the Hittites, and the Amorites, and the Perizzites, and the Hivites, and the Jebusites.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.3.9" type="verse">
						Now therefore, behold, the cry of the children of Israel is come unto me: and I have also seen the oppression wherewith the Egyptians oppress them.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.3.10" type="verse">
						Come now therefore, and I will send thee unto Pharaoh, that thou mayest bring forth my people the children of Israel out of Egypt.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.3.11" type="verse">
						And Moses said unto God, Who am I, that I should go unto Pharaoh, and that I should bring forth the children of Israel out of Egypt?
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.3.12" type="verse">
						And he said, Certainly I will be with thee; and this shall be a token unto thee, that I have sent thee: When thou hast brought forth the people out of Egypt, ye shall serve God upon this mountain.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.3.13" type="verse">
						And Moses said unto God, Behold, when I come unto the children of Israel, and shall say unto them, The God of your fathers hath sent me unto you; and they shall say to me, What is his name? what shall I say unto them?
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.3.14" type="verse">
						And God said unto Moses, I AM THAT I AM: and he said, Thus shalt thou say unto the children of Israel, I AM hath sent me unto you.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.3.15" type="verse">
						And God said moreover unto Moses, Thus shalt thou say unto the children of Israel, The LORD God of your fathers, the God of Abraham, the God of Isaac, and the God of Jacob, hath sent me unto you: this is my name for ever, and this is my memorial unto all generations.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.3.16" type="verse">
						Go, and gather the elders of Israel together, and say unto them, The LORD God of your fathers, the God of Abraham, of Isaac, and of Jacob, appeared unto me, saying, I have surely visited you, and seen that which is done to you in Egypt:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.3.17" type="verse">
						And I have said, I will bring you up out of the affliction of Egypt unto the land of the Canaanites, and the Hittites, and the Amorites, and the Perizzites, and the Hivites, and the Jebusites, unto a land flowing with milk and honey.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.3.18" type="verse">
						And they shall hearken to thy voice: and thou shalt come, thou and the elders of Israel, unto the king of Egypt, and ye shall say unto him, The LORD God of the Hebrews hath met with us: and now let us go, we beseech thee, three days' journey into the wilderness, that we may sacrifice to the LORD our God.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.3.19" type="verse">
						And I am sure that the king of Egypt will not let you go, no, not by a mighty hand.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.3.20" type="verse">
						And I will stretch out my hand, and smite Egypt with all my wonders which I will do in the midst thereof: and after that he will let you go.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.3.21" type="verse">
						And I will give this people favour in the sight of the Egyptians: and it shall come to pass, that, when ye go, ye shall not go empty:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.3.22" type="verse">
						But every woman shall borrow of her neighbour, and of her that sojourneth in her house, jewels of silver, and jewels of gold, and raiment: and ye shall put them upon your sons, and upon your daughters; and ye shall spoil the Egyptians.
					</seg>
				</div>
				<div id="b.EXO.4" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.EXO.4.1" type="verse">
						And Moses answered and said, But, behold, they will not believe me, nor hearken unto my voice: for they will say, The LORD hath not appeared unto thee.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.4.2" type="verse">
						And the LORD said unto him, What is that in thine hand? And he said, A rod.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.4.3" type="verse">
						And he said, Cast it on the ground. And he cast it on the ground, and it became a serpent; and Moses fled from before it.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.4.4" type="verse">
						And the LORD said unto Moses, Put forth thine hand, and take it by the tail. And he put forth his hand, and caught it, and it became a rod in his hand:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.4.5" type="verse">
						That they may believe that the LORD God of their fathers, the God of Abraham, the God of Isaac, and the God of Jacob, hath appeared unto thee.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.4.6" type="verse">
						And the LORD said furthermore unto him, Put now thine hand into thy bosom. And he put his hand into his bosom: and when he took it out, behold, his hand was leprous as snow.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.4.7" type="verse">
						And he said, Put thine hand into thy bosom again. And he put his hand into his bosom again; and plucked it out of his bosom, and, behold, it was turned again as his other flesh.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.4.8" type="verse">
						And it shall come to pass, if they will not believe thee, neither hearken to the voice of the first sign, that they will believe the voice of the latter sign.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.4.9" type="verse">
						And it shall come to pass, if they will not believe also these two signs, neither hearken unto thy voice, that thou shalt take of the water of the river, and pour it upon the dry land: and the water which thou takest out of the river shall become blood upon the dry land.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.4.10" type="verse">
						And Moses said unto the LORD, O my Lord, I am not eloquent, neither heretofore, nor since thou hast spoken unto thy servant: but I am slow of speech, and of a slow tongue.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.4.11" type="verse">
						And the LORD said unto him, Who hath made man's mouth? or who maketh the dumb, or deaf, or the seeing, or the blind? have not I the LORD?
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.4.12" type="verse">
						Now therefore go, and I will be with thy mouth, and teach thee what thou shalt say.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.4.13" type="verse">
						And he said, O my Lord, send, I pray thee, by the hand of him whom thou wilt send.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.4.14" type="verse">
						And the anger of the LORD was kindled against Moses, and he said, Is not Aaron the Levite thy brother? I know that he can speak well. And also, behold, he cometh forth to meet thee: and when he seeth thee, he will be glad in his heart.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.4.15" type="verse">
						And thou shalt speak unto him, and put words in his mouth: and I will be with thy mouth, and with his mouth, and will teach you what ye shall do.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.4.16" type="verse">
						And he shall be thy spokesman unto the people: and he shall be, even he shall be to thee instead of a mouth, and thou shalt be to him instead of God.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.4.17" type="verse">
						And thou shalt take this rod in thine hand, wherewith thou shalt do signs.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.4.18" type="verse">
						And Moses went and returned to Jethro his father in law, and said unto him, Let me go, I pray thee, and return unto my brethren which are in Egypt, and see whether they be yet alive. And Jethro said to Moses, Go in peace.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.4.19" type="verse">
						And the LORD said unto Moses in Midian, Go, return into Egypt: for all the men are dead which sought thy life.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.4.20" type="verse">
						And Moses took his wife and his sons, and set them upon an ass, and he returned to the land of Egypt: and Moses took the rod of God in his hand.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.4.21" type="verse">
						And the LORD said unto Moses, When thou goest to return into Egypt, see that thou do all those wonders before Pharaoh, which I have put in thine hand: but I will harden his heart, that he shall not let the people go.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.4.22" type="verse">
						And thou shalt say unto Pharaoh, Thus saith the LORD, Israel is my son, even my firstborn:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.4.23" type="verse">
						And I say unto thee, Let my son go, that he may serve me: and if thou refuse to let him go, behold, I will slay thy son, even thy firstborn.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.4.24" type="verse">
						And it came to pass by the way in the inn, that the LORD met him, and sought to kill him.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.4.25" type="verse">
						Then Zipporah took a sharp stone, and cut off the foreskin of her son, and cast it at his feet, and said, Surely a bloody husband art thou to me.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.4.26" type="verse">
						So he let him go: then she said, A bloody husband thou art, because of the circumcision.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.4.27" type="verse">
						And the LORD said to Aaron, Go into the wilderness to meet Moses. And he went, and met him in the mount of God, and kissed him.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.4.28" type="verse">
						And Moses told Aaron all the words of the LORD who had sent him, and all the signs which he had commanded him.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.4.29" type="verse">
						And Moses and Aaron went and gathered together all the elders of the children of Israel:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.4.30" type="verse">
						And Aaron spake all the words which the LORD had spoken unto Moses, and did the signs in the sight of the people.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.4.31" type="verse">
						And the people believed: and when they heard that the LORD had visited the children of Israel, and that he had looked upon their affliction, then they bowed their heads and worshipped.
					</seg>
				</div>
				<div id="b.EXO.5" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.EXO.5.1" type="verse">
						And afterward Moses and Aaron went in, and told Pharaoh, Thus saith the LORD God of Israel, Let my people go, that they may hold a feast unto me in the wilderness.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.5.2" type="verse">
						And Pharaoh said, Who is the LORD, that I should obey his voice to let Israel go? I know not the LORD, neither will I let Israel go.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.5.3" type="verse">
						And they said, The God of the Hebrews hath met with us: let us go, we pray thee, three days' journey into the desert, and sacrifice unto the LORD our God; lest he fall upon us with pestilence, or with the sword.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.5.4" type="verse">
						And the king of Egypt said unto them, Wherefore do ye, Moses and Aaron, let the people from their works? get you unto your burdens.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.5.5" type="verse">
						And Pharaoh said, Behold, the people of the land now are many, and ye make them rest from their burdens.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.5.6" type="verse">
						And Pharaoh commanded the same day the taskmasters of the people, and their officers, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.5.7" type="verse">
						Ye shall no more give the people straw to make brick, as heretofore: let them go and gather straw for themselves.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.5.8" type="verse">
						And the tale of the bricks, which they did make heretofore, ye shall lay upon them; ye shall not diminish ought thereof: for they be idle; therefore they cry, saying, Let us go and sacrifice to our God.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.5.9" type="verse">
						Let there more work be laid upon the men, that they may labour therein; and let them not regard vain words.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.5.10" type="verse">
						And the taskmasters of the people went out, and their officers, and they spake to the people, saying, Thus saith Pharaoh, I will not give you straw.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.5.11" type="verse">
						Go ye, get you straw where ye can find it: yet not ought of your work shall be diminished.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.5.12" type="verse">
						So the people were scattered abroad throughout all the land of Egypt to gather stubble instead of straw.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.5.13" type="verse">
						And the taskmasters hasted them, saying, Fulfil your works, your daily tasks, as when there was straw.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.5.14" type="verse">
						And the officers of the children of Israel, which Pharaoh's taskmasters had set over them, were beaten, and demanded, Wherefore have ye not fulfilled your task in making brick both yesterday and to day, as heretofore?
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.5.15" type="verse">
						Then the officers of the children of Israel came and cried unto Pharaoh, saying, Wherefore dealest thou thus with thy servants?
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.5.16" type="verse">
						There is no straw given unto thy servants, and they say to us, Make brick: and, behold, thy servants are beaten; but the fault is in thine own people.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.5.17" type="verse">
						But he said, Ye are idle, ye are idle: therefore ye say, Let us go and do sacrifice to the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.5.18" type="verse">
						Go therefore now, and work; for there shall no straw be given you, yet shall ye deliver the tale of bricks.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.5.19" type="verse">
						And the officers of the children of Israel did see that they were in evil case, after it was said, Ye shall not minish ought from your bricks of your daily task.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.5.20" type="verse">
						And they met Moses and Aaron, who stood in the way, as they came forth from Pharaoh:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.5.21" type="verse">
						And they said unto them, The LORD look upon you, and judge; because ye have made our savour to be abhorred in the eyes of Pharaoh, and in the eyes of his servants, to put a sword in their hand to slay us.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.5.22" type="verse">
						And Moses returned unto the LORD, and said, Lord, wherefore hast thou so evil entreated this people? why is it that thou hast sent me?
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.5.23" type="verse">
						For since I came to Pharaoh to speak in thy name, he hath done evil to this people; neither hast thou delivered thy people at all.
					</seg>

					</seg>

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.6.6" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.6.7" type="verse">

					</seg>

					</seg>

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.7.10" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.7.11" type="verse">

					</seg>

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.7.15" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.7.16" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.7.17" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.7.18" type="verse">
						And the fish that is in the river shall die, and the river shall stink; and the Egyptians shall lothe to drink of the water of the river.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.7.19" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses, Say unto Aaron, Take thy rod, and stretch out thine hand upon the waters of Egypt, upon their streams, upon their rivers, and upon their ponds, and upon all their pools of water, that they may become blood; and that there may be blood throughout all the land of Egypt, both in vessels of wood, and in vessels of stone.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.7.20" type="verse">
						And Moses and Aaron did so, as the LORD commanded; and he lifted up the rod, and smote the waters that were in the river, in the sight of Pharaoh, and in the sight of his servants; and all the waters that were in the river were turned to blood.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.7.21" type="verse">
						And the fish that was in the river died; and the river stank, and the Egyptians could not drink of the water of the river; and there was blood throughout all the land of Egypt.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.7.22" type="verse">
						And the magicians of Egypt did so with their enchantments: and Pharaoh's heart was hardened, neither did he hearken unto them; as the LORD had said.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.7.23" type="verse">
						And Pharaoh turned and went into his house, neither did he set his heart to this also.
					</seg>

					</seg>

					</seg>

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.8.4" type="verse">

					</seg>

					</seg>

					</seg>

					</seg>

					</seg>

					</seg>

					</seg>

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.8.17" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.8.18" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.8.20" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.8.21" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.8.22" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.8.23" type="verse">
						And I will put a division between my people and thy people: to morrow shall this sign be.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.8.24" type="verse">
						And the LORD did so; and there came a grievous swarm of flies into the house of Pharaoh, and into his servants' houses, and into all the land of Egypt: the land was corrupted by reason of the swarm of flies.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.8.25" type="verse">
						And Pharaoh called for Moses and for Aaron, and said, Go ye, sacrifice to your God in the land.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.8.26" type="verse">
						And Moses said, It is not meet so to do; for we shall sacrifice the abomination of the Egyptians to the LORD our God: lo, shall we sacrifice the abomination of the Egyptians before their eyes, and will they not stone us?
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.8.27" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.8.28" type="verse">
						And Pharaoh said, I will let you go, that ye may sacrifice to the LORD your God in the wilderness; only ye shall not go very far away: intreat for me.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.8.29" type="verse">
						And Moses said, Behold, I go out from thee, and I will intreat the LORD that the swarms of flies may depart from Pharaoh, from his servants, and from his people, to morrow: but let not Pharaoh deal deceitfully any more in not letting the people go to sacrifice to the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.8.30" type="verse">
						And Moses went out from Pharaoh, and intreated the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.8.31" type="verse">
						And the LORD did according to the word of Moses; and he removed the swarms of flies from Pharaoh, from his servants, and from his people; there remained not one.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.8.32" type="verse">
						And Pharaoh hardened his heart at this time also, neither would he let the people go.
					</seg>

				<div id="b.EXO.9" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.EXO.9.1" type="verse">
						Then the LORD said unto Moses, Go in unto Pharaoh, and tell him, Thus saith the LORD God of the Hebrews, Let my people go, that they may serve me.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.9.2" type="verse">
						For if thou refuse to let them go, and wilt hold them still,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.9.3" type="verse">
						Behold, the hand of the LORD is upon thy cattle which is in the field, upon the horses, upon the asses, upon the camels, upon the oxen, and upon the sheep: there shall be a very grievous murrain.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.9.4" type="verse">
						And the LORD shall sever between the cattle of Israel and the cattle of Egypt: and there shall nothing die of all that is the children's of Israel.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.9.5" type="verse">
						And the LORD appointed a set time, saying, To morrow the LORD shall do this thing in the land.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.9.6" type="verse">
						And the LORD did that thing on the morrow, and all the cattle of Egypt died: but of the cattle of the children of Israel died not one.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.9.7" type="verse">
						And Pharaoh sent, and, behold, there was not one of the cattle of the Israelites dead. And the heart of Pharaoh was hardened, and he did not let the people go.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.9.8" type="verse">
						And the LORD said unto Moses and unto Aaron, Take to you handfuls of ashes of the furnace, and let Moses sprinkle it toward the heaven in the sight of Pharaoh.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.9.9" type="verse">
						And it shall become small dust in all the land of Egypt, and shall be a boil breaking forth with blains upon man, and upon beast, throughout all the land of Egypt.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.9.10" type="verse">
						And they took ashes of the furnace, and stood before Pharaoh; and Moses sprinkled it up toward heaven; and it became a boil breaking forth with blains upon man, and upon beast.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.9.11" type="verse">
						And the magicians could not stand before Moses because of the boils; for the boil was upon the magicians, and upon all the Egyptians.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.9.12" type="verse">
						And the LORD hardened the heart of Pharaoh, and he hearkened not unto them; as the LORD had spoken unto Moses.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.9.13" type="verse">
						And the LORD said unto Moses, Rise up early in the morning, and stand before Pharaoh, and say unto him, Thus saith the LORD God of the Hebrews, Let my people go, that they may serve me.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.9.14" type="verse">
						For I will at this time send all my plagues upon thine heart, and upon thy servants, and upon thy people; that thou mayest know that there is none like me in all the earth.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.9.15" type="verse">
						For now I will stretch out my hand, that I may smite thee and thy people with pestilence; and thou shalt be cut off from the earth.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.9.16" type="verse">
						And in very deed for this cause have I raised thee up, for to shew in thee my power; and that my name may be declared throughout all the earth.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.9.17" type="verse">
						As yet exaltest thou thyself against my people, that thou wilt not let them go?
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.9.18" type="verse">
						Behold, to morrow about this time I will cause it to rain a very grievous hail, such as hath not been in Egypt since the foundation thereof even until now.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.9.19" type="verse">
						Send therefore now, and gather thy cattle, and all that thou hast in the field; for upon every man and beast which shall be found in the field, and shall not be brought home, the hail shall come down upon them, and they shall die.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.9.20" type="verse">
						He that feared the word of the LORD among the servants of Pharaoh made his servants and his cattle flee into the houses:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.9.21" type="verse">
						And he that regarded not the word of the LORD left his servants and his cattle in the field.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.9.22" type="verse">
						And the LORD said unto Moses, Stretch forth thine hand toward heaven, that there may be hail in all the land of Egypt, upon man, and upon beast, and upon every herb of the field, throughout the land of Egypt.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.9.23" type="verse">
						And Moses stretched forth his rod toward heaven: and the LORD sent thunder and hail, and the fire ran along upon the ground; and the LORD rained hail upon the land of Egypt.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.9.24" type="verse">
						So there was hail, and fire mingled with the hail, very grievous, such as there was none like it in all the land of Egypt since it became a nation.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.9.25" type="verse">
						And the hail smote throughout all the land of Egypt all that was in the field, both man and beast; and the hail smote every herb of the field, and brake every tree of the field.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.9.26" type="verse">
						Only in the land of Goshen, where the children of Israel were, was there no hail.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.9.27" type="verse">
						And Pharaoh sent, and called for Moses and Aaron, and said unto them, I have sinned this time: the LORD is righteous, and I and my people are wicked.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.9.28" type="verse">
						Intreat the LORD (for it is enough) that there be no more mighty thunderings and hail; and I will let you go, and ye shall stay no longer.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.9.29" type="verse">
						And Moses said unto him, As soon as I am gone out of the city, I will spread abroad my hands unto the LORD; and the thunder shall cease, neither shall there be any more hail; that thou mayest know how that the earth is the LORD's.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.9.30" type="verse">
						But as for thee and thy servants, I know that ye will not yet fear the LORD God.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.9.31" type="verse">
						And the flax and the barley was smitten: for the barley was in the ear, and the flax was bolled.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.9.32" type="verse">
						But the wheat and the rie were not smitten: for they were not grown up.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.9.33" type="verse">
						And Moses went out of the city from Pharaoh, and spread abroad his hands unto the LORD: and the thunders and hail ceased, and the rain was not poured upon the earth.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.9.34" type="verse">
						And when Pharaoh saw that the rain and the hail and the thunders were ceased, he sinned yet more, and hardened his heart, he and his servants.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.9.35" type="verse">
						And the heart of Pharaoh was hardened, neither would he let the children of Israel go; as the LORD had spoken by Moses.
					</seg>

				<div id="b.EXO.10" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.EXO.10.1" type="verse">
						And the LORD said unto Moses, Go in unto Pharaoh: for I have hardened his heart, and the heart of his servants, that I might shew these my signs before him:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.10.2" type="verse">
						And that thou mayest tell in the ears of thy son, and of thy son's son, what things I have wrought in Egypt, and my signs which I have done among them; that ye may know how that I am the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.10.3" type="verse">
						And Moses and Aaron came in unto Pharaoh, and said unto him, Thus saith the LORD God of the Hebrews, How long wilt thou refuse to humble thyself before me? let my people go, that they may serve me.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.10.4" type="verse">
						Else, if thou refuse to let my people go, behold, to morrow will I bring the locusts into thy coast:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.10.5" type="verse">
						And they shall cover the face of the earth, that one cannot be able to see the earth: and they shall eat the residue of that which is escaped, which remaineth unto you from the hail, and shall eat every tree which groweth for you out of the field:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.10.6" type="verse">
						And they shall fill thy houses, and the houses of all thy servants, and the houses of all the Egyptians; which neither thy fathers, nor thy fathers' fathers have seen, since the day that they were upon the earth unto this day. And he turned himself, and went out from Pharaoh.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.10.7" type="verse">
						And Pharaoh's servants said unto him, How long shall this man be a snare unto us? let the men go, that they may serve the LORD their God: knowest thou not yet that Egypt is destroyed?
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.10.8" type="verse">
						And Moses and Aaron were brought again unto Pharaoh: and he said unto them, Go, serve the LORD your God: but who are they that shall go?
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.10.9" type="verse">
						And Moses said, We will go with our young and with our old, with our sons and with our daughters, with our flocks and with our herds will we go; for we must hold a feast unto the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.10.10" type="verse">
						And he said unto them, Let the LORD be so with you, as I will let you go, and your little ones: look to it; for evil is before you.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.10.11" type="verse">
						Not so: go now ye that are men, and serve the LORD; for that ye did desire. And they were driven out from Pharaoh's presence.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.10.12" type="verse">
						And the LORD said unto Moses, Stretch out thine hand over the land of Egypt for the locusts, that they may come up upon the land of Egypt, and eat every herb of the land, even all that the hail hath left.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.10.13" type="verse">
						And Moses stretched forth his rod over the land of Egypt, and the LORD brought an east wind upon the land all that day, and all that night; and when it was morning, the east wind brought the locusts.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.10.14" type="verse">
						And the locusts went up over all the land of Egypt, and rested in all the coasts of Egypt: very grievous were they; before them there were no such locusts as they, neither after them shall be such.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.10.15" type="verse">
						For they covered the face of the whole earth, so that the land was darkened; and they did eat every herb of the land, and all the fruit of the trees which the hail had left: and there remained not any green thing in the trees, or in the herbs of the field, through all the land of Egypt.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.10.16" type="verse">
						Then Pharaoh called for Moses and Aaron in haste; and he said, I have sinned against the LORD your God, and against you.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.10.17" type="verse">
						Now therefore forgive, I pray thee, my sin only this once, and intreat the LORD your God, that he may take away from me this death only.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.10.18" type="verse">
						And he went out from Pharaoh, and intreated the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.10.19" type="verse">
						And the LORD turned a mighty strong west wind, which took away the locusts, and cast them into the Red sea; there remained not one locust in all the coasts of Egypt.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.10.20" type="verse">
						But the LORD hardened Pharaoh's heart, so that he would not let the children of Israel go.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.10.21" type="verse">
						And the LORD said unto Moses, Stretch out thine hand toward heaven, that there may be darkness over the land of Egypt, even darkness which may be felt.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.10.22" type="verse">
						And Moses stretched forth his hand toward heaven; and there was a thick darkness in all the land of Egypt three days:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.10.23" type="verse">
						They saw not one another, neither rose any from his place for three days: but all the children of Israel had light in their dwellings.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.10.24" type="verse">
						And Pharaoh called unto Moses, and said, Go ye, serve the LORD; only let your flocks and your herds be stayed: let your little ones also go with you.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.10.25" type="verse">
						And Moses said, Thou must give us also sacrifices and burnt offerings, that we may sacrifice unto the LORD our God.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.10.26" type="verse">
						Our cattle also shall go with us; there shall not an hoof be left behind; for thereof must we take to serve the LORD our God; and we know not with what we must serve the LORD, until we come thither.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.10.27" type="verse">
						But the LORD hardened Pharaoh's heart, and he would not let them go.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.10.28" type="verse">
						And Pharaoh said unto him, Get thee from me, take heed to thyself, see my face no more; for in that day thou seest my face thou shalt die.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.10.29" type="verse">
						And Moses said, Thou hast spoken well, I will see thy face again no more.
					</seg>

				<div id="b.EXO.11" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.EXO.11.1" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.11.2" type="verse">
						Speak now in the ears of the people, and let every man borrow of his neighbour, and every woman of her neighbour, jewels of silver, and jewels of gold.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.11.3" type="verse">
						And the LORD gave the people favour in the sight of the Egyptians. Moreover the man Moses was very great in the land of Egypt, in the sight of Pharaoh's servants, and in the sight of the people.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.11.4" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.11.5" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.11.6" type="verse">
						And there shall be a great cry throughout all the land of Egypt, such as there was none like it, nor shall be like it any more.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.11.7" type="verse">
						But against any of the children of Israel shall not a dog move his tongue, against man or beast: that ye may know how that the LORD doth put a difference between the Egyptians and Israel.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.11.8" type="verse">
						And all these thy servants shall come down unto me, and bow down themselves unto me, saying, Get thee out, and all the people that follow thee: and after that I will go out. And he went out from Pharaoh in a great anger.
					</seg>

					</seg>

						And Moses and Aaron did all these wonders before Pharaoh: and the LORD hardened Pharaoh's heart, so that he would not let the children of Israel go out of his land.
					</seg>

				<div id="b.EXO.12" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.1" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses and Aaron in the land of Egypt, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.2" type="verse">
						This month shall be unto you the beginning of months: it shall be the first month of the year to you.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.3" type="verse">
						Speak ye unto all the congregation of Israel, saying, In the tenth day of this month they shall take to them every man a lamb, according to the house of their fathers, a lamb for an house:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.4" type="verse">
						And if the household be too little for the lamb, let him and his neighbour next unto his house take it according to the number of the souls; every man according to his eating shall make your count for the lamb.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.5" type="verse">
						Your lamb shall be without blemish, a male of the first year: ye shall take it out from the sheep, or from the goats:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.6" type="verse">
						And ye shall keep it up until the fourteenth day of the same month: and the whole assembly of the congregation of Israel shall kill it in the evening.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.7" type="verse">
						And they shall take of the blood, and strike it on the two side posts and on the upper door post of the houses, wherein they shall eat it.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.8" type="verse">
						And they shall eat the flesh in that night, roast with fire, and unleavened bread; and with bitter herbs they shall eat it.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.9" type="verse">
						Eat not of it raw, nor sodden at all with water, but roast with fire; his head with his legs, and with the purtenance thereof.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.10" type="verse">
						And ye shall let nothing of it remain until the morning; and that which remaineth of it until the morning ye shall burn with fire.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.11" type="verse">
						And thus shall ye eat it; with your loins girded, your shoes on your feet, and your staff in your hand; and ye shall eat it in haste: it is the LORD's passover.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.12" type="verse">
						For I will pass through the land of Egypt this night, and will smite all the firstborn in the land of Egypt, both man and beast; and against all the gods of Egypt I will execute judgment: I am the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.13" type="verse">
						And the blood shall be to you for a token upon the houses where ye are: and when I see the blood, I will pass over you, and the plague shall not be upon you to destroy you, when I smite the land of Egypt.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.14" type="verse">
						And this day shall be unto you for a memorial; and ye shall keep it a feast to the LORD throughout your generations; ye shall keep it a feast by an ordinance for ever.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.15" type="verse">
						Seven days shall ye eat unleavened bread; even the first day ye shall put away leaven out of your houses: for whosoever eateth leavened bread from the first day until the seventh day, that soul shall be cut off from Israel.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.16" type="verse">
						And in the first day there shall be an holy convocation, and in the seventh day there shall be an holy convocation to you; no manner of work shall be done in them, save that which every man must eat, that only may be done of you.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.17" type="verse">
						And ye shall observe the feast of unleavened bread; for in this selfsame day have I brought your armies out of the land of Egypt: therefore shall ye observe this day in your generations by an ordinance for ever.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.18" type="verse">
						In the first month, on the fourteenth day of the month at even, ye shall eat unleavened bread, until the one and twentieth day of the month at even.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.19" type="verse">
						Seven days shall there be no leaven found in your houses: for whosoever eateth that which is leavened, even that soul shall be cut off from the congregation of Israel, whether he be a stranger, or born in the land.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.20" type="verse">
						Ye shall eat nothing leavened; in all your habitations shall ye eat unleavened bread.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.21" type="verse">
						Then Moses called for all the elders of Israel, and said unto them, Draw out and take you a lamb according to your families, and kill the passover.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.22" type="verse">
						And ye shall take a bunch of hyssop, and dip it in the blood that is in the bason, and strike the lintel and the two side posts with the blood that is in the bason; and none of you shall go out at the door of his house until the morning.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.23" type="verse">
						For the LORD will pass through to smite the Egyptians; and when he seeth the blood upon the lintel, and on the two side posts, the LORD will pass over the door, and will not suffer the destroyer to come in unto your houses to smite you.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.24" type="verse">
						And ye shall observe this thing for an ordinance to thee and to thy sons for ever.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.25" type="verse">
						And it shall come to pass, when ye be come to the land which the LORD will give you, according as he hath promised, that ye shall keep this service.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.26" type="verse">
						And it shall come to pass, when your children shall say unto you, What mean ye by this service?
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.27" type="verse">
						That ye shall say, It is the sacrifice of the LORD's passover, who passed over the houses of the children of Israel in Egypt, when he smote the Egyptians, and delivered our houses. And the people bowed the head and worshipped.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.28" type="verse">
						And the children of Israel went away, and did as the LORD had commanded Moses and Aaron, so did they.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.29" type="verse">
						And it came to pass, that at midnight the LORD smote all the firstborn in the land of Egypt, from the firstborn of Pharoah that sat on his throne unto the firstborn of the captive that was in the dungeon; and all the firstborn of cattle.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.30" type="verse">
						And Pharaoh rose up in the night, he, and all his servants, and all the Egyptians; and there was a great cry in Egypt; for there was not a house where there was not one dead.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.31" type="verse">
						And he called for Moses and Aaron by night, and said, Rise up, and get you forth from among my people, both ye and the children of Israel; and go, serve the LORD, as ye have said.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.32" type="verse">
						Also take your flocks and your herds, as ye have said, and be gone; and bless me also.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.33" type="verse">
						And the Egyptians were urgent upon the people, that they might send them out of the land in haste; for they said, We be all dead men.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.34" type="verse">
						And the people took their dough before it was leavened, their kneadingtroughs being bound up in their clothes upon their shoulders.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.35" type="verse">
						And the children of Israel did according to the word of Moses; and they borrowed of the Egyptians jewels of silver, and jewels of gold, and raiment:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.36" type="verse">
						And the LORD gave the people favour in the sight of the Egyptians, so that they lent unto them such things as they required. And they spoiled the Egyptians.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.37" type="verse">
						And the children of Israel journeyed from Rameses to Succoth, about six hundred thousand on foot that were men, beside children.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.38" type="verse">
						And a mixed multitude went up also with them; and flocks, and herds, even very much cattle.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.39" type="verse">
						And they baked unleavened cakes of the dough which they brought forth out of Egypt, for it was not leavened; because they were thrust out of Egypt, and could not tarry, neither had they prepared for themselves any victual.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.40" type="verse">
						Now the sojourning of the children of Israel, who dwelt in Egypt, was four hundred and thirty years.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.41" type="verse">
						And it came to pass at the end of the four hundred and thirty years, even the selfsame day it came to pass, that all the hosts of the LORD went out from the land of Egypt.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.42" type="verse">
						It is a night to be much observed unto the LORD for bringing them out from the land of Egypt: this is that night of the LORD to be observed of all the children of Israel in their generations.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.43" type="verse">
						And the LORD said unto Moses and Aaron, This is the ordinance of the passover: There shall no stranger eat thereof:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.44" type="verse">
						But every man's servant that is bought for money, when thou hast circumcised him, then shall he eat thereof.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.45" type="verse">
						A foreigner and an hired servant shall not eat thereof.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.46" type="verse">
						In one house shall it be eaten; thou shalt not carry forth ought of the flesh abroad out of the house; neither shall ye break a bone thereof.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.47" type="verse">
						All the congregation of Israel shall keep it.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.48" type="verse">
						And when a stranger shall sojourn with thee, and will keep the passover to the LORD, let all his males be circumcised, and then let him come near and keep it; and he shall be as one that is born in the land: for no uncircumcised person shall eat thereof.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.49" type="verse">
						One law shall be to him that is homeborn, and unto the stranger that sojourneth among you.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.50" type="verse">
						Thus did all the children of Israel; as the LORD commanded Moses and Aaron, so did they.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.12.51" type="verse">
						And it came to pass the selfsame day, that the LORD did bring the children of Israel out of the land of Egypt by their armies.
					</seg>

				<div id="b.EXO.13" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.EXO.13.1" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.13.2" type="verse">
						Sanctify unto me all the firstborn, whatsoever openeth the womb among the children of Israel, both of man and of beast: it is mine.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.13.3" type="verse">
						And Moses said unto the people, Remember this day, in which ye came out from Egypt, out of the house of bondage; for by strength of hand the LORD brought you out from this place: there shall no leavened bread be eaten.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.13.4" type="verse">
						This day came ye out in the month Abib.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.13.5" type="verse">
						And it shall be when the LORD shall bring thee into the land of the Canaanites, and the Hittites, and the Amorites, and the Hivites, and the Jebusites, which he sware unto thy fathers to give thee, a land flowing with milk and honey, that thou shalt keep this service in this month.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.13.6" type="verse">
						Seven days thou shalt eat unleavened bread, and in the seventh day shall be a feast to the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.13.7" type="verse">
						Unleavened bread shall be eaten seven days; and there shall no leavened bread be seen with thee, neither shall there be leaven seen with thee in all thy quarters.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.13.8" type="verse">
						And thou shalt shew thy son in that day, saying, This is done because of that which the LORD did unto me when I came forth out of Egypt.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.13.9" type="verse">
						And it shall be for a sign unto thee upon thine hand, and for a memorial between thine eyes, that the LORD's law may be in thy mouth: for with a strong hand hath the LORD brought thee out of Egypt.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.13.10" type="verse">
						Thou shalt therefore keep this ordinance in his season from year to year.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.13.11" type="verse">
						And it shall be when the LORD shall bring thee into the land of the Canaanites, as he sware unto thee and to thy fathers, and shall give it thee,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.13.12" type="verse">
						That thou shalt set apart unto the LORD all that openeth the matrix, and every firstling that cometh of a beast which thou hast; the males shall be the LORD's.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.13.13" type="verse">
						And every firstling of an ass thou shalt redeem with a lamb; and if thou wilt not redeem it, then thou shalt break his neck: and all the firstborn of man among thy children shalt thou redeem.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.13.14" type="verse">
						And it shall be when thy son asketh thee in time to come, saying, What is this? that thou shalt say unto him, By strength of hand the LORD brought us out from Egypt, from the house of bondage:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.13.15" type="verse">
						And it came to pass, when Pharaoh would hardly let us go, that the LORD slew all the firstborn in the land of Egypt, both the firstborn of man, and the firstborn of beast: therefore I sacrifice to the LORD all that openeth the matrix, being males; but all the firstborn of my children I redeem.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.13.16" type="verse">
						And it shall be for a token upon thine hand, and for frontlets between thine eyes: for by strength of hand the LORD brought us forth out of Egypt.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.13.17" type="verse">
						And it came to pass, when Pharaoh had let the people go, that God led them not through the way of the land of the Philistines, although that was near; for God said, Lest peradventure the people repent when they see war, and they return to Egypt:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.13.18" type="verse">
						But God led the people about, through the way of the wilderness of the Red sea: and the children of Israel went up harnessed out of the land of Egypt.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.13.19" type="verse">
						And Moses took the bones of Joseph with him: for he had straitly sworn the children of Israel, saying, God will surely visit you; and ye shall carry up my bones away hence with you.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.13.20" type="verse">
						And they took their journey from Succoth, and encamped in Etham, in the edge of the wilderness.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.13.21" type="verse">
						And the LORD went before them by day in a pillar of a cloud, to lead them the way; and by night in a pillar of fire, to give them light; to go by day and night:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.13.22" type="verse">
						He took not away the pillar of the cloud by day, nor the pillar of fire by night, from before the people.
					</seg>

				<div id="b.EXO.14" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.EXO.14.1" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.14.2" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.14.3" type="verse">
						For Pharaoh will say of the children of Israel, They are entangled in the land, the wilderness hath shut them in.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.14.4" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.14.5" type="verse">
						And it was told the king of Egypt that the people fled: and the heart of Pharaoh and of his servants was turned against the people, and they said, Why have we done this, that we have let Israel go from serving us?
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.14.6" type="verse">
						And he made ready his chariot, and took his people with him:
					</seg>

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.14.8" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.14.9" type="verse">
						But the Egyptians pursued after them, all the horses and chariots of Pharaoh, and his horsemen, and his army, and overtook them encamping by the sea, beside Pi-hahiroth, before Baal-zephon.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.14.10" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.14.11" type="verse">
						And they said unto Moses, Because there were no graves in Egypt, hast thou taken us away to die in the wilderness? wherefore hast thou dealt thus with us, to carry us forth out of Egypt?
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.14.12" type="verse">
						Is not this the word that we did tell thee in Egypt, saying, Let us alone, that we may serve the Egyptians? For it had been better for us to serve the Egyptians, than that we should die in the wilderness.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.14.13" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.14.14" type="verse">
						The LORD shall fight for you, and ye shall hold your peace.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.14.15" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.14.16" type="verse">
						But lift thou up thy rod, and stretch out thine hand over the sea, and divide it: and the children of Israel shall go on dry ground through the midst of the sea.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.14.17" type="verse">
						And I, behold, I will harden the hearts of the Egyptians, and they shall follow them: and I will get me honour upon Pharaoh, and upon all his host, upon his chariots, and upon his horsemen.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.14.18" type="verse">
						And the Egyptians shall know that I am the LORD, when I have gotten me honour upon Pharaoh, upon his chariots, and upon his horsemen.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.14.19" type="verse">
						And the angel of God, which went before the camp of Israel, removed and went behind them; and the pillar of the cloud went from before their face, and stood behind them:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.14.20" type="verse">
						And it came between the camp of the Egyptians and the camp of Israel; and it was a cloud and darkness to them, but it gave light by night to these: so that the one came not near the other all the night.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.14.21" type="verse">
						And Moses stretched out his hand over the sea; and the LORD caused the sea to go back by a strong east wind all that night, and made the sea dry land, and the waters were divided.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.14.22" type="verse">
						And the children of Israel went into the midst of the sea upon the dry ground: and the waters were a wall unto them on their right hand, and on their left.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.14.23" type="verse">
						And the Egyptians pursued, and went in after them to the midst of the sea, even all Pharaoh's horses, his chariots, and his horsemen.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.14.24" type="verse">
						And it came to pass, that in the morning watch the LORD looked unto the host of the Egyptians through the pillar of fire and of the cloud, and troubled the host of the Egyptians,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.14.25" type="verse">
						And took off their chariot wheels, that they drave them heavily: so that the Egyptians said, Let us flee from the face of Israel; for the LORD fighteth for them against the Egyptians.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.14.26" type="verse">
						And the LORD said unto Moses, Stretch out thine hand over the sea, that the waters may come again upon the Egyptians, upon their chariots, and upon their horsemen.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.14.27" type="verse">
						And Moses stretched forth his hand over the sea, and the sea returned to his strength when the morning appeared; and the Egyptians fled against it; and the LORD overthrew the Egyptians in the midst of the sea.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.14.28" type="verse">
						And the waters returned, and covered the chariots, and the horsemen, and all the host of Pharaoh that came into the sea after them; there remained not so much as one of them.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.14.29" type="verse">
						But the children of Israel walked upon dry land in the midst of the sea; and the waters were a wall unto them on their right hand, and on their left.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.14.30" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.14.31" type="verse">

				<div id="b.EXO.15" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.EXO.15.1" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.15.2" type="verse">
						The LORD is my strength and song, and he is become my salvation: he is my God, and I will prepare him an habitation; my father's God, and I will exalt him.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.15.3" type="verse">
						The LORD is a man of war: the LORD is his name.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.15.4" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.15.5" type="verse">
						The depths have covered them: they sank into the bottom as a stone.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.15.6" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.15.7" type="verse">
						And in the greatness of thine excellency thou hast overthrown them that rose up against thee: thou sentest forth thy wrath, which consumed them as stubble.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.15.8" type="verse">
						And with the blast of thy nostrils the waters were gathered together, the floods stood upright as an heap, and the depths were congealed in the heart of the sea.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.15.9" type="verse">
						The enemy said, I will pursue, I will overtake, I will divide the spoil; my lust shall be satisfied upon them; I will draw my sword, my hand shall destroy them.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.15.10" type="verse">
						Thou didst blow with thy wind, the sea covered them: they sank as lead in the mighty waters.
					</seg>

					</seg>

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.15.13" type="verse">

					</seg>

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.15.15" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.15.16" type="verse">
						Fear and dread shall fall upon them; by the greatness of thine arm they shall be as still as a stone; till thy people pass over, O LORD, till the people pass over, which thou hast purchased.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.15.17" type="verse">
						Thou shalt bring them in, and plant them in the mountain of thine inheritance, in the place, O LORD, which thou hast made for thee to dwell in, in the Sanctuary, O Lord, which thy hands have established.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.15.18" type="verse">
						The LORD shall reign for ever and ever.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.15.19" type="verse">
						For the horse of Pharaoh went in with his chariots and with his horsemen into the sea, and the LORD brought again the waters of the sea upon them; but the children of Israel went on dry land in the midst of the sea.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.15.20" type="verse">
						And Miriam the prophetess, the sister of Aaron, took a timbrel in her hand; and all the women went out after her with timbrels and with dances.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.15.21" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.15.22" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.15.23" type="verse">
						And when they came to Marah, they could not drink of the waters of Marah, for they were bitter: therefore the name of it was called Marah.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.15.24" type="verse">
						And the people murmured against Moses, saying, What shall we drink?
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.15.25" type="verse">
						And he cried unto the LORD; and the LORD shewed him a tree, which when he had cast into the waters, the waters were made sweet: there he made for them a statute and an ordinance, and there he proved them,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.15.26" type="verse">
						And said, If thou wilt diligently hearken to the voice of the LORD thy God, and wilt do that which is right in his sight, and wilt give ear to his commandments, and keep all his statutes, I will put none of these diseases upon thee, which I have brought upon the Egyptians: for I am the LORD that healeth thee.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.15.27" type="verse">
						And they came to Elim, where were twelve wells of water, and threescore and ten palm trees: and they encamped there by the waters.

				<div id="b.EXO.16" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.EXO.16.1" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.16.2" type="verse">
						And the whole congregation of the children of Israel murmured against Moses and Aaron in the wilderness:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.16.3" type="verse">
						And the children of Israel said unto them, Would to God we had died by the hand of the LORD in the land of Egypt, when we sat by the flesh pots, and when we did eat bread to the full; for ye have brought us forth into this wilderness, to kill this whole assembly with hunger.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.16.4" type="verse">
						Then said the LORD unto Moses, Behold, I will rain bread from heaven for you; and the people shall go out and gather a certain rate every day, that I may prove them, whether they will walk in my law, or no.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.16.5" type="verse">
						And it shall come to pass, that on the sixth day they shall prepare that which they bring in; and it shall be twice as much as they gather daily.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.16.6" type="verse">
						And Moses and Aaron said unto all the children of Israel, At even, then ye shall know that the LORD hath brought you out from the land of Egypt:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.16.7" type="verse">
						And in the morning, then ye shall see the glory of the LORD; for that he heareth your murmurings against the LORD: and what are we, that ye murmur against us?
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.16.8" type="verse">
						And Moses said, This shall be, when the LORD shall give you in the evening flesh to eat, and in the morning bread to the full; for that the LORD heareth your murmurings which ye murmur against him: and what are we? your murmurings are not against us, but against the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.16.9" type="verse">
						And Moses spake unto Aaron, Say unto all the congregation of the children of Israel, Come near before the LORD: for he hath heard your murmurings.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.16.10" type="verse">
						And it came to pass, as Aaron spake unto the whole congregation of the children of Israel, that they looked toward the wilderness, and, behold, the glory of the LORD appeared in the cloud.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.16.11" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.16.12" type="verse">
						I have heard the murmurings of the children of Israel: speak unto them, saying, At even ye shall eat flesh, and in the morning ye shall be filled with bread; and ye shall know that I am the LORD your God.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.16.13" type="verse">
						And it came to pass, that at even the quails came up, and covered the camp: and in the morning the dew lay round about the host.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.16.14" type="verse">
						And when the dew that lay was gone up, behold, upon the face of the wilderness there lay a small round thing, as small as the hoar frost on the ground.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.16.15" type="verse">
						And when the children of Israel saw it, they said one to another, It is manna: for they wist not what it was. And Moses said unto them, This is the bread which the LORD hath given you to eat.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.16.16" type="verse">
						This is the thing which the LORD hath commanded, Gather of it every man according to his eating, an omer for every man, according to the number of your persons; take ye every man for them which are in his tents.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.16.17" type="verse">
						And the children of Israel did so, and gathered, some more, some less.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.16.18" type="verse">
						And when they did mete it with an omer, he that gathered much had nothing over, and he that gathered little had no lack; they gathered every man according to his eating.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.16.19" type="verse">
						And Moses said, Let no man leave of it till the morning.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.16.20" type="verse">
						Notwithstanding they hearkened not unto Moses; but some of them left of it until the morning, and it bred worms, and stank: and Moses was wroth with them.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.16.21" type="verse">
						And they gathered it every morning, every man according to his eating: and when the sun waxed hot, it melted.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.16.22" type="verse">
						And it came to pass, that on the sixth day they gathered twice as much bread, two omers for one man: and all the rulers of the congregation came and told Moses.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.16.23" type="verse">
						And he said unto them, This is that which the LORD hath said, To morrow is the rest of the holy sabbath unto the LORD: bake that which ye will bake to day, and seethe that ye will seethe; and that which remaineth over lay up for you to be kept until the morning.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.16.24" type="verse">
						And they laid it up till the morning, as Moses bade: and it did not stink, neither was there any worm therein.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.16.25" type="verse">
						And Moses said, Eat that to day; for to day is a sabbath unto the LORD: to day ye shall not find it in the field.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.16.26" type="verse">
						Six days ye shall gather it; but on the seventh day, which is the sabbath, in it there shall be none.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.16.27" type="verse">
						And it came to pass, that there went out some of the people on the seventh day for to gather, and they found none.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.16.28" type="verse">
						And the LORD said unto Moses, How long refuse ye to keep my commandments and my laws?
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.16.29" type="verse">
						See, for that the LORD hath given you the sabbath, therefore he giveth you on the sixth day the bread of two days; abide ye every man in his place, let no man go out of his place on the seventh day.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.16.30" type="verse">
						So the people rested on the seventh day.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.16.31" type="verse">
						And the house of Israel called the name thereof Manna: and it was like coriander seed, white; and the taste of it was like wafers made with honey.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.16.32" type="verse">
						And Moses said, This is the thing which the LORD commandeth, Fill an omer of it to be kept for your generations; that they may see the bread wherewith I have fed you in the wilderness, when I brought you forth from the land of Egypt.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.16.33" type="verse">
						And Moses said unto Aaron, Take a pot, and put an omer full of manna therein, and lay it up before the LORD, to be kept for your generations.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.16.34" type="verse">
						As the LORD commanded Moses, so Aaron laid it up before the Testimony, to be kept.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.16.35" type="verse">
						And the children of Israel did eat manna forty years, until they came to a land inhabited; they did eat manna, until they came unto the borders of the land of Canaan.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.16.36" type="verse">
						Now an omer is the tenth part of an ephah.
					</seg>

				<div id="b.EXO.17" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.EXO.17.1" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.17.2" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.17.3" type="verse">
						And the people thirsted there for water; and the people murmured against Moses, and said, Wherefore is this that thou hast brought us up out of Egypt, to kill us and our children and our cattle with thirst?
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.17.4" type="verse">
						And Moses cried unto the LORD, saying, What shall I do unto this people? they be almost ready to stone me.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.17.5" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.17.6" type="verse">
						Behold, I will stand before thee there upon the rock in Horeb; and thou shalt smite the rock, and there shall come water out of it, that the people may drink. And Moses did so in the sight of the elders of Israel.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.17.7" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.17.8" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.17.9" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.17.10" type="verse">
						So Joshua did as Moses had said to him, and fought with Amalek: and Moses, Aaron, and Hur went up to the top of the hill.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.17.11" type="verse">
						And it came to pass, when Moses held up his hand, that Israel prevailed: and when he let down his hand, Amalek prevailed.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.17.12" type="verse">
