					<seg id="b.EXO.30.21" type="verse">
						So they shall wash their hands and their feet, that they die not: and it shall be a statute for ever to them, even to him and to his seed throughout their generations.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.30.22" type="verse">
						Moreover the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.30.23" type="verse">
						Take thou also unto thee principal spices, of pure myrrh five hundred shekels, and of sweet cinnamon half so much, even two hundred and fifty shekels, and of sweet calamus two hundred and fifty shekels,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.30.24" type="verse">
						And of cassia five hundred shekels, after the shekel of the sanctuary, and of oil olive an hin:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.30.25" type="verse">
						And thou shalt make it an oil of holy ointment, an ointment compound after the art of the apothecary: it shall be an holy anointing oil.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.30.26" type="verse">
						And thou shalt anoint the tabernacle of the congregation therewith, and the ark of the testimony,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.30.27" type="verse">
						And the table and all his vessels, and the candlestick and his vessels, and the altar of incense,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.30.28" type="verse">
						And the altar of burnt offering with all his vessels, and the laver and his foot.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.30.29" type="verse">
						And thou shalt sanctify them, that they may be most holy: whatsoever toucheth them shall be holy.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.30.30" type="verse">
						And thou shalt anoint Aaron and his sons, and consecrate them, that they may minister unto me in the priest's office.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.30.31" type="verse">
						And thou shalt speak unto the children of Israel, saying, This shall be an holy anointing oil unto me throughout your generations.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.30.32" type="verse">
						Upon man's flesh shall it not be poured, neither shall ye make any other like it, after the composition of it: it is holy, and it shall be holy unto you.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.30.33" type="verse">
						Whosoever compoundeth any like it, or whosoever putteth any of it upon a stranger, shall even be cut off from his people.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.30.34" type="verse">
						And the LORD said unto Moses, Take unto thee sweet spices, stacte, and onycha, and galbanum; these sweet spices with pure frankincense: of each shall there be a like weight:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.30.35" type="verse">
						And thou shalt make it a perfume, a confection after the art of the apothecary, tempered together, pure and holy:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.30.36" type="verse">
						And thou shalt beat some of it very small, and put of it before the testimony in the tabernacle of the congregation, where I will meet with thee: it shall be unto you most holy.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.30.37" type="verse">
						And as for the perfume which thou shalt make, ye shall not make to yourselves according to the composition thereof: it shall be unto thee holy for the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.30.38" type="verse">
						Whosoever shall make like unto that, to smell thereto, shall even be cut off from his people.
					</seg>
				</div>
				<div id="b.EXO.31" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.EXO.31.1" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.31.2" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.31.3" type="verse">
						And I have filled him with the spirit of God, in wisdom, and in understanding, and in knowledge, and in all manner of workmanship,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.31.4" type="verse">
						To devise cunning works, to work in gold, and in silver, and in brass,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.31.5" type="verse">
						And in cutting of stones, to set them, and in carving of timber, to work in all manner of workmanship.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.31.6" type="verse">
						And I, behold, I have given with him Aholiab, the son of Ahisamach, of the tribe of Dan: and in the hearts of all that are wise hearted I have put wisdom, that they may make all that I have commanded thee;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.31.7" type="verse">
						The tabernacle of the congregation, and the ark of the testimony, and the mercy seat that is thereupon, and all the furniture of the tabernacle,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.31.8" type="verse">
						And the table and his furniture, and the pure candlestick with all his furniture, and the altar of incense,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.31.9" type="verse">
						And the altar of burnt offering with all his furniture, and the laver and his foot,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.31.10" type="verse">
						And the cloths of service, and the holy garments for Aaron the priest, and the garments of his sons, to minister in the priest's office,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.31.11" type="verse">
						And the anointing oil, and sweet incense for the holy place: according to all that I have commanded thee shall they do.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.31.12" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.31.13" type="verse">
						Speak thou also unto the children of Israel, saying, Verily my sabbaths ye shall keep: for it is a sign between me and you throughout your generations; that ye may know that I am the LORD that doth sanctify you.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.31.14" type="verse">
						Ye shall keep the sabbath therefore; for it is holy unto you: every one that defileth it shall surely be put to death: for whosoever doeth any work therein, that soul shall be cut off from among his people.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.31.15" type="verse">
						Six days may work be done; but in the seventh is the sabbath of rest, holy to the LORD: whosoever doeth any work in the sabbath day, he shall surely be put to death.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.31.16" type="verse">
						Wherefore the children of Israel shall keep the sabbath, to observe the sabbath throughout their generations, for a perpetual covenant.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.31.17" type="verse">
						It is a sign between me and the children of Israel for ever: for in six days the LORD made heaven and earth, and on the seventh day he rested, and was refreshed.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.31.18" type="verse">
						And he gave unto Moses, when he had made an end of communing with him upon mount Sinai, two tables of testimony, tables of stone, written with the finger of God.
					</seg>
				</div>
				<div id="b.EXO.32" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.EXO.32.1" type="verse">
						And when the people saw that Moses delayed to come down out of the mount, the people gathered themselves together unto Aaron, and said unto him, Up, make us gods, which shall go before us; for as for this Moses, the man that brought us up out of the land of Egypt, we wot not what is become of him.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.32.2" type="verse">
						And Aaron said unto them, Break off the golden earrings, which are in the ears of your wives, of your sons, and of your daughters, and bring them unto me.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.32.3" type="verse">
						And all the people brake off the golden earrings which were in their ears, and brought them unto Aaron.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.32.4" type="verse">
						And he received them at their hand, and fashioned it with a graving tool, after he had made it a molten calf: and they said, These be thy gods, O Israel, which brought thee up out of the land of Egypt.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.32.5" type="verse">
						And when Aaron saw it, he built an altar before it; and Aaron made proclamation, and said, To morrow is a feast to the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.32.6" type="verse">
						And they rose up early on the morrow, and offered burnt offerings, and brought peace offerings; and the people sat down to eat and to drink, and rose up to play.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.32.7" type="verse">
						And the LORD said unto Moses, Go, get thee down; for thy people, which thou broughtest out of the land of Egypt, have corrupted themselves:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.32.8" type="verse">
						They have turned aside quickly out of the way which I commanded them: they have made them a molten calf, and have worshipped it, and have sacrificed thereunto, and said, These be thy gods, O Israel, which have brought thee up out of the land of Egypt.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.32.9" type="verse">
						And the LORD said unto Moses, I have seen this people, and, behold, it is a stiffnecked people:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.32.10" type="verse">
						Now therefore let me alone, that my wrath may wax hot against them, and that I may consume them: and I will make of thee a great nation.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.32.11" type="verse">
						And Moses besought the LORD his God, and said, LORD, why doth thy wrath wax hot against thy people, which thou hast brought forth out of the land of Egypt with great power, and with a mighty hand?
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.32.12" type="verse">
						Wherefore should the Egyptians speak, and say, For mischief did he bring them out, to slay them in the mountains, and to consume them from the face of the earth? Turn from thy fierce wrath, and repent of this evil against thy people.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.32.13" type="verse">
						Remember Abraham, Isaac, and Israel, thy servants, to whom thou swarest by thine own self, and saidst unto them, I will multiply your seed as the stars of heaven, and all this land that I have spoken of will I give unto your seed, and they shall inherit it for ever.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.32.14" type="verse">
						And the LORD repented of the evil which he thought to do unto his people.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.32.15" type="verse">
						And Moses turned, and went down from the mount, and the two tables of the testimony were in his hand: the tables were written on both their sides; on the one side and on the other were they written.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.32.16" type="verse">
						And the tables were the work of God, and the writing was the writing of God, graven upon the tables.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.32.17" type="verse">
						And when Joshua heard the noise of the people as they shouted, he said unto Moses, There is a noise of war in the camp.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.32.18" type="verse">
						And he said, It is not the voice of them that shout for mastery, neither is it the voice of them that cry for being overcome: but the noise of them that sing do I hear.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.32.19" type="verse">
						And it came to pass, as soon as he came nigh unto the camp, that he saw the calf, and the dancing: and Moses' anger waxed hot, and he cast the tables out of his hands, and brake them beneath the mount.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.32.20" type="verse">
						And he took the calf which they had made, and burnt it in the fire, and ground it to powder, and strawed it upon the water, and made the children of Israel drink of it.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.32.21" type="verse">
						And Moses said unto Aaron, What did this people unto thee, that thou hast brought so great a sin upon them?
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.32.22" type="verse">
						And Aaron said, Let not the anger of my lord wax hot: thou knowest the people, that they are set on mischief.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.32.23" type="verse">
						For they said unto me, Make us gods, which shall go before us: for as for this Moses, the man that brought us up out of the land of Egypt, we wot not what is become of him.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.32.24" type="verse">
						And I said unto them, Whosoever hath any gold, let them break it off. So they gave it me: then I cast it into the fire, and there came out this calf.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.32.25" type="verse">
						And when Moses saw that the people were naked; (for Aaron had made them naked unto their shame among their enemies:)
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.32.26" type="verse">
						Then Moses stood in the gate of the camp, and said, Who is on the LORD's side? let him come unto me. And all the sons of Levi gathered themselves together unto him.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.32.27" type="verse">
						And he said unto them, Thus saith the LORD God of Israel, Put every man his sword by his side, and go in and out from gate to gate throughout the camp, and slay every man his brother, and every man his companion, and every man his neighbour.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.32.28" type="verse">
						And the children of Levi did according to the word of Moses: and there fell of the people that day about three thousand men.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.32.29" type="verse">
						For Moses had said, Consecrate yourselves to day to the LORD, even every man upon his son, and upon his brother; that he may bestow upon you a blessing this day.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.32.30" type="verse">
						And it came to pass on the morrow, that Moses said unto the people, Ye have sinned a great sin: and now I will go up unto the LORD; peradventure I shall make an atonement for your sin.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.32.31" type="verse">
						And Moses returned unto the LORD, and said, Oh, this people have sinned a great sin, and have made them gods of gold.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.32.32" type="verse">
						Yet now, if thou wilt forgive their sin--; and if not, blot me, I pray thee, out of thy book which thou hast written.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.32.33" type="verse">
						And the LORD said unto Moses, Whosoever hath sinned against me, him will I blot out of my book.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.32.34" type="verse">
						Therefore now go, lead the people unto the place of which I have spoken unto thee: behold, mine Angel shall go before thee: nevertheless in the day when I visit I will visit their sin upon them.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.32.35" type="verse">
						And the LORD plagued the people, because they made the calf, which Aaron made.
					</seg>

				<div id="b.EXO.33" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.EXO.33.1" type="verse">
						And the LORD said unto Moses, Depart, and go up hence, thou and the people which thou hast brought up out of the land of Egypt, unto the land which I sware unto Abraham, to Isaac, and to Jacob, saying, Unto thy seed will I give it:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.33.2" type="verse">
						And I will send an angel before thee; and I will drive out the Canaanite, the Amorite, and the Hittite, and the Perizzite, the Hivite, and the Jebusite:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.33.3" type="verse">
						Unto a land flowing with milk and honey: for I will not go up in the midst of thee; for thou art a stiffnecked people: lest I consume thee in the way.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.33.4" type="verse">
						And when the people heard these evil tidings, they mourned: and no man did put on him his ornaments.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.33.5" type="verse">
						For the LORD had said unto Moses, Say unto the children of Israel, Ye are a stiffnecked people: I will come up into the midst of thee in a moment, and consume thee: therefore now put off thy ornaments from thee, that I may know what to do unto thee.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.33.6" type="verse">
						And the children of Israel stripped themselves of their ornaments by the mount Horeb.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.33.7" type="verse">
						And Moses took the tabernacle, and pitched it without the camp, afar off from the camp, and called it the Tabernacle of the congregation. And it came to pass, that every one which sought the LORD went out unto the tabernacle of the congregation, which was without the camp.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.33.8" type="verse">
						And it came to pass, when Moses went out unto the tabernacle, that all the people rose up, and stood every man at his tent door, and looked after Moses, until he was gone into the tabernacle.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.33.9" type="verse">
						And it came to pass, as Moses entered into the tabernacle, the cloudy pillar descended, and stood at the door of the tabernacle, and the LORD talked with Moses.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.33.10" type="verse">
						And all the people saw the cloudy pillar stand at the tabernacle door: and all the people rose up and worshipped, every man in his tent door.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.33.11" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses face to face, as a man speaketh unto his friend. And he turned again into the camp: but his servant Joshua, the son of Nun, a young man, departed not out of the tabernacle.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.33.12" type="verse">
						And Moses said unto the LORD, See, thou sayest unto me, Bring up this people: and thou hast not let me know whom thou wilt send with me. Yet thou hast said, I know thee by name, and thou hast also found grace in my sight.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.33.13" type="verse">
						Now therefore, I pray thee, if I have found grace in thy sight, shew me now thy way, that I may know thee, that I may find grace in thy sight: and consider that this nation is thy people.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.33.14" type="verse">
						And he said, My presence shall go with thee, and I will give thee rest.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.33.15" type="verse">
						And he said unto him, If thy presence go not with me, carry us not up hence.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.33.16" type="verse">
						For wherein shall it be known here that I and thy people have found grace in thy sight? is it not in that thou goest with us? so shall we be separated, I and thy people, from all the people that are upon the face of the earth.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.33.17" type="verse">
						And the LORD said unto Moses, I will do this thing also that thou hast spoken: for thou hast found grace in my sight, and I know thee by name.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.33.18" type="verse">
						And he said, I beseech thee, shew me thy glory.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.33.19" type="verse">
						And he said, I will make all my goodness pass before thee, and I will proclaim the name of the LORD before thee; and will be gracious to whom I will be gracious, and will shew mercy on whom I will shew mercy.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.33.20" type="verse">
						And he said, Thou canst not see my face: for there shall no man see me, and live.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.33.21" type="verse">
						And the LORD said, Behold, there is a place by me, and thou shalt stand upon a rock:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.33.22" type="verse">
						And it shall come to pass, while my glory passeth by, that I will put thee in a clift of the rock, and will cover thee with my hand while I pass by:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.33.23" type="verse">
						And I will take away mine hand, and thou shalt see my back parts: but my face shall not be seen.
					</seg>
				</div>
				<div id="b.EXO.34" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.EXO.34.1" type="verse">
						And the LORD said unto Moses, Hew thee two tables of stone like unto the first: and I will write upon these tables the words that were in the first tables, which thou brakest.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.34.2" type="verse">
						And be ready in the morning, and come up in the morning unto mount Sinai, and present thyself there to me in the top of the mount.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.34.3" type="verse">
						And no man shall come up with thee, neither let any man be seen throughout all the mount; neither let the flocks nor herds feed before that mount.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.34.4" type="verse">
						And he hewed two tables of stone like unto the first; and Moses rose up early in the morning, and went up unto mount Sinai, as the LORD had commanded him, and took in his hand the two tables of stone.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.34.5" type="verse">
						And the LORD descended in the cloud, and stood with him there, and proclaimed the name of the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.34.6" type="verse">
						And the LORD passed by before him, and proclaimed, The LORD, The LORD God, merciful and gracious, longsuffering, and abundant in goodness and truth,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.34.7" type="verse">
						Keeping mercy for thousands, forgiving iniquity and transgression and sin, and that will by no means clear the guilty; visiting the iniquity of the fathers upon the children, and upon the children's children, unto the third and to the fourth generation.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.34.8" type="verse">
						And Moses made haste, and bowed his head toward the earth, and worshipped.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.34.9" type="verse">
						And he said, If now I have found grace in thy sight, O Lord, let my Lord, I pray thee, go among us; for it is a stiffnecked people; and pardon our iniquity and our sin, and take us for thine inheritance.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.34.10" type="verse">
						And he said, Behold, I make a covenant: before all thy people I will do marvels, such as have not been done in all the earth, nor in any nation: and all the people among which thou art shall see the work of the LORD: for it is a terrible thing that I will do with thee.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.34.11" type="verse">
						Observe thou that which I command thee this day: behold, I drive out before thee the Amorite, and the Canaanite, and the Hittite, and the Perizzite, and the Hivite, and the Jebusite.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.34.12" type="verse">
						Take heed to thyself, lest thou make a covenant with the inhabitants of the land whither thou goest, lest it be for a snare in the midst of thee:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.34.13" type="verse">
						But ye shall destroy their altars, break their images, and cut down their groves:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.34.14" type="verse">
						For thou shalt worship no other god: for the LORD, whose name is Jealous, is a jealous God:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.34.15" type="verse">
						Lest thou make a covenant with the inhabitants of the land, and they go a whoring after their gods , and do sacrifice unto their gods, and one call thee, and thou eat of his sacrifice;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.34.16" type="verse">
						And thou take of their daughters unto thy sons, and their daughters go a whoring after their gods, and make thy sons go a whoring after their gods.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.34.17" type="verse">
						Thou shalt make thee no molten gods.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.34.18" type="verse">
						The feast of unleavened bread shalt thou keep. Seven days thou shalt eat unleavened bread, as I commanded thee, in the time of the month Abib: for in the month Abib thou camest out from Egypt.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.34.19" type="verse">
						All that openeth the matrix is mine; and every firstling among thy cattle, whether ox or sheep, that is male.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.34.20" type="verse">
						But the firstling of an ass thou shalt redeem with a lamb: and if thou redeem him not, then shalt thou break his neck. All the firstborn of thy sons thou shalt redeem. And none shall appear before me empty.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.34.21" type="verse">
						Six days thou shalt work, but on the seventh day thou shalt rest: in earing time and in harvest thou shalt rest.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.34.22" type="verse">
						And thou shalt observe the feast of weeks, of the firstfruits of wheat harvest, and the feast of ingathering at the year's end.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.34.23" type="verse">
						Thrice in the year shall all your men children appear before the Lord GOD, the God of Israel.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.34.24" type="verse">
						For I will cast out the nations before thee, and enlarge thy borders: neither shall any man desire thy land, when thou shalt go up to appear before the LORD thy God thrice in the year.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.34.25" type="verse">
						Thou shalt not offer the blood of my sacrifice with leaven; neither shall the sacrifice of the feast of the passover be left unto the morning.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.34.26" type="verse">
						The first of the firstfruits of thy land thou shalt bring unto the house of the LORD thy God. Thou shalt not seethe a kid in his mother's milk.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.34.27" type="verse">
						And the LORD said unto Moses, Write thou these words: for after the tenor of these words I have made a covenant with thee and with Israel.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.34.28" type="verse">
						And he was there with the LORD forty days and forty nights; he did neither eat bread, nor drink water. And he wrote upon the tables the words of the covenant, the ten commandments.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.34.29" type="verse">
						And it came to pass, when Moses came down from mount Sinai with the two tables of testimony in Moses' hand, when he came down from the mount, that Moses wist not that the skin of his face shone while he talked with him.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.34.30" type="verse">
						And when Aaron and all the children of Israel saw Moses, behold, the skin of his face shone; and they were afraid to come nigh him.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.34.31" type="verse">
						And Moses called unto them; and Aaron and all the rulers of the congregation returned unto him: and Moses talked with them.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.34.32" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.34.33" type="verse">
						And till Moses had done speaking with them, he put a vail on his face.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.34.34" type="verse">
						But when Moses went in before the LORD to speak with him, he took the vail off, until he came out. And he came out, and spake unto the children of Israel that which he was commanded.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.34.35" type="verse">

					</seg>

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.35.35" type="verse">

					</seg>

				<div id="b.EXO.36" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.EXO.36.1" type="verse">
						Then wrought Bezaleel and Aholiab, and every wise hearted man, in whom the LORD put wisdom and understanding to know how to work all manner of work for the service of the sanctuary, according to all that the LORD had commanded.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.36.2" type="verse">
						And Moses called Bezaleel and Aholiab, and every wise hearted man, in whose heart the LORD had put wisdom, even every one whose heart stirred him up to come unto the work to do it:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.36.3" type="verse">
						And they received of Moses all the offering, which the children of Israel had brought for the work of the service of the sanctuary, to make it withal. And they brought yet unto him free offerings every morning.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.36.4" type="verse">
						And all the wise men, that wrought all the work of the sanctuary, came every man from his work which they made;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.36.5" type="verse">
						And they spake unto Moses, saying, The people bring much more than enough for the service of the work, which the LORD commanded to make.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.36.6" type="verse">
						And Moses gave commandment, and they caused it to be proclaimed throughout the camp, saying, Let neither man nor woman make any more work for the offering of the sanctuary. So the people were restrained from bringing.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.36.7" type="verse">
						For the stuff they had was sufficient for all the work to make it, and too much.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.36.8" type="verse">
						And every wise hearted man among them that wrought the work of the tabernacle made ten curtains of fine twined linen, and blue, and purple, and scarlet: with cherubims of cunning work made he them.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.36.9" type="verse">
						The length of one curtain was twenty and eight cubits, and the breadth of one curtain four cubits: the curtains were all of one size.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.36.10" type="verse">
						And he coupled the five curtains one unto another: and the other five curtains he coupled one unto another.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.36.11" type="verse">
						And he made loops of blue on the edge of one curtain from the selvedge in the coupling: likewise he made in the uttermost side of another curtain, in the coupling of the second.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.36.12" type="verse">
						Fifty loops made he in one curtain, and fifty loops made he in the edge of the curtain which was in the coupling of the second: the loops held one curtain to another.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.36.13" type="verse">
						And he made fifty taches of gold, and coupled the curtains one unto another with the taches: so it became one tabernacle.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.36.14" type="verse">
						And he made curtains of goats' hair for the tent over the tabernacle: eleven curtains he made them.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.36.15" type="verse">
						The length of one curtain was thirty cubits, and four cubits was the breadth of one curtain: the eleven curtains were of one size.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.36.16" type="verse">
						And he coupled five curtains by themselves, and six curtains by themselves.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.36.17" type="verse">
						And he made fifty loops upon the uttermost edge of the curtain in the coupling, and fifty loops made he upon the edge of the curtain which coupleth the second.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.36.18" type="verse">
						And he made fifty taches of brass to couple the tent together, that it might be one.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.36.19" type="verse">
						And he made a covering for the tent of rams' skins dyed red, and a covering of badgers' skins above that.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.36.20" type="verse">

					</seg>

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.36.22" type="verse">

					</seg>

					</seg>

					</seg>

					</seg>

						And their forty sockets of silver; two sockets under one board, and two sockets under another board.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.36.27" type="verse">
						And for the sides of the tabernacle westward he made six boards.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.36.28" type="verse">
						And two boards made he for the corners of the tabernacle in the two sides.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.36.29" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.36.30" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.36.31" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.36.32" type="verse">

					</seg>

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.36.34" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.36.35" type="verse">
						And he made a vail of blue, and purple, and scarlet, and fine twined linen: with cherubims made he it of cunning work.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.36.36" type="verse">
						And he made thereunto four pillars of shittim wood, and overlaid them with gold: their hooks were of gold; and he cast for them four sockets of silver.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.36.37" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.36.38" type="verse">
						And the five pillars of it with their hooks: and he overlaid their chapiters and their fillets with gold: but their five sockets were of brass.

				<div id="b.EXO.37" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.EXO.37.1" type="verse">
						And Bezaleel made the ark of shittim wood: two cubits and a half was the length of it, and a cubit and a half the breadth of it, and a cubit and a half the height of it:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.37.2" type="verse">
						And he overlaid it with pure gold within and without, and made a crown of gold to it round about.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.37.3" type="verse">
						And he cast for it four rings of gold, to be set by the four corners of it; even two rings upon the one side of it, and two rings upon the other side of it.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.37.4" type="verse">
						And he made staves of shittim wood, and overlaid them with gold.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.37.5" type="verse">
						And he put the staves into the rings by the sides of the ark, to bear the ark.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.37.6" type="verse">
						And he made the mercy seat of pure gold: two cubits and a half was the length thereof, and one cubit and a half the breadth thereof.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.37.7" type="verse">
						And he made two cherubims of gold, beaten out of one piece made he them, on the two ends of the mercy seat;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.37.8" type="verse">
						One cherub on the end on this side, and another cherub on the other end on that side: out of the mercy seat made he the cherubims on the two ends thereof.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.37.9" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.37.10" type="verse">
						And he made the table of shittim wood: two cubits was the length thereof, and a cubit the breadth thereof, and a cubit and a half the height thereof:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.37.11" type="verse">
						And he overlaid it with pure gold, and made thereunto a crown of gold round about.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.37.12" type="verse">
						Also he made thereunto a border of an handbreadth round about; and made a crown of gold for the border thereof round about.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.37.13" type="verse">
						And he cast for it four rings of gold, and put the rings upon the four corners that were in the four feet thereof.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.37.14" type="verse">
						Over against the border were the rings, the places for the staves to bear the table.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.37.15" type="verse">
						And he made the staves of shittim wood, and overlaid them with gold, to bear the table.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.37.16" type="verse">
						And he made the vessels which were upon the table, his dishes, and his spoons, and his bowls, and his covers to cover withal, of pure gold.

					<seg id="b.EXO.37.17" type="verse">
						And he made the candlestick of pure gold: of beaten work made he the candlestick; his shaft, and his branch, his bowls, his knops, and his flowers, were of the same:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.37.18" type="verse">
						And six branches going out of the sides thereof; three branches of the candlestick out of the one side thereof, and three branches of the candlestick out of the other side thereof:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.37.19" type="verse">
						Three bowls made after the fashion of almonds in one branch, a knop and a flower; and three bowls made like almonds in another branch, a knop and a flower: so throughout the six branches going out of the candlestick.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.37.20" type="verse">
						And in the candlestick were four bowls made like almonds, his knops, and his flowers:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.37.21" type="verse">
						And a knop under two branches of the same, and a knop under two branches of the same, and a knop under two branches of the same, according to the six branches going out of it.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.37.22" type="verse">
						Their knops and their branches were of the same: all of it was one beaten work of pure gold.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.37.23" type="verse">
						And he made his seven lamps, and his snuffers, and his snuffdishes, of pure gold.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.37.24" type="verse">
						Of a talent of pure gold made he it, and all the vessels thereof.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.37.25" type="verse">
						And he made the incense altar of shittim wood: the length of it was a cubit, and the breadth of it a cubit; it was foursquare; and two cubits was the height of it; the horns thereof were of the same.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.37.26" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.37.27" type="verse">

					</seg>

					</seg>

				<div id="b.EXO.40" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.EXO.40.1" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.40.2" type="verse">
						On the first day of the first month shalt thou set up the tabernacle of the tent of the congregation.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.40.3" type="verse">
						And thou shalt put therein the ark of the testimony, and cover the ark with the vail.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.40.4" type="verse">
						And thou shalt bring in the table, and set in order the things that are to be set in order upon it; and thou shalt bring in the candlestick, and light the lamps thereof.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.40.5" type="verse">
						And thou shalt set the altar of gold for the incense before the ark of the testimony, and put the hanging of the door to the tabernacle.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.40.6" type="verse">
						And thou shalt set the altar of the burnt offering before the door of the tabernacle of the tent of the congregation.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.40.7" type="verse">
						And thou shalt set the laver between the tent of the congregation and the altar, and shalt put water therein.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.40.8" type="verse">
						And thou shalt set up the court round about, and hang up the hanging at the court gate.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.40.9" type="verse">
						And thou shalt take the anointing oil, and anoint the tabernacle, and all that is therein, and shalt hallow it, and all the vessels thereof: and it shall be holy.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.40.10" type="verse">
						And thou shalt anoint the altar of the burnt offering, and all his vessels, and sanctify the altar: and it shall be an altar most holy.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.40.11" type="verse">
						And thou shalt anoint the laver and his foot, and sanctify it.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.40.12" type="verse">
						And thou shalt bring Aaron and his sons unto the door of the tabernacle of the congregation, and wash them with water.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.40.13" type="verse">
						And thou shalt put upon Aaron the holy garments, and anoint him, and sanctify him; that he may minister unto me in the priest's office.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.40.14" type="verse">
						And thou shalt bring his sons, and clothe them with coats:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.40.15" type="verse">
						And thou shalt anoint them, as thou didst anoint their father, that they may minister unto me in the priest's office: for their anointing shall surely be an everlasting priesthood throughout their generations.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.40.16" type="verse">
						Thus did Moses: according to all that the LORD commanded him, so did he.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.40.17" type="verse">
						And it came to pass in the first month in the second year, on the first day of the month, that the tabernacle was reared up.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.40.18" type="verse">
						And Moses reared up the tabernacle, and fastened his sockets, and set up the boards thereof, and put in the bars thereof, and reared up his pillars.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.40.19" type="verse">
						And he spread abroad the tent over the tabernacle, and put the covering of the tent above upon it; as the LORD commanded Moses.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.40.20" type="verse">
						And he took and put the testimony into the ark, and set the staves on the ark, and put the mercy seat above upon the ark:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.40.21" type="verse">
						And he brought the ark into the tabernacle, and set up the vail of the covering, and covered the ark of the testimony; as the LORD commanded Moses.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.40.22" type="verse">
						And he put the table in the tent of the congregation, upon the side of the tabernacle northward, without the vail.
					</seg>

						And he set the bread in order upon it before the LORD; as the LORD had commanded Moses.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.40.24" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.40.25" type="verse">
						And he lighted the lamps before the LORD; as the LORD commanded Moses.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.40.26" type="verse">
						And he put the golden altar in the tent of the congregation before the vail:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.40.27" type="verse">
						And he burnt sweet incense thereon; as the LORD commanded Moses.
					</seg>

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.40.29" type="verse">

					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.40.30" type="verse">
						And he set the laver between the tent of the congregation and the altar, and put water there, to wash withal.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.40.31" type="verse">
						And Moses and Aaron and his sons washed their hands and their feet thereat:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.40.32" type="verse">
						When they went into the tent of the congregation, and when they came near unto the altar, they washed; as the LORD commanded Moses.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.40.33" type="verse">
						And he reared up the court round about the tabernacle and the altar, and set up the hanging of the court gate. So Moses finished the work.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.40.34" type="verse">
						Then a cloud covered the tent of the congregation, and the glory of the LORD filled the tabernacle.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.40.35" type="verse">
						And Moses was not able to enter into the tent of the congregation, because the cloud abode thereon, and the glory of the LORD filled the tabernacle.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.40.36" type="verse">
						And when the cloud was taken up from over the tabernacle, the children of Israel went onward in all their journeys:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.40.37" type="verse">
						But if the cloud were not taken up, then they journeyed not till the day that it was taken up.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.EXO.40.38" type="verse">
						For the cloud of the LORD was upon the tabernacle by day, and fire was on it by night, in the sight of all the house of Israel, throughout all their journeys.
					</seg>
				</div>
			</div>
			<div id="b.LEV" type="book">
				<div id="b.LEV.1" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.LEV.1.1" type="verse">
						And the LORD called unto Moses, and spake unto him out of the tabernacle of the congregation, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.1.2" type="verse">
						Speak unto the children of Israel, and say unto them, If any man of you bring an offering unto the LORD, ye shall bring your offering of the cattle, even of the herd, and of the flock.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.1.3" type="verse">
						If his offering be a burnt sacrifice of the herd, let him offer a male without blemish: he shall offer it of his own voluntary will at the door of the tabernacle of the congregation before the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.1.4" type="verse">
						And he shall put his hand upon the head of the burnt offering; and it shall be accepted for him to make atonement for him.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.1.5" type="verse">
						And he shall kill the bullock before the LORD: and the priests, Aaron's sons, shall bring the blood, and sprinkle the blood round about upon the altar that is by the door of the tabernacle of the congregation.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.1.6" type="verse">
						And he shall flay the burnt offering, and cut it into his pieces.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.1.7" type="verse">
						And the sons of Aaron the priest shall put fire upon the altar, and lay the wood in order upon the fire:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.1.8" type="verse">
						And the priests, Aaron's sons, shall lay the parts, the head, and the fat, in order upon the wood that is on the fire which is upon the altar:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.1.9" type="verse">
						But his inwards and his legs shall he wash in water: and the priest shall burn all on the altar, to be a burnt sacrifice, an offering made by fire, of a sweet savour unto the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.1.10" type="verse">
						And if his offering be of the flocks, namely, of the sheep, or of the goats, for a burnt sacrifice; he shall bring it a male without blemish.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.1.11" type="verse">
						And he shall kill it on the side of the altar northward before the LORD: and the priests, Aaron's sons, shall sprinkle his blood round about upon the altar.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.1.12" type="verse">
						And he shall cut it into his pieces, with his head and his fat: and the priest shall lay them in order on the wood that is on the fire which is upon the altar:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.1.13" type="verse">
						But he shall wash the inwards and the legs with water: and the priest shall bring it all, and burn it upon the altar: it is a burnt sacrifice, an offering made by fire, of a sweet savour unto the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.1.14" type="verse">
						And if the burnt sacrifice for his offering to the LORD be of fowls, then he shall bring his offering of turtledoves, or of young pigeons.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.1.15" type="verse">
						And the priest shall bring it unto the altar, and wring off his head, and burn it on the altar; and the blood thereof shall be wrung out at the side of the altar:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.1.16" type="verse">
						And he shall pluck away his crop with his feathers, and cast it beside the altar on the east part, by the place of the ashes:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.1.17" type="verse">
						And he shall cleave it with the wings thereof, but shall not divide it asunder: and the priest shall burn it upon the altar, upon the wood that is upon the fire: it is a burnt sacrifice, an offering made by fire, of a sweet savour unto the LORD.
					</seg>
				</div>
				<div id="b.LEV.2" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.LEV.2.1" type="verse">
						And when any will offer a meat offering unto the LORD, his offering shall be of fine flour; and he shall pour oil upon it, and put frankincense thereon:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.2.2" type="verse">
						And he shall bring it to Aaron's sons the priests: and he shall take thereout his handful of the flour thereof, and of the oil thereof, with all the frankincense thereof; and the priest shall burn the memorial of it upon the altar, to be an offering made by fire, of a sweet savour unto the LORD:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.2.3" type="verse">
						And the remnant of the meat offering shall be Aaron's and his sons': it is a thing most holy of the offerings of the LORD made by fire.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.2.4" type="verse">
						And if thou bring an oblation of a meat offering baken in the oven, it shall be unleavened cakes of fine flour mingled with oil, or unleavened wafers anointed with oil.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.2.5" type="verse">
						And if thy oblation be a meat offering baken in a pan, it shall be of fine flour unleavened, mingled with oil.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.2.6" type="verse">
						Thou shalt part it in pieces, and pour oil thereon: it is a meat offering.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.2.7" type="verse">
						And if thy oblation be a meat offering baken in the fryingpan, it shall be made of fine flour with oil.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.2.8" type="verse">
						And thou shalt bring the meat offering that is made of these things unto the LORD: and when it is presented unto the priest, he shall bring it unto the altar.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.2.9" type="verse">
						And the priest shall take from the meat offering a memorial thereof, and shall burn it upon the altar: it is an offering made by fire, of a sweet savour unto the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.2.10" type="verse">
						And that which is left of the meat offering shall be Aaron's and his sons': it is a thing most holy of the offerings of the LORD made by fire.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.2.11" type="verse">
						No meat offering, which ye shall bring unto the LORD, shall be made with leaven: for ye shall burn no leaven, nor any honey, in any offering of the LORD made by fire.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.2.12" type="verse">
						As for the oblation of the firstfruits, ye shall offer them unto the LORD: but they shall not be burnt on the altar for a sweet savour.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.2.13" type="verse">
						And every oblation of thy meat offering shalt thou season with salt; neither shalt thou suffer the salt of the covenant of thy God to be lacking from thy meat offering: with all thine offerings thou shalt offer salt.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.2.14" type="verse">
						And if thou offer a meat offering of thy firstfruits unto the LORD, thou shalt offer for the meat offering of thy firstfruits green ears of corn dried by the fire, even corn beaten out of full ears.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.2.15" type="verse">
						And thou shalt put oil upon it, and lay frankincense thereon: it is a meat offering.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.2.16" type="verse">
						And the priest shall burn the memorial of it, part of the beaten corn thereof, and part of the oil thereof, with all the frankincense thereof: it is an offering made by fire unto the LORD.
					</seg>
				</div>
				<div id="b.LEV.3" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.LEV.3.1" type="verse">
						And if his oblation be a sacrifice of peace offering, if he offer it of the herd; whether it be a male or female, he shall offer it without blemish before the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.3.2" type="verse">
						And he shall lay his hand upon the head of his offering, and kill it at the door of the tabernacle of the congregation: and Aaron's sons the priests shall sprinkle the blood upon the altar round about.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.3.3" type="verse">
						And he shall offer of the sacrifice of the peace offering an offering made by fire unto the LORD; the fat that covereth the inwards, and all the fat that is upon the inwards,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.3.4" type="verse">
						And the two kidneys, and the fat that is on them, which is by the flanks, and the caul above the liver, with the kidneys, it shall he take away.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.3.5" type="verse">
						And Aaron's sons shall burn it on the altar upon the burnt sacrifice, which is upon the wood that is on the fire: it is an offering made by fire, of a sweet savour unto the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.3.6" type="verse">
						And if his offering for a sacrifice of peace offering unto the LORD be of the flock; male or female, he shall offer it without blemish.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.3.7" type="verse">
						If he offer a lamb for his offering, then shall he offer it before the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.3.8" type="verse">
						And he shall lay his hand upon the head of his offering, and kill it before the tabernacle of the congregation: and Aaron's sons shall sprinkle the blood thereof round about upon the altar.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.3.9" type="verse">
						And he shall offer of the sacrifice of the peace offering an offering made by fire unto the LORD; the fat thereof, and the whole rump, it shall he take off hard by the backbone; and the fat that covereth the inwards, and all the fat that is upon the inwards,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.3.10" type="verse">
						And the two kidneys, and the fat that is upon them, which is by the flanks, and the caul above the liver, with the kidneys, it shall he take away.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.3.11" type="verse">
						And the priest shall burn it upon the altar: it is the food of the offering made by fire unto the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.3.12" type="verse">
						And if his offering be a goat, then he shall offer it before the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.3.13" type="verse">
						And he shall lay his hand upon the head of it, and kill it before the tabernacle of the congregation: and the sons of Aaron shall sprinkle the blood thereof upon the altar round about.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.3.14" type="verse">
						And he shall offer thereof his offering, even an offering made by fire unto the LORD; the fat that covereth the inwards, and all the fat that is upon the inwards,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.3.15" type="verse">
						And the two kidneys, and the fat that is upon them, which is by the flanks, and the caul above the liver, with the kidneys, it shall he take away.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.3.16" type="verse">
						And the priest shall burn them upon the altar: it is the food of the offering made by fire for a sweet savour: all the fat is the LORD's.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.3.17" type="verse">
						It shall be a perpetual statute for your generations throughout all your dwellings, that ye eat neither fat nor blood.
					</seg>
				</div>
				<div id="b.LEV.4" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.LEV.4.1" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.4.2" type="verse">
						Speak unto the children of Israel, saying, If a soul shall sin through ignorance against any of the commandments of the LORD concerning things which ought not to be done, and shall do against any of them:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.4.3" type="verse">
						If the priest that is anointed do sin according to the sin of the people; then let him bring for his sin, which he hath sinned, a young bullock without blemish unto the LORD for a sin offering.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.4.4" type="verse">
						And he shall bring the bullock unto the door of the tabernacle of the congregation before the LORD; and shall lay his hand upon the bullock's head, and kill the bullock before the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.4.5" type="verse">
						And the priest that is anointed shall take of the bullock's blood, and bring it to the tabernacle of the congregation:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.4.6" type="verse">
						And the priest shall dip his finger in the blood, and sprinkle of the blood seven times before the LORD, before the vail of the sanctuary.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.4.7" type="verse">
						And the priest shall put some of the blood upon the horns of the altar of sweet incense before the LORD, which is in the tabernacle of the congregation: and shall pour all the blood of the bullock at the bottom of the altar of the burnt offering, which is at the door of the tabernacle of the congregation.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.4.8" type="verse">
						And he shall take off from it all the fat of the bullock for the sin offering; the fat that covereth the inwards, and all the fat that is upon the inwards,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.4.9" type="verse">
						And the two kidneys, and the fat that is upon them, which is by the flanks, and the caul above the liver, with the kidneys, it shall he take away,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.4.10" type="verse">
						As it was taken off from the bullock of the sacrifice of peace offerings: and the priest shall burn them upon the altar of the burnt offering.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.4.11" type="verse">
						And the skin of the bullock, and all his flesh, with his head, and with his legs, and his inwards, and his dung,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.4.12" type="verse">
						Even the whole bullock shall he carry forth without the camp unto a clean place, where the ashes are poured out, and burn him on the wood with fire: where the ashes are poured out shall he be burnt.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.4.13" type="verse">
						And if the whole congregation of Israel sin through ignorance, and the thing be hid from the eyes of the assembly, and they have done somewhat against any of the commandments of the LORD concerning things which should not be done, and are guilty;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.4.14" type="verse">
						When the sin, which they have sinned against it, is known, then the congregation shall offer a young bullock for the sin, and bring him before the tabernacle of the congregation.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.4.15" type="verse">
						And the elders of the congregation shall lay their hands upon the head of the bullock before the LORD: and the bullock shall be killed before the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.4.16" type="verse">
						And the priest that is anointed shall bring of the bullock's blood to the tabernacle of the congregation:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.4.17" type="verse">
						And the priest shall dip his finger in some of the blood, and sprinkle it seven times before the LORD, even before the vail.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.4.18" type="verse">
						And he shall put some of the blood upon the horns of the altar which is before the LORD, that is in the tabernacle of the congregation, and shall pour out all the blood at the bottom of the altar of the burnt offering, which is at the door of the tabernacle of the congregation.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.4.19" type="verse">
						And he shall take all his fat from him, and burn it upon the altar.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.4.20" type="verse">
						And he shall do with the bullock as he did with the bullock for a sin offering, so shall he do with this: and the priest shall make an atonement for them, and it shall be forgiven them.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.4.21" type="verse">
						And he shall carry forth the bullock without the camp, and burn him as he burned the first bullock: it is a sin offering for the congregation.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.4.22" type="verse">
						When a ruler hath sinned, and done somewhat through ignorance against any of the commandments of the LORD his God concerning things which should not be done, and is guilty;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.4.23" type="verse">
						Or if his sin, wherein he hath sinned, come to his knowledge; he shall bring his offering, a kid of the goats, a male without blemish:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.4.24" type="verse">
						And he shall lay his hand upon the head of the goat, and kill it in the place where they kill the burnt offering before the LORD: it is a sin offering.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.4.25" type="verse">
						And the priest shall take of the blood of the sin offering with his finger, and put it upon the horns of the altar of burnt offering, and shall pour out his blood at the bottom of the altar of burnt offering.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.4.26" type="verse">
						And he shall burn all his fat upon the altar, as the fat of the sacrifice of peace offerings: and the priest shall make an atonement for him as concerning his sin, and it shall be forgiven him.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.4.27" type="verse">
						And if any one of the common people sin through ignorance, while he doeth somewhat against any of the commandments of the LORD concerning things which ought not to be done, and be guilty;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.4.28" type="verse">
						Or if his sin, which he hath sinned, come to his knowledge: then he shall bring his offering, a kid of the goats, a female without blemish, for his sin which he hath sinned.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.4.29" type="verse">
						And he shall lay his hand upon the head of the sin offering, and slay the sin offering in the place of the burnt offering.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.4.30" type="verse">
						And the priest shall take of the blood thereof with his finger, and put it upon the horns of the altar of burnt offering, and shall pour out all the blood thereof at the bottom of the altar.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.4.31" type="verse">
						And he shall take away all the fat thereof, as the fat is taken away from off the sacrifice of peace offerings; and the priest shall burn it upon the altar for a sweet savour unto the LORD; and the priest shall make an atonement for him, and it shall be forgiven him.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.4.32" type="verse">
						And if he bring a lamb for a sin offering, he shall bring it a female without blemish.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.4.33" type="verse">
						And he shall lay his hand upon the head of the sin offering, and slay it for a sin offering in the place where they kill the burnt offering
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.4.34" type="verse">
						And the priest shall take of the blood of the sin offering with his finger, and put it upon the horns of the altar of burnt offering, and shall pour out all the blood thereof at the bottom of the altar:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.4.35" type="verse">
						And he shall take away all the fat thereof, as the fat of the lamb is taken away from the sacrifice of the peace offerings; and the priest shall burn them upon the altar, according to the offerings made by fire unto the LORD: and the priest shall make an atonement for his sin that he hath committed, and it shall be forgiven him.
					</seg>
				</div>
				<div id="b.LEV.5" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.LEV.5.1" type="verse">
						And if a soul sin, and hear the voice of swearing, and is a witness, whether he hath seen or known of it; if he do not utter it, then he shall bear his iniquity.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.5.2" type="verse">
						Or if a soul touch any unclean thing, whether it be a carcase of an unclean beast, or a carcase of unclean cattle, or the carcase of unclean creeping things, and if it be hidden from him; he also shall be unclean, and guilty.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.5.3" type="verse">
						Or if he touch the uncleanness of man, whatsoever uncleanness it be that a man shall be defiled withal, and it be hid from him; when he knoweth of it, then he shall be guilty.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.5.4" type="verse">
						Or if a soul swear, pronouncing with his lips to do evil, or to do good, whatsoever it be that a man shall pronounce with an oath, and it be hid from him; when he knoweth of it, then he shall be guilty in one of these.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.5.5" type="verse">
						And it shall be, when he shall be guilty in one of these things, that he shall confess that he hath sinned in that thing:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.5.6" type="verse">
						And he shall bring his trespass offering unto the LORD for his sin which he hath sinned, a female from the flock, a lamb or a kid of the goats, for a sin offering; and the priest shall make an atonement for him concerning his sin.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.5.7" type="verse">
						And if he be not able to bring a lamb, then he shall bring for his trespass, which he hath committed, two turtledoves, or two young pigeons, unto the LORD; one for a sin offering, and the other for a burnt offering.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.5.8" type="verse">
						And he shall bring them unto the priest, who shall offer that which is for the sin offering first, and wring off his head from his neck, but shall not divide it asunder:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.5.9" type="verse">
						And he shall sprinkle of the blood of the sin offering upon the side of the altar; and the rest of the blood shall be wrung out at the bottom of the altar: it is a sin offering.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.5.10" type="verse">
						And he shall offer the second for a burnt offering, according to the manner: and the priest shall make an atonement for him for his sin which he hath sinned, and it shall be forgiven him.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.5.11" type="verse">
						But if he be not able to bring two turtledoves, or two young pigeons, then he that sinned shall bring for his offering the tenth part of an ephah of fine flour for a sin offering; he shall put no oil upon it, neither shall he put any frankincense thereon: for it is a sin offering.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.5.12" type="verse">
						Then shall he bring it to the priest, and the priest shall take his handful of it, even a memorial thereof, and burn it on the altar, according to the offerings made by fire unto the LORD: it is a sin offering.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.5.13" type="verse">
						And the priest shall make an atonement for him as touching his sin that he hath sinned in one of these, and it shall be forgiven him: and the remnant shall be the priest's, as a meat offering.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.5.14" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.5.15" type="verse">
						If a soul commit a trespass, and sin through ignorance, in the holy things of the LORD; then he shall bring for his trespass unto the LORD a ram without blemish out of the flocks, with thy estimation by shekels of silver, after the shekel of the sanctuary, for a trespass offering:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.5.16" type="verse">
						And he shall make amends for the harm that he hath done in the holy thing, and shall add the fifth part thereto, and give it unto the priest: and the priest shall make an atonement for him with the ram of the trespass offering, and it shall be forgiven him.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.5.17" type="verse">
						And if a soul sin, and commit any of these things which are forbidden to be done by the commandments of the LORD; though he wist it not, yet is he guilty, and shall bear his iniquity.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.5.18" type="verse">
						And he shall bring a ram without blemish out of the flock, with thy estimation, for a trespass offering, unto the priest: and the priest shall make an atonement for him concerning his ignorance wherein he erred and wist it not, and it shall be forgiven him.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.5.19" type="verse">
						It is a trespass offering: he hath certainly trespassed against the LORD.
					</seg>
				</div>
				<div id="b.LEV.6" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.LEV.6.1" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.6.2" type="verse">
						If a soul sin, and commit a trespass against the LORD, and lie unto his neighbour in that which was delivered him to keep, or in fellowship, or in a thing taken away by violence, or hath deceived his neighbour;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.6.3" type="verse">
						Or have found that which was lost, and lieth concerning it, and sweareth falsely; in any of all these that a man doeth, sinning therein:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.6.4" type="verse">
						Then it shall be, because he hath sinned, and is guilty, that he shall restore that which he took violently away, or the thing which he hath deceitfully gotten, or that which was delivered him to keep, or the lost thing which he found,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.6.5" type="verse">
						Or all that about which he hath sworn falsely; he shall even restore it in the principal, and shall add the fifth part more thereto, and give it unto him to whom it appertaineth, in the day of his trespass offering.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.6.6" type="verse">
						And he shall bring his trespass offering unto the LORD, a ram without blemish out of the flock, with thy estimation, for a trespass offering, unto the priest:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.6.7" type="verse">
						And the priest shall make an atonement for him before the LORD: and it shall be forgiven him for any thing of all that he hath done in trespassing therein.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.6.8" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.6.9" type="verse">
						Command Aaron and his sons, saying, This is the law of the burnt offering: It is the burnt offering, because of the burning upon the altar all night unto the morning, and the fire of the altar shall be burning in it.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.6.10" type="verse">
						And the priest shall put on his linen garment, and his linen breeches shall he put upon his flesh, and take up the ashes which the fire hath consumed with the burnt offering on the altar, and he shall put them beside the altar.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.6.11" type="verse">
						And he shall put off his garments, and put on other garments, and carry forth the ashes without the camp unto a clean place.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.6.12" type="verse">
						And the fire upon the altar shall be burning in it; it shall not be put out: and the priest shall burn wood on it every morning, and lay the burnt offering in order upon it; and he shall burn thereon the fat of the peace offerings.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.6.13" type="verse">
						The fire shall ever be burning upon the altar; it shall never go out.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.6.14" type="verse">
						And this is the law of the meat offering: the sons of Aaron shall offer it before the LORD, before the altar.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.6.15" type="verse">
						And he shall take of it his handful, of the flour of the meat offering, and of the oil thereof, and all the frankincense which is upon the meat offering, and shall burn it upon the altar for a sweet savour, even the memorial of it, unto the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.6.16" type="verse">
						And the remainder thereof shall Aaron and his sons eat: with unleavened bread shall it be eaten in the holy place; in the court of the tabernacle of the congregation they shall eat it.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.6.17" type="verse">
						It shall not be baken with leaven. I have given it unto them for their portion of my offerings made by fire; it is most holy, as is the sin offering, and as the trespass offering.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.6.18" type="verse">
						All the males among the children of Aaron shall eat of it. It shall be a statute for ever in your generations concerning the offerings of the LORD made by fire: every one that toucheth them shall be holy.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.6.19" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.6.20" type="verse">
						This is the offering of Aaron and of his sons, which they shall offer unto the LORD in the day when he is anointed; the tenth part of an ephah of fine flour for a meat offering perpetual, half of it in the morning, and half thereof at night.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.6.21" type="verse">
						In a pan it shall be made with oil; and when it is baken, thou shalt bring it in: and the baken pieces of the meat offering shalt thou offer for a sweet savour unto the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.6.22" type="verse">
						And the priest of his sons that is anointed in his stead shall offer it: it is a statute for ever unto the LORD, it shall be wholly burnt.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.6.23" type="verse">
						For every meat offering for the priest shall be wholly burnt: it shall not be eaten.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.6.24" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.6.25" type="verse">
						Speak unto Aaron and to his sons, saying, This is the law of the sin offering: In the place where the burnt offering is killed shall the sin offering be killed before the LORD: it is most holy.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.6.26" type="verse">
						The priest that offereth it for sin shall eat it: in the holy place shall it be eaten, in the court of the tabernacle of the congregation.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.6.27" type="verse">
						Whatsoever shall touch the flesh thereof shall be holy: and when there is sprinkled of the blood thereof upon any garment, thou shalt wash that whereon it was sprinkled in the holy place.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.6.28" type="verse">
						But the earthen vessel wherein it is sodden shall be broken: and if it be sodden in a brasen pot, it shall be both scoured, and rinsed in water.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.6.29" type="verse">
						All the males among the priests shall eat thereof: it is most holy.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.6.30" type="verse">
						And no sin offering, whereof any of the blood is brought into the tabernacle of the congregation to reconcile withal in the holy place, shall be eaten: it shall be burnt in the fire.
					</seg>
				</div>
				<div id="b.LEV.7" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.1" type="verse">
						Likewise this is the law of the trespass offering: it is most holy.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.2" type="verse">
						In the place where they kill the burnt offering shall they kill the trespass offering: and the blood thereof shall he sprinkle round about upon the altar.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.3" type="verse">
						And he shall offer of it all the fat thereof; the rump, and the fat that covereth the inwards,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.4" type="verse">
						And the two kidneys, and the fat that is on them, which is by the flanks, and the caul that is above the liver, with the kidneys, it shall he take away:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.5" type="verse">
						And the priest shall burn them upon the altar for an offering made by fire unto the LORD: it is a trespass offering.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.6" type="verse">
						Every male among the priests shall eat thereof: it shall be eaten in the holy place: it is most holy.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.7" type="verse">
						As the sin offering is, so is the trespass offering: there is one law for them: the priest that maketh atonement therewith shall have it.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.8" type="verse">
						And the priest that offereth any man's burnt offering, even the priest shall have to himself the skin of the burnt offering which he hath offered.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.9" type="verse">
						And all the meat offering that is baken in the oven, and all that is dressed in the fryingpan, and in the pan, shall be the priest's that offereth it.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.10" type="verse">
						And every meat offering, mingled with oil, and dry, shall all the sons of Aaron have, one as much as another.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.11" type="verse">
						And this is the law of the sacrifice of peace offerings, which he shall offer unto the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.12" type="verse">
						If he offer it for a thanksgiving, then he shall offer with the sacrifice of thanksgiving unleavened cakes mingled with oil, and unleavened wafers anointed with oil, and cakes mingled with oil, of fine flour, fried.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.13" type="verse">
						Besides the cakes, he shall offer for his offering leavened bread with the sacrifice of thanksgiving of his peace offerings.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.14" type="verse">
						And of it he shall offer one out of the whole oblation for an heave offering unto the LORD, and it shall be the priest's that sprinkleth the blood of the peace offerings.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.15" type="verse">
						And the flesh of the sacrifice of his peace offerings for thanksgiving shall be eaten the same day that it is offered; he shall not leave any of it until the morning.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.16" type="verse">
						But if the sacrifice of his offering be a vow, or a voluntary offering, it shall be eaten the same day that he offereth his sacrifice: and on the morrow also the remainder of it shall be eaten:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.17" type="verse">
						But the remainder of the flesh of the sacrifice on the third day shall be burnt with fire.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.18" type="verse">
						And if any of the flesh of the sacrifice of his peace offerings be eaten at all on the third day, it shall not be accepted, neither shall it be imputed unto him that offereth it: it shall be an abomination, and the soul that eateth of it shall bear his iniquity.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.19" type="verse">
						And the flesh that toucheth any unclean thing shall not be eaten; it shall be burnt with fire: and as for the flesh, all that be clean shall eat thereof.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.20" type="verse">
						But the soul that eateth of the flesh of the sacrifice of peace offerings, that pertain unto the LORD, having his uncleanness upon him, even that soul shall be cut off from his people.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.21" type="verse">
						Moreover the soul that shall touch any unclean thing, as the uncleanness of man, or any unclean beast, or any abominable unclean thing, and eat of the flesh of the sacrifice of peace offerings, which pertain unto the LORD, even that soul shall be cut off from his people.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.22" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.23" type="verse">
						Speak unto the children of Israel, saying, Ye shall eat no manner of fat, of ox, or of sheep, or of goat.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.24" type="verse">
						And the fat of the beast that dieth of itself, and the fat of that which is torn with beasts, may be used in any other use: but ye shall in no wise eat of it.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.25" type="verse">
						For whosoever eateth the fat of the beast, of which men offer an offering made by fire unto the LORD, even the soul that eateth it shall be cut off from his people.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.26" type="verse">
						Moreover ye shall eat no manner of blood, whether it be of fowl or of beast, in any of your dwellings.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.27" type="verse">
						Whatsoever soul it be that eateth any manner of blood, even that soul shall be cut off from his people.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.28" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.29" type="verse">
						Speak unto the children of Israel, saying, He that offereth the sacrifice of his peace offerings unto the LORD shall bring his oblation unto the LORD of the sacrifice of his peace offerings.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.30" type="verse">
						His own hands shall bring the offerings of the LORD made by fire, the fat with the breast, it shall he bring, that the breast may be waved for a wave offering before the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.31" type="verse">
						And the priest shall burn the fat upon the altar: but the breast shall be Aaron's and his sons'.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.32" type="verse">
						And the right shoulder shall ye give unto the priest for an heave offering of the sacrifices of your peace offerings.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.33" type="verse">
						He among the sons of Aaron, that offereth the blood of the peace offerings, and the fat, shall have the right shoulder for his part.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.34" type="verse">
						For the wave breast and the heave shoulder have I taken of the children of Israel from off the sacrifices of their peace offerings, and have given them unto Aaron the priest and unto his sons by a statute for ever from among the children of Israel.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.35" type="verse">
						This is the portion of the anointing of Aaron, and of the anointing of his sons, out of the offerings of the LORD made by fire, in the day when he presented them to minister unto the LORD in the priest's office;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.36" type="verse">
						Which the LORD commanded to be given them of the children of Israel, in the day that he anointed them, by a statute for ever throughout their generations.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.37" type="verse">
