						This is the law of the burnt offering, of the meat offering, and of the sin offering, and of the trespass offering, and of the consecrations, and of the sacrifice of the peace offerings;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.7.38" type="verse">
						Which the LORD commanded Moses in mount Sinai, in the day that he commanded the children of Israel to offer their oblations unto the LORD, in the wilderness of Sinai.
					</seg>
				</div>
				<div id="b.LEV.8" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.LEV.8.1" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.8.2" type="verse">
						Take Aaron and his sons with him, and the garments, and the anointing oil, and a bullock for the sin offering, and two rams, and a basket of unleavened bread;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.8.3" type="verse">
						And gather thou all the congregation together unto the door of the tabernacle of the congregation.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.8.4" type="verse">
						And Moses did as the LORD commanded him; and the assembly was gathered together unto the door of the tabernacle of the congregation.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.8.5" type="verse">
						And Moses said unto the congregation, This is the thing which the LORD commanded to be done.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.8.6" type="verse">
						And Moses brought Aaron and his sons, and washed them with water.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.8.7" type="verse">
						And he put upon him the coat, and girded him with the girdle, and clothed him with the robe, and put the ephod upon him, and he girded him with the curious girdle of the ephod, and bound it unto him therewith.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.8.8" type="verse">
						And he put the breastplate upon him: also he put in the breastplate the Urim and the Thummim.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.8.9" type="verse">
						And he put the mitre upon his head; also upon the mitre, even upon his forefront, did he put the golden plate, the holy crown; as the LORD commanded Moses.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.8.10" type="verse">
						And Moses took the anointing oil, and anointed the tabernacle and all that was therein, and sanctified them.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.8.11" type="verse">
						And he sprinkled thereof upon the altar seven times, and anointed the altar and all his vessels, both the laver and his foot, to sanctify them.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.8.12" type="verse">
						And he poured of the anointing oil upon Aaron's head, and anointed him, to sanctify him.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.8.13" type="verse">
						And Moses brought Aaron's sons, and put coats upon them, and girded them with girdles, and put bonnets upon them; as the LORD commanded Moses.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.8.14" type="verse">
						And he brought the bullock for the sin offering: and Aaron and his sons laid their hands upon the head of the bullock for the sin offering.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.8.15" type="verse">
						And he slew it; and Moses took the blood, and put it upon the horns of the altar round about with his finger, and purified the altar, and poured the blood at the bottom of the altar, and sanctified it, to make reconciliation upon it.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.8.16" type="verse">
						And he took all the fat that was upon the inwards, and caul above the liver, and the two kidneys, and their fat, and Moses burned it upon the altar.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.8.17" type="verse">
						But the bullock, and his hide, his flesh, and his dung, he burnt with fire without the camp; as the LORD commanded Moses.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.8.18" type="verse">
						And he brought the ram for the burnt offering: and Aaron and his sons laid their hands upon the head of the ram.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.8.19" type="verse">
						And he killed it; and Moses sprinkled the blood upon the altar round about.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.8.20" type="verse">
						And he cut the ram into pieces; and Moses burnt the head, and the pieces, and the fat.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.8.21" type="verse">
						And he washed the inwards and the legs in water; and Moses burnt the whole ram upon the altar: it was a burnt sacrifice for a sweet savour, and an offering made by fire unto the LORD; as the LORD commanded Moses.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.8.22" type="verse">
						And he brought the other ram, the ram of consecration: and Aaron and his sons laid their hands upon the head of the ram.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.8.23" type="verse">
						And he slew it; and Moses took of the blood of it, and put it upon the tip of Aaron's right ear, and upon the thumb of his right hand, and upon the great toe of his right foot.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.8.24" type="verse">
						And he brought Aaron's sons, and Moses put of the blood upon the tip of their right ear, and upon the thumbs of their right hands, and upon the great toes of their right feet: and Moses sprinkled the blood upon the altar round about.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.8.25" type="verse">
						And he took the fat, and the rump, and all the fat that was upon the inwards, and the caul above the liver, and the two kidneys, and their fat, and the right shoulder:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.8.26" type="verse">
						And out of the basket of unleavened bread, that was before the LORD, he took one unleavened cake, and a cake of oiled bread, and one wafer, and put them on the fat, and upon the right shoulder:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.8.27" type="verse">
						And he put all upon Aaron's hands, and upon his sons' hands, and waved them for a wave offering before the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.8.28" type="verse">
						And Moses took them from off their hands, and burnt them on the altar upon the burnt offering: they were consecrations for a sweet savour: it is an offering made by fire unto the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.8.29" type="verse">
						And Moses took the breast, and waved it for a wave offering before the LORD: for of the ram of consecration it was Moses' part; as the LORD commanded Moses.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.8.30" type="verse">
						And Moses took of the anointing oil, and of the blood which was upon the altar, and sprinkled it upon Aaron, and upon his garments, and upon his sons, and upon his sons' garments with him; and sanctified Aaron, and his garments, and his sons, and his sons' garments with him.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.8.31" type="verse">
						And Moses said unto Aaron and to his sons, Boil the flesh at the door of the tabernacle of the congregation: and there eat it with the bread that is in the basket of consecrations, as I commanded, saying, Aaron and his sons shall eat it.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.8.32" type="verse">
						And that which remaineth of the flesh and of the bread shall ye burn with fire.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.8.33" type="verse">
						And ye shall not go out of the door of the tabernacle of the congregation in seven days, until the days of your consecration be at an end: for seven days shall he consecrate you.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.8.34" type="verse">
						As he hath done this day, so the LORD hath commanded to do, to make an atonement for you.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.8.35" type="verse">
						Therefore shall ye abide at the door of the tabernacle of the congregation day and night seven days, and keep the charge of the LORD, that ye die not: for so I am commanded.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.8.36" type="verse">
						So Aaron and his sons did all things which the LORD commanded by the hand of Moses.
					</seg>
				</div>
				<div id="b.LEV.9" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.LEV.9.1" type="verse">
						And it came to pass on the eighth day, that Moses called Aaron and his sons, and the elders of Israel;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.9.2" type="verse">
						And he said unto Aaron, Take thee a young calf for a sin offering, and a ram for a burnt offering, without blemish, and offer them before the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.9.3" type="verse">
						And unto the children of Israel thou shalt speak, saying, Take ye a kid of the goats for a sin offering; and a calf and a lamb, both of the first year, without blemish, for a burnt offering;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.9.4" type="verse">
						Also a bullock and a ram for peace offerings, to sacrifice before the LORD; and a meat offering mingled with oil: for to day the LORD will appear unto you.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.9.5" type="verse">
						And they brought that which Moses commanded before the tabernacle of the congregation: and all the congregation drew near and stood before the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.9.6" type="verse">
						And Moses said, This is the thing which the LORD commanded that ye should do: and the glory of the LORD shall appear unto you.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.9.7" type="verse">
						And Moses said unto Aaron, Go unto the altar, and offer thy sin offering, and thy burnt offering, and make an atonement for thyself, and for the people: and offer the offering of the people, and make an atonement for them; as the LORD commanded.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.9.8" type="verse">
						Aaron therefore went unto the altar, and slew the calf of the sin offering, which was for himself.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.9.9" type="verse">
						And the sons of Aaron brought the blood unto him: and he dipped his finger in the blood, and put it upon the horns of the altar, and poured out the blood at the bottom of the altar:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.9.10" type="verse">
						But the fat, and the kidneys, and the caul above the liver of the sin offering, he burnt upon the altar; as the LORD commanded Moses.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.9.11" type="verse">
						And the flesh and the hide he burnt with fire without the camp.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.9.12" type="verse">
						And he slew the burnt offering; and Aaron's sons presented unto him the blood, which he sprinkled round about upon the altar.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.9.13" type="verse">
						And they presented the burnt offering unto him, with the pieces thereof, and the head: and he burnt them upon the altar.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.9.14" type="verse">
						And he did wash the inwards and the legs, and burnt them upon the burnt offering on the altar.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.9.15" type="verse">
						And he brought the people's offering, and took the goat, which was the sin offering for the people, and slew it, and offered it for sin, as the first.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.9.16" type="verse">
						And he brought the burnt offering, and offered it according to the manner.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.9.17" type="verse">
						And he brought the meat offering, and took an handful thereof, and burnt it upon the altar, beside the burnt sacrifice of the morning.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.9.18" type="verse">
						He slew also the bullock and the ram for a sacrifice of peace offerings, which was for the people: and Aaron's sons presented unto him the blood, which he sprinkled upon the altar round about,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.9.19" type="verse">
						And the fat of the bullock and of the ram, the rump, and that which covereth the inwards, and the kidneys, and the caul above the liver:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.9.20" type="verse">
						And they put the fat upon the breasts, and he burnt the fat upon the altar:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.9.21" type="verse">
						And the breasts and the right shoulder Aaron waved for a wave offering before the LORD; as Moses commanded.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.9.22" type="verse">
						And Aaron lifted up his hand toward the people, and blessed them, and came down from offering of the sin offering, and the burnt offering, and peace offerings.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.9.23" type="verse">
						And Moses and Aaron went into the tabernacle of the congregation, and came out, and blessed the people: and the glory of the LORD appeared unto all the people.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.9.24" type="verse">
						And there came a fire out from before the LORD, and consumed upon the altar the burnt offering and the fat: which when all the people saw, they shouted, and fell on their faces.
					</seg>
				</div>
				<div id="b.LEV.10" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.LEV.10.1" type="verse">
						And Nadab and Abihu, the sons of Aaron, took either of them his censer, and put fire therein, and put incense thereon, and offered strange fire before the LORD, which he commanded them not.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.10.2" type="verse">
						And there went out fire from the LORD, and devoured them, and they died before the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.10.3" type="verse">
						Then Moses said unto Aaron, This is it that the LORD spake, saying, I will be sanctified in them that come nigh me, and before all the people I will be glorified. And Aaron held his peace.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.10.4" type="verse">
						And Moses called Mishael and Elzaphan, the sons of Uzziel the uncle of Aaron, and said unto them, Come near, carry your brethren from before the sanctuary out of the camp.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.10.5" type="verse">
						So they went near, and carried them in their coats out of the camp; as Moses had said.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.10.6" type="verse">
						And Moses said unto Aaron, and unto Eleazar and unto Ithamar, his sons, Uncover not your heads, neither rend your clothes; lest ye die, and lest wrath come upon all the people: but let your brethren, the whole house of Israel, bewail the burning which the LORD hath kindled.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.10.7" type="verse">
						And ye shall not go out from the door of the tabernacle of the congregation, lest ye die: for the anointing oil of the LORD is upon you. And they did according to the word of Moses.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.10.8" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Aaron, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.10.9" type="verse">
						Do not drink wine nor strong drink, thou, nor thy sons with thee, when ye go into the tabernacle of the congregation, lest ye die: it shall be a statute for ever throughout your generations:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.10.10" type="verse">
						And that ye may put difference between holy and unholy, and between unclean and clean;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.10.11" type="verse">
						And that ye may teach the children of Israel all the statutes which the LORD hath spoken unto them by the hand of Moses.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.10.12" type="verse">
						And Moses spake unto Aaron, and unto Eleazar and unto Ithamar, his sons that were left, Take the meat offering that remaineth of the offerings of the LORD made by fire, and eat it without leaven beside the altar: for it is most holy:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.10.13" type="verse">
						And ye shall eat it in the holy place, because it is thy due, and thy sons' due, of the sacrifices of the LORD made by fire: for so I am commanded.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.10.14" type="verse">
						And the wave breast and heave shoulder shall ye eat in a clean place; thou, and thy sons, and thy daughters with thee: for they be thy due, and thy sons' due, which are given out of the sacrifices of peace offerings of the children of Israel.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.10.15" type="verse">
						The heave shoulder and the wave breast shall they bring with the offerings made by fire of the fat, to wave it for a wave offering before the LORD; and it shall be thine, and thy sons' with thee, by a statute for ever; as the LORD hath commanded.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.10.16" type="verse">
						And Moses diligently sought the goat of the sin offering, and, behold, it was burnt: and he was angry with Eleazar and Ithamar, the sons of Aaron which were left alive, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.10.17" type="verse">
						Wherefore have ye not eaten the sin offering in the holy place, seeing it is most holy, and God hath given it you to bear the iniquity of the congregation, to make atonement for them before the LORD?
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.10.18" type="verse">
						Behold, the blood of it was not brought in within the holy place: ye should indeed have eaten it in the holy place, as I commanded.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.10.19" type="verse">
						And Aaron said unto Moses, Behold, this day have they offered their sin offering and their burnt offering before the LORD; and such things have befallen me: and if I had eaten the sin offering to day, should it have been accepted in the sight of the LORD?
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.10.20" type="verse">
						And when Moses heard that, he was content.
					</seg>
				</div>
				<div id="b.LEV.11" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.1" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses and to Aaron, saying unto them,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.2" type="verse">
						Speak unto the children of Israel, saying, These are the beasts which ye shall eat among all the beasts that are on the earth.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.3" type="verse">
						Whatsoever parteth the hoof, and is clovenfooted, and cheweth the cud, among the beasts, that shall ye eat.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.4" type="verse">
						Nevertheless these shall ye not eat of them that chew the cud, or of them that divide the hoof: as the camel, because he cheweth the cud, but divideth not the hoof; he is unclean unto you.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.5" type="verse">
						And the coney, because he cheweth the cud, but divideth not the hoof; he is unclean unto you.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.6" type="verse">
						And the hare, because he cheweth the cud, but divideth not the hoof; he is unclean unto you.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.7" type="verse">
						And the swine, though he divide the hoof, and be clovenfooted, yet he cheweth not the cud; he is unclean to you.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.8" type="verse">
						Of their flesh shall ye not eat, and their carcase shall ye not touch; they are unclean to you.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.9" type="verse">
						These shall ye eat of all that are in the waters: whatsoever hath fins and scales in the waters, in the seas, and in the rivers, them shall ye eat.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.10" type="verse">
						And all that have not fins and scales in the seas, and in the rivers, of all that move in the waters, and of any living thing which is in the waters, they shall be an abomination unto you:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.11" type="verse">
						They shall be even an abomination unto you; ye shall not eat of their flesh, but ye shall have their carcases in abomination.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.12" type="verse">
						Whatsoever hath no fins nor scales in the waters, that shall be an abomination unto you.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.13" type="verse">
						And these are they which ye shall have in abomination among the fowls; they shall not be eaten, they are an abomination: the eagle, and the ossifrage, and the ospray,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.14" type="verse">
						And the vulture, and the kite after his kind;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.15" type="verse">
						Every raven after his kind;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.16" type="verse">
						And the owl, and the night hawk, and the cuckow, and the hawk after his kind,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.17" type="verse">
						And the little owl, and the cormorant, and the great owl,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.18" type="verse">
						And the swan, and the pelican, and the gier eagle,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.19" type="verse">
						And the stork, the heron after her kind, and the lapwing, and the bat.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.20" type="verse">
						All fowls that creep, going upon all four, shall be an abomination unto you.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.21" type="verse">
						Yet these may ye eat of every flying creeping thing that goeth upon all four, which have legs above their feet, to leap withal upon the earth;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.22" type="verse">
						Even these of them ye may eat; the locust after his kind, and the bald locust after his kind, and the beetle after his kind, and the grasshopper after his kind.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.23" type="verse">
						But all other flying creeping things, which have four feet, shall be an abomination unto you.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.24" type="verse">
						And for these ye shall be unclean: whosoever toucheth the carcase of them shall be unclean until the even.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.25" type="verse">
						And whosoever beareth ought of the carcase of them shall wash his clothes, and be unclean until the even.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.26" type="verse">
						The carcases of every beast which divideth the hoof, and is not clovenfooted, nor cheweth the cud, are unclean unto you: every one that toucheth them shall be unclean.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.27" type="verse">
						And whatsoever goeth upon his paws, among all manner of beasts that go on all four, those are unclean unto you: whoso toucheth their carcase shall be unclean until the even.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.28" type="verse">
						And he that beareth the carcase of them shall wash his clothes, and be unclean until the even: they are unclean unto you.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.29" type="verse">
						These also shall be unclean unto you among the creeping things that creep upon the earth; the weasel, and the mouse, and the tortoise after his kind,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.30" type="verse">
						And the ferret, and the chameleon, and the lizard, and the snail, and the mole.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.31" type="verse">
						These are unclean to you among all that creep: whosoever doth touch them, when they be dead, shall be unclean until the even.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.32" type="verse">
						And upon whatsoever any of them, when they are dead, doth fall, it shall be unclean; whether it be any vessel of wood, or raiment, or skin, or sack, whatsoever vessel it be, wherein any work is done, it must be put into water, and it shall be unclean until the even; so it shall be cleansed.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.33" type="verse">
						And every earthen vessel, whereinto any of them falleth, whatsoever is in it shall be unclean; and ye shall break it.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.34" type="verse">
						Of all meat which may be eaten, that on which such water cometh shall be unclean: and all drink that may be drunk in every such vessel shall be unclean.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.35" type="verse">
						And every thing whereupon any part of their carcase falleth shall be unclean; whether it be oven, or ranges for pots, they shall be broken down: for they are unclean, and shall be unclean unto you.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.36" type="verse">
						Nevertheless a fountain or pit, wherein there is plenty of water, shall be clean: but that which toucheth their carcase shall be unclean.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.37" type="verse">
						And if any part of their carcase fall upon any sowing seed which is to be sown, it shall be clean.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.38" type="verse">
						But if any water be put upon the seed, and any part of their carcase fall thereon, it shall be unclean unto you.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.39" type="verse">
						And if any beast, of which ye may eat, die; he that toucheth the carcase thereof shall be unclean until the even.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.40" type="verse">
						And he that eateth of the carcase of it shall wash his clothes, and be unclean until the even: he also that beareth the carcase of it shall wash his clothes, and be unclean until the even.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.41" type="verse">
						And every creeping thing that creepeth upon the earth shall be an abomination; it shall not be eaten.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.42" type="verse">
						Whatsoever goeth upon the belly, and whatsoever goeth upon all four, or whatsoever hath more feet among all creeping things that creep upon the earth, them ye shall not eat; for they are an abomination.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.43" type="verse">
						Ye shall not make yourselves abominable with any creeping thing that creepeth, neither shall ye make yourselves unclean with them, that ye should be defiled thereby.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.44" type="verse">
						For I am the LORD your God: ye shall therefore sanctify yourselves, and ye shall be holy; for I am holy: neither shall ye defile yourselves with any manner of creeping thing that creepeth upon the earth.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.45" type="verse">
						For I am the LORD that bringeth you up out of the land of Egypt, to be your God: ye shall therefore be holy, for I am holy.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.46" type="verse">
						This is the law of the beasts, and of the fowl, and of every living creature that moveth in the waters, and of every creature that creepeth upon the earth:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.11.47" type="verse">
						To make a difference between the unclean and the clean, and between the beast that may be eaten and the beast that may not be eaten.
					</seg>
				</div>
				<div id="b.LEV.12" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.LEV.12.1" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.12.2" type="verse">
						Speak unto the children of Israel, saying, If a woman have conceived seed, and born a man child: then she shall be unclean seven days; according to the days of the separation for her infirmity shall she be unclean.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.12.3" type="verse">
						And in the eighth day the flesh of his foreskin shall be circumcised.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.12.4" type="verse">
						And she shall then continue in the blood of her purifying three and thirty days; she shall touch no hallowed thing, nor come into the sanctuary, until the days of her purifying be fulfilled.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.12.5" type="verse">
						But if she bear a maid child, then she shall be unclean two weeks, as in her separation: and she shall continue in the blood of her purifying threescore and six days.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.12.6" type="verse">
						And when the days of her purifying are fulfilled, for a son, or for a daughter, she shall bring a lamb of the first year for a burnt offering, and a young pigeon, or a turtledove, for a sin offering, unto the door of the tabernacle of the congregation, unto the priest:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.12.7" type="verse">
						Who shall offer it before the LORD, and make an atonement for her; and she shall be cleansed from the issue of her blood. This is the law for her that hath born a male or a female.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.12.8" type="verse">
						And if she be not able to bring a lamb, then she shall bring two turtles, or two young pigeons; the one for the burnt offering, and the other for a sin offering: and the priest shall make an atonement for her, and she shall be clean.
					</seg>
				</div>
				<div id="b.LEV.13" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.1" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses and Aaron, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.2" type="verse">
						When a man shall have in the skin of his flesh a rising, a scab, or a bright spot, and it be in the skin of his flesh like the plague of leprosy; then he shall be brought unto Aaron the priest, or unto one of his sons the priests:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.3" type="verse">
						And the priest shall look on the plague in the skin of the flesh: and when the hair in the plague is turned white, and the plague in sight be deeper than the skin of his flesh, it is a plague of leprosy: and the priest shall look on him, and pronounce him unclean.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.4" type="verse">
						If the bright spot be white in the skin of his flesh, and in sight be not deeper than the skin, and the hair thereof be not turned white; then the priest shall shut up him that hath the plague seven days:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.5" type="verse">
						And the priest shall look on him the seventh day: and, behold, if the plague in his sight be at a stay, and the plague spread not in the skin; then the priest shall shut him up seven days more:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.6" type="verse">
						And the priest shall look on him again the seventh day: and, behold, if the plague be somewhat dark, and the plague spread not in the skin, the priest shall pronounce him clean: it is but a scab: and he shall wash his clothes, and be clean.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.7" type="verse">
						But if the scab spread much abroad in the skin, after that he hath been seen of the priest for his cleansing, he shall be seen of the priest again:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.8" type="verse">
						And if the priest see that, behold, the scab spreadeth in the skin, then the priest shall pronounce him unclean: it is a leprosy.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.9" type="verse">
						When the plague of leprosy is in a man, then he shall be brought unto the priest;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.10" type="verse">
						And the priest shall see him: and, behold, if the rising be white in the skin, and it have turned the hair white, and there be quick raw flesh in the rising;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.11" type="verse">
						It is an old leprosy in the skin of his flesh, and the priest shall pronounce him unclean, and shall not shut him up: for he is unclean.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.12" type="verse">
						And if a leprosy break out abroad in the skin, and the leprosy cover all the skin of him that hath the plague from his head even to his foot, wheresoever the priest looketh;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.13" type="verse">
						Then the priest shall consider: and, behold, if the leprosy have covered all his flesh, he shall pronounce him clean that hath the plague: it is all turned white: he is clean.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.14" type="verse">
						But when raw flesh appeareth in him, he shall be unclean.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.15" type="verse">
						And the priest shall see the raw flesh, and pronounce him to be unclean: for the raw flesh is unclean: it is a leprosy.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.16" type="verse">
						Or if the raw flesh turn again, and be changed unto white, he shall come unto the priest;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.17" type="verse">
						And the priest shall see him: and, behold, if the plague be turned into white; then the priest shall pronounce him clean that hath the plague: he is clean.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.18" type="verse">
						The flesh also, in which, even in the skin thereof, was a boil, and is healed,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.19" type="verse">
						And in the place of the boil there be a white rising, or a bright spot, white, and somewhat reddish, and it be shewed to the priest;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.20" type="verse">
						And if, when the priest seeth it, behold, it be in sight lower than the skin, and the hair thereof be turned white; the priest shall pronounce him unclean: it is a plague of leprosy broken out of the boil.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.21" type="verse">
						But if the priest look on it, and, behold, there be no white hairs therein, and if it be not lower than the skin, but be somewhat dark; then the priest shall shut him up seven days:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.22" type="verse">
						And if it spread much abroad in the skin, then the priest shall pronounce him unclean: it is a plague.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.23" type="verse">
						But if the bright spot stay in his place, and spread not, it is a burning boil; and the priest shall pronounce him clean.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.24" type="verse">
						Or if there be any flesh, in the skin whereof there is a hot burning, and the quick flesh that burneth have a white bright spot, somewhat reddish, or white;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.25" type="verse">
						Then the priest shall look upon it: and, behold, if the hair in the bright spot be turned white, and it be in sight deeper than the skin; it is a leprosy broken out of the burning: wherefore the priest shall pronounce him unclean: it is the plague of leprosy.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.26" type="verse">
						But if the priest look on it, and, behold, there be no white hair in the bright spot, and it be no lower than the other skin, but be somewhat dark; then the priest shall shut him up seven days:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.27" type="verse">
						And the priest shall look upon him the seventh day: and if it be spread much abroad in the skin, then the priest shall pronounce him unclean: it is the plague of leprosy.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.28" type="verse">
						And if the bright spot stay in his place, and spread not in the skin, but it be somewhat dark; it is a rising of the burning, and the priest shall pronounce him clean: for it is an inflammation of the burning.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.29" type="verse">
						If a man or woman have a plague upon the head or the beard;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.30" type="verse">
						Then the priest shall see the plague: and, behold, if it be in sight deeper than the skin; and there be in it a yellow thin hair; then the priest shall pronounce him unclean: it is a dry scall, even a leprosy upon the head or beard.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.31" type="verse">
						And if the priest look on the plague of the scall, and, behold, it be not in sight deeper than the skin, and that there is no black hair in it; then the priest shall shut up him that hath the plague of the scall seven days:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.32" type="verse">
						And in the seventh day the priest shall look on the plague: and, behold, if the scall spread not, and there be in it no yellow hair, and the scall be not in sight deeper than the skin;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.33" type="verse">
						He shall be shaven, but the scall shall he not shave; and the priest shall shut up him that hath the scall seven days more:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.34" type="verse">
						And in the seventh day the priest shall look on the scall: and, behold, if the scall be not spread in the skin, nor be in sight deeper than the skin; then the priest shall pronounce him clean: and he shall wash his clothes, and be clean.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.35" type="verse">
						But if the scall spread much in the skin after his cleansing;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.36" type="verse">
						Then the priest shall look on him: and, behold, if the scall be spread in the skin, the priest shall not seek for yellow hair; he is unclean.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.37" type="verse">
						But if the scall be in his sight at a stay, and that there is black hair grown up therein; the scall is healed, he is clean: and the priest shall pronounce him clean.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.38" type="verse">
						If a man also or a woman have in the skin of their flesh bright spots, even white bright spots;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.39" type="verse">
						Then the priest shall look: and, behold, if the bright spots in the skin of their flesh be darkish white; it is a freckled spot that groweth in the skin; he is clean.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.40" type="verse">
						And the man whose hair is fallen off his head, he is bald; yet is he clean.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.41" type="verse">
						And he that hath his hair fallen off from the part of his head toward his face, he is forehead bald: yet is he clean.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.42" type="verse">
						And if there be in the bald head, or bald forehead, a white reddish sore; it is a leprosy sprung up in his bald head, or his bald forehead.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.43" type="verse">
						Then the priest shall look upon it: and, behold, if the rising of the sore be white reddish in his bald head, or in his bald forehead, as the leprosy appeareth in the skin of the flesh;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.44" type="verse">
						He is a leprous man, he is unclean: the priest shall pronounce him utterly unclean; his plague is in his head.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.45" type="verse">
						And the leper in whom the plague is, his clothes shall be rent, and his head bare, and he shall put a covering upon his upper lip, and shall cry, Unclean, unclean.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.46" type="verse">
						All the days wherein the plague shall be in him he shall be defiled; he is unclean: he shall dwell alone; without the camp shall his habitation be.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.47" type="verse">
						The garment also that the plague of leprosy is in, whether it be a woollen garment, or a linen garment;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.48" type="verse">
						Whether it be in the warp, or woof; of linen, or of woollen; whether in a skin, or in any thing made of skin;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.49" type="verse">
						And if the plague be greenish or reddish in the garment, or in the skin, either in the warp, or in the woof, or in any thing of skin; it is a plague of leprosy, and shall be shewed unto the priest:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.50" type="verse">
						And the priest shall look upon the plague, and shut up it that hath the plague seven days:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.51" type="verse">
						And he shall look on the plague on the seventh day: if the plague be spread in the garment, either in the warp, or in the woof, or in a skin, or in any work that is made of skin; the plague is a fretting leprosy; it is unclean.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.52" type="verse">
						He shall therefore burn that garment, whether warp or woof, in woollen or in linen, or any thing of skin, wherein the plague is: for it is a fretting leprosy; it shall be burnt in the fire.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.53" type="verse">
						And if the priest shall look, and, behold, the plague be not spread in the garment, either in the warp, or in the woof, or in any thing of skin;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.54" type="verse">
						Then the priest shall command that they wash the thing wherein the plague is, and he shall shut it up seven days more:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.55" type="verse">
						And the priest shall look on the plague, after that it is washed: and, behold, if the plague have not changed his colour, and the plague be not spread; it is unclean; thou shalt burn it in the fire; it is fret inward, whether it be bare within or without.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.56" type="verse">
						And if the priest look, and, behold, the plague be somewhat dark after the washing of it; then he shall rend it out of the garment, or out of the skin, or out of the warp, or out of the woof:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.57" type="verse">
						And if it appear still in the garment, either in the warp, or in the woof, or in any thing of skin; it is a spreading plague: thou shalt burn that wherein the plague is with fire.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.58" type="verse">
						And the garment, either warp, or woof, or whatsoever thing of skin it be, which thou shalt wash, if the plague be departed from them, then it shall be washed the second time, and shall be clean.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.13.59" type="verse">
						This is the law of the plague of leprosy in a garment of woollen or linen, either in the warp, or woof, or any thing of skins, to pronounce it clean, or to pronounce it unclean.
					</seg>
				</div>
				<div id="b.LEV.14" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.1" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.2" type="verse">
						This shall be the law of the leper in the day of his cleansing: He shall be brought unto the priest:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.3" type="verse">
						And the priest shall go forth out of the camp; and the priest shall look, and, behold, if the plague of leprosy be healed in the leper;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.4" type="verse">
						Then shall the priest command to take for him that is to be cleansed two birds alive and clean, and cedar wood, and scarlet, and hyssop:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.5" type="verse">
						And the priest shall command that one of the birds be killed in an earthen vessel over running water:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.6" type="verse">
						As for the living bird, he shall take it, and the cedar wood, and the scarlet, and the hyssop, and shall dip them and the living bird in the blood of the bird that was killed over the running water:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.7" type="verse">
						And he shall sprinkle upon him that is to be cleansed from the leprosy seven times, and shall pronounce him clean, and shall let the living bird loose into the open field.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.8" type="verse">
						And he that is to be cleansed shall wash his clothes, and shave off all his hair, and wash himself in water, that he may be clean: and after that he shall come into the camp, and shall tarry abroad out of his tent seven days.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.9" type="verse">
						But it shall be on the seventh day, that he shall shave all his hair off his head and his beard and his eyebrows, even all his hair he shall shave off: and he shall wash his clothes, also he shall wash his flesh in water, and he shall be clean.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.10" type="verse">
						And on the eighth day he shall take two he lambs without blemish, and one ewe lamb of the first year without blemish, and three tenth deals of fine flour for a meat offering, mingled with oil, and one log of oil.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.11" type="verse">
						And the priest that maketh him clean shall present the man that is to be made clean, and those things, before the LORD, at the door of the tabernacle of the congregation:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.12" type="verse">
						And the priest shall take one he lamb, and offer him for a trespass offering, and the log of oil, and wave them for a wave offering before the LORD:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.13" type="verse">
						And he shall slay the lamb in the place where he shall kill the sin offering and the burnt offering, in the holy place: for as the sin offering is the priest's, so is the trespass offering: it is most holy:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.14" type="verse">
						And the priest shall take some of the blood of the trespass offering, and the priest shall put it upon the tip of the right ear of him that is to be cleansed, and upon the thumb of his right hand, and upon the great toe of his right foot:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.15" type="verse">
						And the priest shall take some of the log of oil, and pour it into the palm of his own left hand:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.16" type="verse">
						And the priest shall dip his right finger in the oil that is in his left hand, and shall sprinkle of the oil with his finger seven times before the LORD:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.17" type="verse">
						And of the rest of the oil that is in his hand shall the priest put upon the tip of the right ear of him that is to be cleansed, and upon the thumb of his right hand, and upon the great toe of his right foot, upon the blood of the trespass offering:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.18" type="verse">
						And the remnant of the oil that is in the priest's hand he shall pour upon the head of him that is to be cleansed: and the priest shall make an atonement for him before the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.19" type="verse">
						And the priest shall offer the sin offering, and make an atonement for him that is to be cleansed from his uncleanness; and afterward he shall kill the burnt offering:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.20" type="verse">
						And the priest shall offer the burnt offering and the meat offering upon the altar: and the priest shall make an atonement for him, and he shall be clean.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.21" type="verse">
						And if he be poor, and cannot get so much; then he shall take one lamb for a trespass offering to be waved, to make an atonement for him, and one tenth deal of fine flour mingled with oil for a meat offering, and a log of oil;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.22" type="verse">
						And two turtledoves, or two young pigeons, such as he is able to get; and the one shall be a sin offering, and the other a burnt offering.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.23" type="verse">
						And he shall bring them on the eighth day for his cleansing unto the priest, unto the door of the tabernacle of the congregation, before the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.24" type="verse">
						And the priest shall take the lamb of the trespass offering, and the log of oil, and the priest shall wave them for a wave offering before the LORD:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.25" type="verse">
						And he shall kill the lamb of the trespass offering, and the priest shall take some of the blood of the trespass offering, and put it upon the tip of the right ear of him that is to be cleansed, and upon the thumb of his right hand, and upon the great toe of his right foot:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.26" type="verse">
						And the priest shall pour of the oil into the palm of his own left hand:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.27" type="verse">
						And the priest shall sprinkle with his right finger some of the oil that is in his left hand seven times before the LORD:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.28" type="verse">
						And the priest shall put of the oil that is in his hand upon the tip of the right ear of him that is to be cleansed, and upon the thumb of his right hand, and upon the great toe of his right foot, upon the place of the blood of the trespass offering:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.29" type="verse">
						And the rest of the oil that is in the priest's hand he shall put upon the head of him that is to be cleansed, to make an atonement for him before the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.30" type="verse">
						And he shall offer the one of the turtledoves, or of the young pigeons, such as he can get;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.31" type="verse">
						Even such as he is able to get, the one for a sin offering, and the other for a burnt offering, with the meat offering: and the priest shall make an atonement for him that is to be cleansed before the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.32" type="verse">
						This is the law of him in whom is the plague of leprosy, whose hand is not able to get that which pertaineth to his cleansing.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.33" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses and unto Aaron, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.34" type="verse">
						When ye be come into the land of Canaan, which I give to you for a possession, and I put the plague of leprosy in a house of the land of your possession;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.35" type="verse">
						And he that owneth the house shall come and tell the priest, saying, It seemeth to me there is as it were a plague in the house:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.36" type="verse">
						Then the priest shall command that they empty the house, before the priest go into it to see the plague, that all that is in the house be not made unclean: and afterward the priest shall go in to see the house:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.37" type="verse">
						And he shall look on the plague, and, behold, if the plague be in the walls of the house with hollow strakes, greenish or reddish, which in sight are lower than the wall;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.38" type="verse">
						Then the priest shall go out of the house to the door of the house, and shut up the house seven days:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.39" type="verse">
						And the priest shall come again the seventh day, and shall look: and, behold, if the plague be spread in the walls of the house;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.40" type="verse">
						Then the priest shall command that they take away the stones in which the plague is, and they shall cast them into an unclean place without the city:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.41" type="verse">
						And he shall cause the house to be scraped within round about, and they shall pour out the dust that they scrape off without the city into an unclean place:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.42" type="verse">
						And they shall take other stones, and put them in the place of those stones; and he shall take other morter, and shall plaister the house.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.43" type="verse">
						And if the plague come again, and break out in the house, after that he hath taken away the stones, and after he hath scraped the house, and after it is plaistered;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.44" type="verse">
						Then the priest shall come and look, and, behold, if the plague be spread in the house, it is a fretting leprosy in the house: it is unclean.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.45" type="verse">
						And he shall break down the house, the stones of it, and the timber thereof, and all the morter of the house; and he shall carry them forth out of the city into an unclean place.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.46" type="verse">
						Moreover he that goeth into the house all the while that it is shut up shall be unclean until the even.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.47" type="verse">
						And he that lieth in the house shall wash his clothes; and he that eateth in the house shall wash his clothes.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.48" type="verse">
						And if the priest shall come in, and look upon it, and, behold, the plague hath not spread in the house, after the house was plaistered: then the priest shall pronounce the house clean, because the plague is healed.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.49" type="verse">
						And he shall take to cleanse the house two birds, and cedar wood, and scarlet, and hyssop:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.50" type="verse">
						And he shall kill the one of the birds in an earthen vessel over running water:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.51" type="verse">
						And he shall take the cedar wood, and the hyssop, and the scarlet, and the living bird, and dip them in the blood of the slain bird, and in the running water, and sprinkle the house seven times:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.52" type="verse">
						And he shall cleanse the house with the blood of the bird, and with the running water, and with the living bird, and with the cedar wood, and with the hyssop, and with the scarlet:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.53" type="verse">
						But he shall let go the living bird out of the city into the open fields, and make an atonement for the house: and it shall be clean.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.54" type="verse">
						This is the law for all manner of plague of leprosy, and scall,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.55" type="verse">
						And for the leprosy of a garment, and of a house,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.56" type="verse">
						And for a rising, and for a scab, and for a bright spot:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.14.57" type="verse">
						To teach when it is unclean, and when it is clean: this is the law of leprosy.
					</seg>
				</div>
				<div id="b.LEV.15" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.LEV.15.1" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses and to Aaron, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.15.2" type="verse">
						Speak unto the children of Israel, and say unto them, When any man hath a running issue out of his flesh, because of his issue he is unclean.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.15.3" type="verse">
						And this shall be his uncleanness in his issue: whether his flesh run with his issue, or his flesh be stopped from his issue, it is his uncleanness.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.15.4" type="verse">
						Every bed, whereon he lieth that hath the issue, is unclean: and every thing, whereon he sitteth, shall be unclean.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.15.5" type="verse">
						And whosoever toucheth his bed shall wash his clothes, and bathe himself in water, and be unclean until the even.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.15.6" type="verse">
						And he that sitteth on any thing whereon he sat that hath the issue shall wash his clothes, and bathe himself in water, and be unclean until the even.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.15.7" type="verse">
						And he that toucheth the flesh of him that hath the issue shall wash his clothes, and bathe himself in water, and be unclean until the even.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.15.8" type="verse">
						And if he that hath the issue spit upon him that is clean; then he shall wash his clothes, and bathe himself in water, and be unclean until the even.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.15.9" type="verse">
						And what saddle soever he rideth upon that hath the issue shall be unclean.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.15.10" type="verse">
						And whosoever toucheth any thing that was under him shall be unclean until the even: and he that beareth any of those things shall wash his clothes, and bathe himself in water, and be unclean until the even.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.15.11" type="verse">
						And whomsoever he toucheth that hath the issue, and hath not rinsed his hands in water, he shall wash his clothes, and bathe himself in water, and be unclean until the even.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.15.12" type="verse">
						And the vessel of earth, that he toucheth which hath the issue, shall be broken: and every vessel of wood shall be rinsed in water.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.15.13" type="verse">
						And when he that hath an issue is cleansed of his issue; then he shall number to himself seven days for his cleansing, and wash his clothes, and bathe his flesh in running water, and shall be clean.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.15.14" type="verse">
						And on the eighth day he shall take to him two turtledoves, or two young pigeons, and come before the LORD unto the door of the tabernacle of the congregation, and give them unto the priest:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.15.15" type="verse">
						And the priest shall offer them, the one for a sin offering, and the other for a burnt offering; and the priest shall make an atonement for him before the LORD for his issue.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.15.16" type="verse">
						And if any man's seed of copulation go out from him, then he shall wash all his flesh in water, and be unclean until the even.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.15.17" type="verse">
						And every garment, and every skin, whereon is the seed of copulation, shall be washed with water, and be unclean until the even.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.15.18" type="verse">
						The woman also with whom man shall lie with seed of copulation, they shall both bathe themselves in water, and be unclean until the even.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.15.19" type="verse">
						And if a woman have an issue, and her issue in her flesh be blood, she shall be put apart seven days: and whosoever toucheth her shall be unclean until the even.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.15.20" type="verse">
						And every thing that she lieth upon in her separation shall be unclean: every thing also that she sitteth upon shall be unclean.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.15.21" type="verse">
						And whosoever toucheth her bed shall wash his clothes, and bathe himself in water, and be unclean until the even.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.15.22" type="verse">
						And whosoever toucheth any thing that she sat upon shall wash his clothes, and bathe himself in water, and be unclean until the even.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.15.23" type="verse">
						And if it be on her bed, or on any thing whereon she sitteth, when he toucheth it, he shall be unclean until the even.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.15.24" type="verse">
						And if any man lie with her at all, and her flowers be upon him, he shall be unclean seven days; and all the bed whereon he lieth shall be unclean.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.15.25" type="verse">
						And if a woman have an issue of her blood many days out of the time of her separation, or if it run beyond the time of her separation; all the days of the issue of her uncleanness shall be as the days of her separation: she shall be unclean.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.15.26" type="verse">
						Every bed whereon she lieth all the days of her issue shall be unto her as the bed of her separation: and whatsoever she sitteth upon shall be unclean, as the uncleanness of her separation.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.15.27" type="verse">
						And whosoever toucheth those things shall be unclean, and shall wash his clothes, and bathe himself in water, and be unclean until the even.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.15.28" type="verse">
						But if she be cleansed of her issue, then she shall number to herself seven days, and after that she shall be clean.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.15.29" type="verse">
						And on the eighth day she shall take unto her two turtles, or two young pigeons, and bring them unto the priest, to the door of the tabernacle of the congregation.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.15.30" type="verse">
						And the priest shall offer the one for a sin offering, and the other for a burnt offering; and the priest shall make an atonement for her before the LORD for the issue of her uncleanness.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.15.31" type="verse">
						Thus shall ye separate the children of Israel from their uncleanness; that they die not in their uncleanness, when they defile my tabernacle that is among them.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.15.32" type="verse">
						This is the law of him that hath an issue, and of him whose seed goeth from him, and is defiled therewith;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.15.33" type="verse">
						And of her that is sick of her flowers, and of him that hath an issue, of the man, and of the woman, and of him that lieth with her that is unclean.
					</seg>
				</div>
				<div id="b.LEV.16" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.LEV.16.1" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses after the death of the two sons of Aaron, when they offered before the LORD, and died;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.16.2" type="verse">
						And the LORD said unto Moses, Speak unto Aaron thy brother, that he come not at all times into the holy place within the vail before the mercy seat, which is upon the ark; that he die not: for I will appear in the cloud upon the mercy seat.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.16.3" type="verse">
						Thus shall Aaron come into the holy place: with a young bullock for a sin offering, and a ram for a burnt offering.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.16.4" type="verse">
						He shall put on the holy linen coat, and he shall have the linen breeches upon his flesh, and shall be girded with a linen girdle, and with the linen mitre shall he be attired: these are holy garments; therefore shall he wash his flesh in water, and so put them on.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.16.5" type="verse">
						And he shall take of the congregation of the children of Israel two kids of the goats for a sin offering, and one ram for a burnt offering.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.16.6" type="verse">
						And Aaron shall offer his bullock of the sin offering, which is for himself, and make an atonement for himself, and for his house.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.16.7" type="verse">
						And he shall take the two goats, and present them before the LORD at the door of the tabernacle of the congregation.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.16.8" type="verse">
						And Aaron shall cast lots upon the two goats; one lot for the LORD, and the other lot for the scapegoat.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.16.9" type="verse">
						And Aaron shall bring the goat upon which the LORD's lot fell, and offer him for a sin offering.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.16.10" type="verse">
						But the goat, on which the lot fell to be the scapegoat, shall be presented alive before the LORD, to make an atonement with him, and to let him go for a scapegoat into the wilderness.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.16.11" type="verse">
						And Aaron shall bring the bullock of the sin offering, which is for himself, and shall make an atonement for himself, and for his house, and shall kill the bullock of the sin offering which is for himself:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.16.12" type="verse">
						And he shall take a censer full of burning coals of fire from off the altar before the LORD, and his hands full of sweet incense beaten small, and bring it within the vail:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.16.13" type="verse">
						And he shall put the incense upon the fire before the LORD, that the cloud of the incense may cover the mercy seat that is upon the testimony, that he die not:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.16.14" type="verse">
						And he shall take of the blood of the bullock, and sprinkle it with his finger upon the mercy seat eastward; and before the mercy seat shall he sprinkle of the blood with his finger seven times.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.16.15" type="verse">
						Then shall he kill the goat of the sin offering, that is for the people, and bring his blood within the vail, and do with that blood as he did with the blood of the bullock, and sprinkle it upon the mercy seat, and before the mercy seat:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.16.16" type="verse">
						And he shall make an atonement for the holy place, because of the uncleanness of the children of Israel, and because of their transgressions in all their sins: and so shall he do for the tabernacle of the congregation, that remaineth among them in the midst of their uncleanness.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.16.17" type="verse">
						And there shall be no man in the tabernacle of the congregation when he goeth in to make an atonement in the holy place, until he come out, and have made an atonement for himself, and for his household, and for all the congregation of Israel.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.16.18" type="verse">
						And he shall go out unto the altar that is before the LORD, and make an atonement for it; and shall take of the blood of the bullock, and of the blood of the goat, and put it upon the horns of the altar round about.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.16.19" type="verse">
						And he shall sprinkle of the blood upon it with his finger seven times, and cleanse it, and hallow it from the uncleanness of the children of Israel.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.16.20" type="verse">
						And when he hath made an end of reconciling the holy place, and the tabernacle of the congregation, and the altar, he shall bring the live goat:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.16.21" type="verse">
						And Aaron shall lay both his hands upon the head of the live goat, and confess over him all the iniquities of the children of Israel, and all their transgressions in all their sins, putting them upon the head of the goat, and shall send him away by the hand of a fit man into the wilderness:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.16.22" type="verse">
						And the goat shall bear upon him all their iniquities unto a land not inhabited: and he shall let go the goat in the wilderness.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.16.23" type="verse">
						And Aaron shall come into the tabernacle of the congregation, and shall put off the linen garments, which he put on when he went into the holy place, and shall leave them there:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.16.24" type="verse">
						And he shall wash his flesh with water in the holy place, and put on his garments, and come forth, and offer his burnt offering, and the burnt offering of the people, and make an atonement for himself, and for the people.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.16.25" type="verse">
						And the fat of the sin offering shall he burn upon the altar.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.16.26" type="verse">
						And he that let go the goat for the scapegoat shall wash his clothes, and bathe his flesh in water, and afterward come into the camp.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.16.27" type="verse">
						And the bullock for the sin offering, and the goat for the sin offering, whose blood was brought in to make atonement in the holy place, shall one carry forth without the camp; and they shall burn in the fire their skins, and their flesh, and their dung.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.16.28" type="verse">
						And he that burneth them shall wash his clothes, and bathe his flesh in water, and afterward he shall come into the camp.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.16.29" type="verse">
						And this shall be a statute for ever unto you: that in the seventh month, on the tenth day of the month, ye shall afflict your souls, and do no work at all, whether it be one of your own country, or a stranger that sojourneth among you:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.16.30" type="verse">
						For on that day shall the priest make an atonement for you, to cleanse you, that ye may be clean from all your sins before the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.16.31" type="verse">
						It shall be a sabbath of rest unto you, and ye shall afflict your souls, by a statute for ever.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.16.32" type="verse">
						And the priest, whom he shall anoint, and whom he shall consecrate to minister in the priest's office in his father's stead, shall make the atonement, and shall put on the linen clothes, even the holy garments:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.16.33" type="verse">
						And he shall make an atonement for the holy sanctuary, and he shall make an atonement for the tabernacle of the congregation, and for the altar, and he shall make an atonement for the priests, and for all the people of the congregation.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.16.34" type="verse">
						And this shall be an everlasting statute unto you, to make an atonement for the children of Israel for all their sins once a year. And he did as the LORD commanded Moses.
					</seg>
				</div>
				<div id="b.LEV.17" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.LEV.17.1" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.17.2" type="verse">
						Speak unto Aaron, and unto his sons, and unto all the children of Israel, and say unto them; This is the thing which the LORD hath commanded, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.17.3" type="verse">
						What man soever there be of the house of Israel, that killeth an ox, or lamb, or goat, in the camp, or that killeth it out of the camp,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.17.4" type="verse">
						And bringeth it not unto the door of the tabernacle of the congregation, to offer an offering unto the LORD before the tabernacle of the LORD; blood shall be imputed unto that man; he hath shed blood; and that man shall be cut off from among his people:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.17.5" type="verse">
						To the end that the children of Israel may bring their sacrifices, which they offer in the open field, even that they may bring them unto the LORD, unto the door of the tabernacle of the congregation, unto the priest, and offer them for peace offerings unto the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.17.6" type="verse">
						And the priest shall sprinkle the blood upon the altar of the LORD at the door of the tabernacle of the congregation, and burn the fat for a sweet savour unto the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.17.7" type="verse">
						And they shall no more offer their sacrifices unto devils, after whom they have gone a whoring. This shall be a statute for ever unto them throughout their generations.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.17.8" type="verse">
						And thou shalt say unto them, Whatsoever man there be of the house of Israel, or of the strangers which sojourn among you, that offereth a burnt offering of sacrifice,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.17.9" type="verse">
						And bringeth it not unto the door of the tabernacle of the congregation, to offer it unto the LORD; even that man shall be cut off from among his people.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.17.10" type="verse">
						And whatsoever man there be of the house of Israel, or of the strangers that sojourn among you, that eateth any manner of blood; I will even set my face against that soul that eateth blood, and will cut him off from among his people.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.17.11" type="verse">
						For the life of the flesh is in the blood: and I have given it to you upon the altar to make an atonement for your souls: for it is the blood that maketh an atonement for the soul.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.17.12" type="verse">
						Therefore I said unto the children of Israel, No soul of you shall eat blood, neither shall any stranger that sojourneth among you eat blood.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.17.13" type="verse">
						And whatsoever man there be of the children of Israel, or of the strangers that sojourn among you, which hunteth and catcheth any beast or fowl that may be eaten; he shall even pour out the blood thereof, and cover it with dust.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.17.14" type="verse">
						For it is the life of all flesh; the blood of it is for the life thereof: therefore I said unto the children of Israel, Ye shall eat the blood of no manner of flesh: for the life of all flesh is the blood thereof: whosoever eateth it shall be cut off.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.17.15" type="verse">
						And every soul that eateth that which died of itself, or that which was torn with beasts, whether it be one of your own country, or a stranger, he shall both wash his clothes, and bathe himself in water, and be unclean until the even: then shall he be clean.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.17.16" type="verse">
						But if he wash them not, nor bathe his flesh; then he shall bear his iniquity.
					</seg>
				</div>
				<div id="b.LEV.18" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.LEV.18.1" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.18.2" type="verse">
						Speak unto the children of Israel, and say unto them, I am the LORD your God.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.18.3" type="verse">
						After the doings of the land of Egypt, wherein ye dwelt, shall ye not do: and after the doings of the land of Canaan, whither I bring you, shall ye not do: neither shall ye walk in their ordinances.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.18.4" type="verse">
						Ye shall do my judgments, and keep mine ordinances, to walk therein: I am the LORD your God.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.18.5" type="verse">
						Ye shall therefore keep my statutes, and my judgments: which if a man do, he shall live in them: I am the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.18.6" type="verse">
						None of you shall approach to any that is near of kin to him, to uncover their nakedness: I am the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.18.7" type="verse">
						The nakedness of thy father, or the nakedness of thy mother, shalt thou not uncover: she is thy mother; thou shalt not uncover her nakedness.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.18.8" type="verse">
						The nakedness of thy father's wife shalt thou not uncover: it is thy father's nakedness.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.18.9" type="verse">
						The nakedness of thy sister, the daughter of thy father, or daughter of thy mother, whether she be born at home, or born abroad, even their nakedness thou shalt not uncover.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.18.10" type="verse">
						The nakedness of thy son's daughter, or of thy daughter's daughter, even their nakedness thou shalt not uncover: for theirs is thine own nakedness.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.18.11" type="verse">
						The nakedness of thy father's wife's daughter, begotten of thy father, she is thy sister, thou shalt not uncover her nakedness.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.18.12" type="verse">
						Thou shalt not uncover the nakedness of thy father's sister: she is thy father's near kinswoman.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.18.13" type="verse">
						Thou shalt not uncover the nakedness of thy mother's sister: for she is thy mother's near kinswoman.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.18.14" type="verse">
						Thou shalt not uncover the nakedness of thy father's brother, thou shalt not approach to his wife: she is thine aunt.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.18.15" type="verse">
						Thou shalt not uncover the nakedness of thy daughter in law: she is thy son's wife; thou shalt not uncover her nakedness.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.18.16" type="verse">
						Thou shalt not uncover the nakedness of thy brother's wife: it is thy brother's nakedness.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.18.17" type="verse">
						Thou shalt not uncover the nakedness of a woman and her daughter, neither shalt thou take her son's daughter, or her daughter's daughter, to uncover her nakedness; for they are her near kinswomen: it is wickedness.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.18.18" type="verse">
						Neither shalt thou take a wife to her sister, to vex her, to uncover her nakedness, beside the other in her life time.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.18.19" type="verse">
						Also thou shalt not approach unto a woman to uncover her nakedness, as long as she is put apart for her uncleanness.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.18.20" type="verse">
						Moreover thou shalt not lie carnally with thy neighbour's wife, to defile thyself with her.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.18.21" type="verse">
						And thou shalt not let any of thy seed pass through the fire to Molech, neither shalt thou profane the name of thy God: I am the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.18.22" type="verse">
						Thou shalt not lie with mankind, as with womankind: it is abomination.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.18.23" type="verse">
						Neither shalt thou lie with any beast to defile thyself therewith: neither shall any woman stand before a beast to lie down thereto: it is confusion.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.18.24" type="verse">
						Defile not ye yourselves in any of these things: for in all these the nations are defiled which I cast out before you:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.18.25" type="verse">
						And the land is defiled: therefore I do visit the iniquity thereof upon it, and the land itself vomiteth out her inhabitants.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.18.26" type="verse">
						Ye shall therefore keep my statutes and my judgments, and shall not commit any of these abominations; neither any of your own nation, nor any stranger that sojourneth among you:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.18.27" type="verse">
						(For all these abominations have the men of the land done, which were before you, and the land is defiled;)
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.18.28" type="verse">
						That the land spue not you out also, when ye defile it, as it spued out the nations that were before you.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.18.29" type="verse">
						For whosoever shall commit any of these abominations, even the souls that commit them shall be cut off from among their people.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.18.30" type="verse">
						Therefore shall ye keep mine ordinance, that ye commit not any one of these abominable customs, which were committed before you, and that ye defile not yourselves therein: I am the LORD your God.
					</seg>
				</div>
				<div id="b.LEV.19" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.1" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.2" type="verse">
						Speak unto all the congregation of the children of Israel, and say unto them, Ye shall be holy: for I the LORD your God am holy.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.3" type="verse">
						Ye shall fear every man his mother, and his father, and keep my sabbaths: I am the LORD your God.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.4" type="verse">
						Turn ye not unto idols, nor make to yourselves molten gods: I am the LORD your God.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.5" type="verse">
						And if ye offer a sacrifice of peace offerings unto the LORD, ye shall offer it at your own will.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.6" type="verse">
						It shall be eaten the same day ye offer it, and on the morrow: and if ought remain until the third day, it shall be burnt in the fire.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.7" type="verse">
						And if it be eaten at all on the third day, it is abominable; it shall not be accepted.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.8" type="verse">
						Therefore every one that eateth it shall bear his iniquity, because he hath profaned the hallowed thing of the LORD: and that soul shall be cut off from among his people.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.9" type="verse">
						And when ye reap the harvest of your land, thou shalt not wholly reap the corners of thy field, neither shalt thou gather the gleanings of thy harvest.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.10" type="verse">
						And thou shalt not glean thy vineyard, neither shalt thou gather every grape of thy vineyard; thou shalt leave them for the poor and stranger: I am the LORD your God.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.11" type="verse">
						Ye shall not steal, neither deal falsely, neither lie one to another.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.12" type="verse">
						And ye shall not swear by my name falsely, neither shalt thou profane the name of thy God: I am the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.13" type="verse">
						Thou shalt not defraud thy neighbour, neither rob him: the wages of him that is hired shall not abide with thee all night until the morning.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.14" type="verse">
						Thou shalt not curse the deaf, nor put a stumblingblock before the blind, but shalt fear thy God: I am the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.15" type="verse">
						Ye shall do no unrighteousness in judgment: thou shalt not respect the person of the poor, nor honour the person of the mighty: but in righteousness shalt thou judge thy neighbour.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.16" type="verse">
						Thou shalt not go up and down as a talebearer among thy people: neither shalt thou stand against the blood of thy neighbour: I am the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.17" type="verse">
						Thou shalt not hate thy brother in thine heart: thou shalt in any wise rebuke thy neighbour, and not suffer sin upon him.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.18" type="verse">
						Thou shalt not avenge, nor bear any grudge against the children of thy people, but thou shalt love thy neighbour as thyself: I am the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.19" type="verse">
