						Ye shall keep my statutes. Thou shalt not let thy cattle gender with a diverse kind: thou shalt not sow thy field with mingled seed: neither shall a garment mingled of linen and woollen come upon thee.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.20" type="verse">
						And whosoever lieth carnally with a woman, that is a bondmaid, betrothed to an husband, and not at all redeemed, nor freedom given her; she shall be scourged; they shall not be put to death, because she was not free.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.21" type="verse">
						And he shall bring his trespass offering unto the LORD, unto the door of the tabernacle of the congregation, even a ram for a trespass offering.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.22" type="verse">
						And the priest shall make an atonement for him with the ram of the trespass offering before the LORD for his sin which he hath done: and the sin which he hath done shall be forgiven him.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.23" type="verse">
						And when ye shall come into the land, and shall have planted all manner of trees for food, then ye shall count the fruit thereof as uncircumcised: three years shall it be as uncircumcised unto you: it shall not be eaten of.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.24" type="verse">
						But in the fourth year all the fruit thereof shall be holy to praise the LORD withal.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.25" type="verse">
						And in the fifth year shall ye eat of the fruit thereof, that it may yield unto you the increase thereof: I am the LORD your God.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.26" type="verse">
						Ye shall not eat any thing with the blood: neither shall ye use enchantment, nor observe times.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.27" type="verse">
						Ye shall not round the corners of your heads, neither shalt thou mar the corners of thy beard.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.28" type="verse">
						Ye shall not make any cuttings in your flesh for the dead, nor print any marks upon you: I am the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.29" type="verse">
						Do not prostitute thy daughter, to cause her to be a whore; lest the land fall to whoredom, and the land become full of wickedness.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.30" type="verse">
						Ye shall keep my sabbaths, and reverence my sanctuary: I am the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.31" type="verse">
						Regard not them that have familiar spirits, neither seek after wizards, to be defiled by them: I am the LORD your God.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.32" type="verse">
						Thou shalt rise up before the hoary head, and honour the face of the old man, and fear thy God: I am the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.33" type="verse">
						And if a stranger sojourn with thee in your land, ye shall not vex him.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.34" type="verse">
						But the stranger that dwelleth with you shall be unto you as one born among you, and thou shalt love him as thyself; for ye were strangers in the land of Egypt: I am the LORD your God.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.35" type="verse">
						Ye shall do no unrighteousness in judgment, in meteyard, in weight, or in measure.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.36" type="verse">
						Just balances, just weights, a just ephah, and a just hin, shall ye have: I am the LORD your God, which brought you out of the land of Egypt.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.19.37" type="verse">
						Therefore shall ye observe all my statutes, and all my judgments, and do them: I am the LORD.
					</seg>
				</div>
				<div id="b.LEV.20" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.LEV.20.1" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.20.2" type="verse">
						Again, thou shalt say to the children of Israel, Whosoever he be of the children of Israel, or of the strangers that sojourn in Israel, that giveth any of his seed unto Molech; he shall surely be put to death: the people of the land shall stone him with stones.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.20.3" type="verse">
						And I will set my face against that man, and will cut him off from among his people; because he hath given of his seed unto Molech, to defile my sanctuary, and to profane my holy name.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.20.4" type="verse">
						And if the people of the land do any ways hide their eyes from the man, when he giveth of his seed unto Molech, and kill him not:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.20.5" type="verse">
						Then I will set my face against that man, and against his family, and will cut him off, and all that go a whoring after him, to commit whoredom with Molech, from among their people.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.20.6" type="verse">
						And the soul that turneth after such as have familiar spirits, and after wizards, to go a whoring after them, I will even set my face against that soul, and will cut him off from among his people.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.20.7" type="verse">
						Sanctify yourselves therefore, and be ye holy: for I am the LORD your God.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.20.8" type="verse">
						And ye shall keep my statutes, and do them: I am the LORD which sanctify you.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.20.9" type="verse">
						For every one that curseth his father or his mother shall be surely put to death: he hath cursed his father or his mother; his blood shall be upon him.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.20.10" type="verse">
						And the man that committeth adultery with another man's wife, even he that committeth adultery with his neighbour's wife, the adulterer and the adulteress shall surely be put to death.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.20.11" type="verse">
						And the man that lieth with his father's wife hath uncovered his father's nakedness: both of them shall surely be put to death; their blood shall be upon them.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.20.12" type="verse">
						And if a man lie with his daughter in law, both of them shall surely be put to death: they have wrought confusion; their blood shall be upon them.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.20.13" type="verse">
						If a man also lie with mankind, as he lieth with a woman, both of them have committed an abomination: they shall surely be put to death; their blood shall be upon them.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.20.14" type="verse">
						And if a man take a wife and her mother, it is wickedness: they shall be burnt with fire, both he and they; that there be no wickedness among you.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.20.15" type="verse">
						And if a man lie with a beast, he shall surely be put to death: and ye shall slay the beast.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.20.16" type="verse">
						And if a woman approach unto any beast, and lie down thereto, thou shalt kill the woman, and the beast: they shall surely be put to death; their blood shall be upon them.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.20.17" type="verse">
						And if a man shall take his sister, his father's daughter, or his mother's daughter, and see her nakedness, and she see his nakedness; it is a wicked thing; and they shall be cut off in the sight of their people: he hath uncovered his sister's nakedness; he shall bear his iniquity.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.20.18" type="verse">
						And if a man shall lie with a woman having her sickness, and shall uncover her nakedness; he hath discovered her fountain, and she hath uncovered the fountain of her blood: and both of them shall be cut off from among their people.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.20.19" type="verse">
						And thou shalt not uncover the nakedness of thy mother's sister, nor of thy father's sister: for he uncovereth his near kin: they shall bear their iniquity.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.20.20" type="verse">
						And if a man shall lie with his uncle's wife, he hath uncovered his uncle's nakedness: they shall bear their sin; they shall die childless.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.20.21" type="verse">
						And if a man shall take his brother's wife, it is an unclean thing: he hath uncovered his brother's nakedness; they shall be childless.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.20.22" type="verse">
						Ye shall therefore keep all my statutes, and all my judgments, and do them: that the land, whither I bring you to dwell therein, spue you not out.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.20.23" type="verse">
						And ye shall not walk in the manners of the nation, which I cast out before you: for they committed all these things, and therefore I abhorred them.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.20.24" type="verse">
						But I have said unto you, Ye shall inherit their land, and I will give it unto you to possess it, a land that floweth with milk and honey: I am the LORD your God, which have separated you from other people.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.20.25" type="verse">
						Ye shall therefore put difference between clean beasts and unclean, and between unclean fowls and clean: and ye shall not make your souls abominable by beast, or by fowl, or by any manner of living thing that creepeth on the ground, which I have separated from you as unclean.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.20.26" type="verse">
						And ye shall be holy unto me: for I the LORD am holy, and have severed you from other people, that ye should be mine.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.20.27" type="verse">
						A man also or woman that hath a familiar spirit, or that is a wizard, shall surely be put to death: they shall stone them with stones: their blood shall be upon them.
					</seg>
				</div>
				<div id="b.LEV.21" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.LEV.21.1" type="verse">
						And the LORD said unto Moses, Speak unto the priests the sons of Aaron, and say unto them, There shall none be defiled for the dead among his people:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.21.2" type="verse">
						But for his kin, that is near unto him, that is, for his mother, and for his father, and for his son, and for his daughter, and for his brother,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.21.3" type="verse">
						And for his sister a virgin, that is nigh unto him, which hath had no husband; for her may he be defiled.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.21.4" type="verse">
						But he shall not defile himself, being a chief man among his people, to profane himself.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.21.5" type="verse">
						They shall not make baldness upon their head, neither shall they shave off the corner of their beard, nor make any cuttings in their flesh.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.21.6" type="verse">
						They shall be holy unto their God, and not profane the name of their God: for the offerings of the LORD made by fire, and the bread of their God, they do offer: therefore they shall be holy.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.21.7" type="verse">
						They shall not take a wife that is a whore, or profane; neither shall they take a woman put away from her husband: for he is holy unto his God.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.21.8" type="verse">
						Thou shalt sanctify him therefore; for he offereth the bread of thy God: he shall be holy unto thee: for I the LORD, which sanctify you, am holy.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.21.9" type="verse">
						And the daughter of any priest, if she profane herself by playing the whore, she profaneth her father: she shall be burnt with fire.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.21.10" type="verse">
						And he that is the high priest among his brethren, upon whose head the anointing oil was poured, and that is consecrated to put on the garments, shall not uncover his head, nor rend his clothes;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.21.11" type="verse">
						Neither shall he go in to any dead body, nor defile himself for his father, or for his mother;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.21.12" type="verse">
						Neither shall he go out of the sanctuary, nor profane the sanctuary of his God; for the crown of the anointing oil of his God is upon him: I am the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.21.13" type="verse">
						And he shall take a wife in her virginity.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.21.14" type="verse">
						A widow, or a divorced woman, or profane, or an harlot, these shall he not take: but he shall take a virgin of his own people to wife.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.21.15" type="verse">
						Neither shall he profane his seed among his people: for I the LORD do sanctify him.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.21.16" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.21.17" type="verse">
						Speak unto Aaron, saying, Whosoever he be of thy seed in their generations that hath any blemish, let him not approach to offer the bread of his God.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.21.18" type="verse">
						For whatsoever man he be that hath a blemish, he shall not approach: a blind man, or a lame, or he that hath a flat nose, or any thing superfluous,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.21.19" type="verse">
						Or a man that is brokenfooted, or brokenhanded,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.21.20" type="verse">
						Or crookbackt, or a dwarf, or that hath a blemish in his eye, or be scurvy, or scabbed, or hath his stones broken;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.21.21" type="verse">
						No man that hath a blemish of the seed of Aaron the priest shall come nigh to offer the offerings of the LORD made by fire: he hath a blemish; he shall not come nigh to offer the bread of his God.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.21.22" type="verse">
						He shall eat the bread of his God, both of the most holy, and of the holy.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.21.23" type="verse">
						Only he shall not go in unto the vail, nor come nigh unto the altar, because he hath a blemish; that he profane not my sanctuaries: for I the LORD do sanctify them.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.21.24" type="verse">
						And Moses told it unto Aaron, and to his sons, and unto all the children of Israel.
					</seg>
				</div>
				<div id="b.LEV.22" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.LEV.22.1" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.22.2" type="verse">
						Speak unto Aaron and to his sons, that they separate themselves from the holy things of the children of Israel, and that they profane not my holy name in those things which they hallow unto me: I am the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.22.3" type="verse">
						Say unto them, Whosoever he be of all your seed among your generations, that goeth unto the holy things, which the children of Israel hallow unto the LORD, having his uncleanness upon him, that soul shall be cut off from my presence: I am the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.22.4" type="verse">
						What man soever of the seed of Aaron is a leper, or hath a running issue; he shall not eat of the holy things, until he be clean. And whoso toucheth any thing that is unclean by the dead, or a man whose seed goeth from him;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.22.5" type="verse">
						Or whosoever toucheth any creeping thing, whereby he may be made unclean, or a man of whom he may take uncleanness, whatsoever uncleanness he hath;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.22.6" type="verse">
						The soul which hath touched any such shall be unclean until even, and shall not eat of the holy things, unless he wash his flesh with water.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.22.7" type="verse">
						And when the sun is down, he shall be clean, and shall afterward eat of the holy things; because it is his food.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.22.8" type="verse">
						That which dieth of itself, or is torn with beasts, he shall not eat to defile himself therewith: I am the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.22.9" type="verse">
						They shall therefore keep mine ordinance, lest they bear sin for it, and die therefore, if they profane it: I the LORD do sanctify them.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.22.10" type="verse">
						There shall no stranger eat of the holy thing: a sojourner of the priest, or an hired servant, shall not eat of the holy thing.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.22.11" type="verse">
						But if the priest buy any soul with his money, he shall eat of it, and he that is born in his house: they shall eat of his meat.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.22.12" type="verse">
						If the priest's daughter also be married unto a stranger, she may not eat of an offering of the holy things.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.22.13" type="verse">
						But if the priest's daughter be a widow, or divorced, and have no child, and is returned unto her father's house, as in her youth, she shall eat of her father's meat: but there shall no stranger eat thereof.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.22.14" type="verse">
						And if a man eat of the holy thing unwittingly, then he shall put the fifth part thereof unto it, and shall give it unto the priest with the holy thing.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.22.15" type="verse">
						And they shall not profane the holy things of the children of Israel, which they offer unto the LORD;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.22.16" type="verse">
						Or suffer them to bear the iniquity of trespass, when they eat their holy things: for I the LORD do sanctify them.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.22.17" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.22.18" type="verse">
						Speak unto Aaron, and to his sons, and unto all the children of Israel, and say unto them, Whatsoever he be of the house of Israel, or of the strangers in Israel, that will offer his oblation for all his vows, and for all his freewill offerings, which they will offer unto the LORD for a burnt offering;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.22.19" type="verse">
						Ye shall offer at your own will a male without blemish, of the beeves, of the sheep, or of the goats.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.22.20" type="verse">
						But whatsoever hath a blemish, that shall ye not offer: for it shall not be acceptable for you.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.22.21" type="verse">
						And whosoever offereth a sacrifice of peace offerings unto the LORD to accomplish his vow, or a freewill offering in beeves or sheep, it shall be perfect to be accepted; there shall be no blemish therein.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.22.22" type="verse">
						Blind, or broken, or maimed, or having a wen, or scurvy, or scabbed, ye shall not offer these unto the LORD, nor make an offering by fire of them upon the altar unto the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.22.23" type="verse">
						Either a bullock or a lamb that hath any thing superfluous or lacking in his parts, that mayest thou offer for a freewill offering; but for a vow it shall not be accepted.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.22.24" type="verse">
						Ye shall not offer unto the LORD that which is bruised, or crushed, or broken, or cut; neither shall ye make any offering thereof in your land.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.22.25" type="verse">
						Neither from a stranger's hand shall ye offer the bread of your God of any of these; because their corruption is in them, and blemishes be in them: they shall not be accepted for you.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.22.26" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.22.27" type="verse">
						When a bullock, or a sheep, or a goat, is brought forth, then it shall be seven days under the dam; and from the eighth day and thenceforth it shall be accepted for an offering made by fire unto the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.22.28" type="verse">
						And whether it be cow or ewe, ye shall not kill it and her young both in one day.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.22.29" type="verse">
						And when ye will offer a sacrifice of thanksgiving unto the LORD, offer it at your own will.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.22.30" type="verse">
						On the same day it shall be eaten up; ye shall leave none of it until the morrow: I am the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.22.31" type="verse">
						Therefore shall ye keep my commandments, and do them: I am the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.22.32" type="verse">
						Neither shall ye profane my holy name; but I will be hallowed among the children of Israel: I am the LORD which hallow you,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.22.33" type="verse">
						That brought you out of the land of Egypt, to be your God: I am the LORD.
					</seg>
				</div>
				<div id="b.LEV.23" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.1" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.2" type="verse">
						Speak unto the children of Israel, and say unto them, Concerning the feasts of the LORD, which ye shall proclaim to be holy convocations, even these are my feasts.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.3" type="verse">
						Six days shall work be done: but the seventh day is the sabbath of rest, an holy convocation; ye shall do no work therein: it is the sabbath of the LORD in all your dwellings.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.4" type="verse">
						These are the feasts of the LORD, even holy convocations, which ye shall proclaim in their seasons.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.5" type="verse">
						In the fourteenth day of the first month at even is the LORD's passover.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.6" type="verse">
						And on the fifteenth day of the same month is the feast of unleavened bread unto the LORD: seven days ye must eat unleavened bread.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.7" type="verse">
						In the first day ye shall have an holy convocation: ye shall do no servile work therein.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.8" type="verse">
						But ye shall offer an offering made by fire unto the LORD seven days: in the seventh day is an holy convocation: ye shall do no servile work therein.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.9" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.10" type="verse">
						Speak unto the children of Israel, and say unto them, When ye be come into the land which I give unto you, and shall reap the harvest thereof, then ye shall bring a sheaf of the firstfruits of your harvest unto the priest:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.11" type="verse">
						And he shall wave the sheaf before the LORD, to be accepted for you: on the morrow after the sabbath the priest shall wave it.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.12" type="verse">
						And ye shall offer that day when ye wave the sheaf an he lamb without blemish of the first year for a burnt offering unto the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.13" type="verse">
						And the meat offering thereof shall be two tenth deals of fine flour mingled with oil, an offering made by fire unto the LORD for a sweet savour: and the drink offering thereof shall be of wine, the fourth part of an hin.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.14" type="verse">
						And ye shall eat neither bread, nor parched corn, nor green ears, until the selfsame day that ye have brought an offering unto your God: it shall be a statute for ever throughout your generations in all your dwellings.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.15" type="verse">
						And ye shall count unto you from the morrow after the sabbath, from the day that ye brought the sheaf of the wave offering; seven sabbaths shall be complete:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.16" type="verse">
						Even unto the morrow after the seventh sabbath shall ye number fifty days; and ye shall offer a new meat offering unto the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.17" type="verse">
						Ye shall bring out of your habitations two wave loaves of two tenth deals: they shall be of fine flour; they shall be baken with leaven; they are the firstfruits unto the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.18" type="verse">
						And ye shall offer with the bread seven lambs without blemish of the first year, and one young bullock, and two rams: they shall be for a burnt offering unto the LORD, with their meat offering, and their drink offerings, even an offering made by fire, of sweet savour unto the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.19" type="verse">
						Then ye shall sacrifice one kid of the goats for a sin offering, and two lambs of the first year for a sacrifice of peace offerings.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.20" type="verse">
						And the priest shall wave them with the bread of the firstfruits for a wave offering before the LORD, with the two lambs: they shall be holy to the LORD for the priest.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.21" type="verse">
						And ye shall proclaim on the selfsame day, that it may be an holy convocation unto you: ye shall do no servile work therein: it shall be a statute for ever in all your dwellings throughout your generations.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.22" type="verse">
						And when ye reap the harvest of your land, thou shalt not make clean riddance of the corners of thy field when thou reapest, neither shalt thou gather any gleaning of thy harvest: thou shalt leave them unto the poor, and to the stranger: I am the LORD your God.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.23" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.24" type="verse">
						Speak unto the children of Israel, saying, In the seventh month, in the first day of the month, shall ye have a sabbath, a memorial of blowing of trumpets, an holy convocation.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.25" type="verse">
						Ye shall do no servile work therein: but ye shall offer an offering made by fire unto the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.26" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.27" type="verse">
						Also on the tenth day of this seventh month there shall be a day of atonement: it shall be an holy convocation unto you; and ye shall afflict your souls, and offer an offering made by fire unto the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.28" type="verse">
						And ye shall do no work in that same day: for it is a day of atonement, to make an atonement for you before the LORD your God.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.29" type="verse">
						For whatsoever soul it be that shall not be afflicted in that same day, he shall be cut off from among his people.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.30" type="verse">
						And whatsoever soul it be that doeth any work in that same day, the same soul will I destroy from among his people.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.31" type="verse">
						Ye shall do no manner of work: it shall be a statute for ever throughout your generations in all your dwellings.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.32" type="verse">
						It shall be unto you a sabbath of rest, and ye shall afflict your souls: in the ninth day of the month at even, from even unto even, shall ye celebrate your sabbath.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.33" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.34" type="verse">
						Speak unto the children of Israel, saying, The fifteenth day of this seventh month shall be the feast of tabernacles for seven days unto the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.35" type="verse">
						On the first day shall be an holy convocation: ye shall do no servile work therein.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.36" type="verse">
						Seven days ye shall offer an offering made by fire unto the LORD: on the eighth day shall be an holy convocation unto you; and ye shall offer an offering made by fire unto the LORD: it is a solemn assembly; and ye shall do no servile work therein.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.37" type="verse">
						These are the feasts of the LORD, which ye shall proclaim to be holy convocations, to offer an offering made by fire unto the LORD, a burnt offering, and a meat offering, a sacrifice, and drink offerings, every thing upon his day:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.38" type="verse">
						Beside the sabbaths of the LORD, and beside your gifts, and beside all your vows, and beside all your freewill offerings, which ye give unto the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.39" type="verse">
						Also in the fifteenth day of the seventh month, when ye have gathered in the fruit of the land, ye shall keep a feast unto the LORD seven days: on the first day shall be a sabbath, and on the eighth day shall be a sabbath.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.40" type="verse">
						And ye shall take you on the first day the boughs of goodly trees, branches of palm trees, and the boughs of thick trees, and willows of the brook; and ye shall rejoice before the LORD your God seven days.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.41" type="verse">
						And ye shall keep it a feast unto the LORD seven days in the year. It shall be a statute for ever in your generations: ye shall celebrate it in the seventh month.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.42" type="verse">
						Ye shall dwell in booths seven days; all that are Israelites born shall dwell in booths:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.43" type="verse">
						That your generations may know that I made the children of Israel to dwell in booths, when I brought them out of the land of Egypt: I am the LORD your God.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.23.44" type="verse">
						And Moses declared unto the children of Israel the feasts of the LORD.
					</seg>
				</div>
				<div id="b.LEV.24" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.LEV.24.1" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.24.2" type="verse">
						Command the children of Israel, that they bring unto thee pure oil olive beaten for the light, to cause the lamps to burn continually.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.24.3" type="verse">
						Without the vail of the testimony, in the tabernacle of the congregation, shall Aaron order it from the evening unto the morning before the LORD continually: it shall be a statute for ever in your generations.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.24.4" type="verse">
						He shall order the lamps upon the pure candlestick before the LORD continually.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.24.5" type="verse">
						And thou shalt take fine flour, and bake twelve cakes thereof: two tenth deals shall be in one cake.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.24.6" type="verse">
						And thou shalt set them in two rows, six on a row, upon the pure table before the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.24.7" type="verse">
						And thou shalt put pure frankincense upon each row, that it may be on the bread for a memorial, even an offering made by fire unto the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.24.8" type="verse">
						Every sabbath he shall set it in order before the LORD continually, being taken from the children of Israel by an everlasting covenant.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.24.9" type="verse">
						And it shall be Aaron's and his sons'; and they shall eat it in the holy place: for it is most holy unto him of the offerings of the LORD made by fire by a perpetual statute.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.24.10" type="verse">
						And the son of an Israelitish woman, whose father was an Egyptian, went out among the children of Israel: and this son of the Israelitish woman and a man of Israel strove together in the camp;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.24.11" type="verse">
						And the Israelitish woman's son blasphemed the name of the LORD, and cursed. And they brought him unto Moses: (and his mother's name was Shelomith, the daughter of Dibri, of the tribe of Dan:)
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.24.12" type="verse">
						And they put him in ward, that the mind of the LORD might be shewed them.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.24.13" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.24.14" type="verse">
						Bring forth him that hath cursed without the camp; and let all that heard him lay their hands upon his head, and let all the congregation stone him.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.24.15" type="verse">
						And thou shalt speak unto the children of Israel, saying, Whosoever curseth his God shall bear his sin.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.24.16" type="verse">
						And he that blasphemeth the name of the LORD, he shall surely be put to death, and all the congregation shall certainly stone him: as well the stranger, as he that is born in the land, when he blasphemeth the name of the LORD, shall be put to death.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.24.17" type="verse">
						And he that killeth any man shall surely be put to death.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.24.18" type="verse">
						And he that killeth a beast shall make it good; beast for beast.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.24.19" type="verse">
						And if a man cause a blemish in his neighbour; as he hath done, so shall it be done to him;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.24.20" type="verse">
						Breach for breach, eye for eye, tooth for tooth: as he hath caused a blemish in a man, so shall it be done to him again.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.24.21" type="verse">
						And he that killeth a beast, he shall restore it: and he that killeth a man, he shall be put to death.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.24.22" type="verse">
						Ye shall have one manner of law, as well for the stranger, as for one of your own country: for I am the LORD your God.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.24.23" type="verse">
						And Moses spake to the children of Israel, that they should bring forth him that had cursed out of the camp, and stone him with stones. And the children of Israel did as the LORD commanded Moses.
					</seg>
				</div>
				<div id="b.LEV.25" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.1" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses in mount Sinai, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.2" type="verse">
						Speak unto the children of Israel, and say unto them, When ye come into the land which I give you, then shall the land keep a sabbath unto the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.3" type="verse">
						Six years thou shalt sow thy field, and six years thou shalt prune thy vineyard, and gather in the fruit thereof;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.4" type="verse">
						But in the seventh year shall be a sabbath of rest unto the land, a sabbath for the LORD: thou shalt neither sow thy field, nor prune thy vineyard.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.5" type="verse">
						That which groweth of its own accord of thy harvest thou shalt not reap, neither gather the grapes of thy vine undressed: for it is a year of rest unto the land.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.6" type="verse">
						And the sabbath of the land shall be meat for you; for thee, and for thy servant, and for thy maid, and for thy hired servant, and for thy stranger that sojourneth with thee,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.7" type="verse">
						And for thy cattle, and for the beast that are in thy land, shall all the increase thereof be meat.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.8" type="verse">
						And thou shalt number seven sabbaths of years unto thee, seven times seven years; and the space of the seven sabbaths of years shall be unto thee forty and nine years.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.9" type="verse">
						Then shalt thou cause the trumpet of the jubile to sound on the tenth day of the seventh month, in the day of atonement shall ye make the trumpet sound throughout all your land.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.10" type="verse">
						And ye shall hallow the fiftieth year, and proclaim liberty throughout all the land unto all the inhabitants thereof: it shall be a jubile unto you; and ye shall return every man unto his possession, and ye shall return every man unto his family.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.11" type="verse">
						A jubile shall that fiftieth year be unto you: ye shall not sow, neither reap that which groweth of itself in it, nor gather the grapes in it of thy vine undressed.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.12" type="verse">
						For it is the jubile; it shall be holy unto you: ye shall eat the increase thereof out of the field.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.13" type="verse">
						In the year of this jubile ye shall return every man unto his possession.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.14" type="verse">
						And if thou sell ought unto thy neighbour, or buyest ought of thy neighbour's hand, ye shall not oppress one another:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.15" type="verse">
						According to the number of years after the jubile thou shalt buy of thy neighbour, and according unto the number of years of the fruits he shall sell unto thee:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.16" type="verse">
						According to the multitude of years thou shalt increase the price thereof, and according to the fewness of years thou shalt diminish the price of it: for according to the number of the years of the fruits doth he sell unto thee.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.17" type="verse">
						Ye shall not therefore oppress one another; but thou shalt fear thy God: for I am the LORD your God.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.18" type="verse">
						Wherefore ye shall do my statutes, and keep my judgments, and do them; and ye shall dwell in the land in safety.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.19" type="verse">
						And the land shall yield her fruit, and he shall eat your fill, and dwell therein in safety.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.20" type="verse">
						And if ye shall say, What shall we eat the seventh year? behold, we shall not sow, nor gather in our increase:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.21" type="verse">
						Then I will command my blessing upon you in the sixth year, and it shall bring forth fruit for three years.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.22" type="verse">
						And ye shall sow the eighth year, and eat yet of old fruit until the ninth year; until her fruits come in ye shall eat of the old store.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.23" type="verse">
						The land shall not be sold for ever: for the land is mine; for ye are strangers and sojourners with me.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.24" type="verse">
						And in all the land of your possession ye shall grant a redemption for the land.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.25" type="verse">
						If thy brother be waxen poor, and hath sold away some of his possession, and if any of his kin come to redeem it, then shall he redeem that which his brother sold.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.26" type="verse">
						And if the man have none to redeem it, and himself be able to redeem it;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.27" type="verse">
						Then let him count the years of the sale thereof, and restore the overplus unto the man to whom he sold it; that he may return unto his possession.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.28" type="verse">
						But if he be not able to restore it to him, then that which is sold shall remain in the hand of him that hath bought it until the year of jubile: and in the jubile it shall go out, and he shall return unto his possession.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.29" type="verse">
						And if a man sell a dwelling house in a walled city, then he may redeem it within a whole year after it is sold; within a full year may he redeem it.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.30" type="verse">
						And if it be not redeemed within the space of a full year, then the house that is in the walled city shall be established for ever to him that bought it throughout his generations: it shall not go out in the jubile.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.31" type="verse">
						But the houses of the villages which have no wall round about them shall be counted as the fields of the country: they may be redeemed, and they shall go out in the jubile.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.32" type="verse">
						Notwithstanding the cities of the Levites, and the houses of the cities of their possession, may the Levites redeem at any time.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.33" type="verse">
						And if a man purchase of the Levites, then the house that was sold, and the city of his possession, shall go out in the year of jubile: for the houses of the cities of the Levites are their possession among the children of Israel.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.34" type="verse">
						But the field of the suburbs of their cities may not be sold; for it is their perpetual possession.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.35" type="verse">
						And if thy brother be waxen poor, and fallen in decay with thee; then thou shalt relieve him: yea, though he be a stranger, or a sojourner; that he may live with thee.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.36" type="verse">
						Take thou no usury of him, or increase: but fear thy God; that thy brother may live with thee.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.37" type="verse">
						Thou shalt not give him thy money upon usury, nor lend him thy victuals for increase.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.38" type="verse">
						I am the LORD your God, which brought you forth out of the land of Egypt, to give you the land of Canaan, and to be your God.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.39" type="verse">
						And if thy brother that dwelleth by thee be waxen poor, and be sold unto thee; thou shalt not compel him to serve as a bondservant:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.40" type="verse">
						But as an hired servant, and as a sojourner, he shall be with thee, and shall serve thee unto the year of jubile:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.41" type="verse">
						And then shall he depart from thee, both he and his children with him, and shall return unto his own family, and unto the possession of his fathers shall he return.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.42" type="verse">
						For they are my servants, which I brought forth out of the land of Egypt: they shall not be sold as bondmen.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.43" type="verse">
						Thou shalt not rule over him with rigour; but shalt fear thy God.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.44" type="verse">
						Both thy bondmen, and thy bondmaids, which thou shalt have, shall be of the heathen that are round about you; of them shall ye buy bondmen and bondmaids.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.45" type="verse">
						Moreover of the children of the strangers that do sojourn among you, of them shall ye buy, and of their families that are with you, which they begat in your land: and they shall be your possession.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.46" type="verse">
						And ye shall take them as an inheritance for your children after you, to inherit them for a possession; they shall be your bondmen for ever: but over your brethren the children of Israel, ye shall not rule one over another with rigour.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.47" type="verse">
						And if a sojourner or stranger wax rich by thee, and thy brother that dwelleth by him wax poor, and sell himself unto the stranger or sojourner by thee, or to the stock of the stranger's family:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.48" type="verse">
						After that he is sold he may be redeemed again; one of his brethren may redeem him:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.49" type="verse">
						Either his uncle, or his uncle's son, may redeem him, or any that is nigh of kin unto him of his family may redeem him; or if he be able, he may redeem himself.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.50" type="verse">
						And he shall reckon with him that bought him from the year that he was sold to him unto the year of jubile: and the price of his sale shall be according unto the number of years, according to the time of an hired servant shall it be with him.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.51" type="verse">
						If there be yet many years behind, according unto them he shall give again the price of his redemption out of the money that he was bought for.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.52" type="verse">
						And if there remain but few years unto the year of jubile, then he shall count with him, and according unto his years shall he give him again the price of his redemption.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.53" type="verse">
						And as a yearly hired servant shall he be with him: and the other shall not rule with rigour over him in thy sight.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.54" type="verse">
						And if he be not redeemed in these years, then he shall go out in the year of jubile, both he, and his children with him.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.25.55" type="verse">
						For unto me the children of Israel are servants; they are my servants whom I brought forth out of the land of Egypt: I am the LORD your God.
					</seg>
				</div>
				<div id="b.LEV.26" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.1" type="verse">
						Ye shall make you no idols nor graven image, neither rear you up a standing image, neither shall ye set up any image of stone in your land, to bow down unto it: for I am the LORD your God.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.2" type="verse">
						Ye shall keep my sabbaths, and reverence my sanctuary: I am the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.3" type="verse">
						If ye walk in my statutes, and keep my commandments, and do them;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.4" type="verse">
						Then I will give you rain in due season, and the land shall yield her increase, and the trees of the field shall yield their fruit.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.5" type="verse">
						And your threshing shall reach unto the vintage, and the vintage shall reach unto the sowing time: and ye shall eat your bread to the full, and dwell in your land safely.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.6" type="verse">
						And I will give peace in the land, and ye shall lie down, and none shall make you afraid: and I will rid evil beasts out of the land, neither shall the sword go through your land.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.7" type="verse">
						And ye shall chase your enemies, and they shall fall before you by the sword.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.8" type="verse">
						And five of you shall chase an hundred, and an hundred of you shall put ten thousand to flight: and your enemies shall fall before you by the sword.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.9" type="verse">
						For I will have respect unto you, and make you fruitful, and multiply you, and establish my covenant with you.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.10" type="verse">
						And ye shall eat old store, and bring forth the old because of the new.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.11" type="verse">
						And I will set my tabernacle among you: and my soul shall not abhor you.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.12" type="verse">
						And I will walk among you, and will be your God, and ye shall be my people.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.13" type="verse">
						I am the LORD your God, which brought you forth out of the land of Egypt, that ye should not be their bondmen; and I have broken the bands of your yoke, and made you go upright.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.14" type="verse">
						But if ye will not hearken unto me, and will not do all these commandments;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.15" type="verse">
						And if ye shall despise my statutes, or if your soul abhor my judgments, so that ye will not do all my commandments, but that ye break my covenant:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.16" type="verse">
						I also will do this unto you; I will even appoint over you terror, consumption, and the burning ague, that shall consume the eyes, and cause sorrow of heart: and ye shall sow your seed in vain, for your enemies shall eat it.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.17" type="verse">
						And I will set my face against you, and ye shall be slain before your enemies: they that hate you shall reign over you; and ye shall flee when none pursueth you.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.18" type="verse">
						And if ye will not yet for all this hearken unto me, then I will punish you seven times more for your sins.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.19" type="verse">
						And I will break the pride of your power; and I will make your heaven as iron, and your earth as brass:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.20" type="verse">
						And your strength shall be spent in vain: for your land shall not yield her increase, neither shall the trees of the land yield their fruits.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.21" type="verse">
						And if ye walk contrary unto me, and will not hearken unto me; I will bring seven times more plagues upon you according to your sins.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.22" type="verse">
						I will also send wild beasts among you, which shall rob you of your children, and destroy your cattle, and make you few in number; and your highways shall be desolate.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.23" type="verse">
						And if ye will not be reformed by me by these things, but will walk contrary unto me;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.24" type="verse">
						Then will I also walk contrary unto you, and will punish you yet seven times for your sins.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.25" type="verse">
						And I will bring a sword upon you, that shall avenge the quarrel of my covenant: and when ye are gathered together within your cities, I will send the pestilence among you; and ye shall be delivered into the hand of the enemy.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.26" type="verse">
						And when I have broken the staff of your bread, ten women shall bake your bread in one oven, and they shall deliver you your bread again by weight: and ye shall eat, and not be satisfied.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.27" type="verse">
						And if ye will not for all this hearken unto me, but walk contrary unto me;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.28" type="verse">
						Then I will walk contrary unto you also in fury; and I, even I, will chastise you seven times for your sins.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.29" type="verse">
						And ye shall eat the flesh of your sons, and the flesh of your daughters shall ye eat.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.30" type="verse">
						And I will destroy your high places, and cut down your images, and cast your carcases upon the carcases of your idols, and my soul shall abhor you.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.31" type="verse">
						And I will make your cities waste, and bring your sanctuaries unto desolation, and I will not smell the savour of your sweet odours.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.32" type="verse">
						And I will bring the land into desolation: and your enemies which dwell therein shall be astonished at it.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.33" type="verse">
						And I will scatter you among the heathen, and will draw out a sword after you: and your land shall be desolate, and your cities waste.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.34" type="verse">
						Then shall the land enjoy her sabbaths, as long as it lieth desolate, and ye be in your enemies' land; even then shall the land rest, and enjoy her sabbaths.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.35" type="verse">
						As long as it lieth desolate it shall rest; because it did not rest in your sabbaths, when ye dwelt upon it.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.36" type="verse">
						And upon them that are left alive of you I will send a faintness into their hearts in the lands of their enemies; and the sound of a shaken leaf shall chase them; and they shall flee, as fleeing from a sword; and they shall fall when none pursueth.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.37" type="verse">
						And they shall fall one upon another, as it were before a sword, when none pursueth: and ye shall have no power to stand before your enemies.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.38" type="verse">
						And ye shall perish among the heathen, and the land of your enemies shall eat you up.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.39" type="verse">
						And they that are left of you shall pine away in their iniquity in your enemies' lands; and also in the iniquities of their fathers shall they pine away with them.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.40" type="verse">
						If they shall confess their iniquity, and the iniquity of their fathers, with their trespass which they trespassed against me, and that also they have walked contrary unto me;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.41" type="verse">
						And that I also have walked contrary unto them, and have brought them into the land of their enemies; if then their uncircumcised hearts be humbled, and they then accept of the punishment of their iniquity:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.42" type="verse">
						Then will I remember my covenant with Jacob, and also my covenant with Isaac, and also my covenant with Abraham will I remember; and I will remember the land.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.43" type="verse">
						The land also shall be left of them, and shall enjoy her sabbaths, while she lieth desolate without them: and they shall accept of the punishment of their iniquity: because, even because they despised my judgments, and because their soul abhorred my statutes.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.44" type="verse">
						And yet for all that, when they be in the land of their enemies, I will not cast them away, neither will I abhor them, to destroy them utterly, and to break my covenant with them: for I am the LORD their God.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.45" type="verse">
						But I will for their sakes remember the covenant of their ancestors, whom I brought forth out of the land of Egypt in the sight of the heathen, that I might be their God: I am the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.26.46" type="verse">
						These are the statutes and judgments and laws, which the LORD made between him and the children of Israel in mount Sinai by the hand of Moses.
					</seg>
				</div>
				<div id="b.LEV.27" type="chapter">
					<seg id="b.LEV.27.1" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.27.2" type="verse">
						Speak unto the children of Israel, and say unto them, When a man shall make a singular vow, the persons shall be for the LORD by thy estimation.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.27.3" type="verse">
						And thy estimation shall be of the male from twenty years old even unto sixty years old, even thy estimation shall be fifty shekels of silver, after the shekel of the sanctuary.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.27.4" type="verse">
						And if it be a female, then thy estimation shall be thirty shekels.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.27.5" type="verse">
						And if it be from five years old even unto twenty years old, then thy estimation shall be of the male twenty shekels, and for the female ten shekels.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.27.6" type="verse">
						And if it be from a month old even unto five years old, then thy estimation shall be of the male five shekels of silver, and for the female thy estimation shall be three shekels of silver.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.27.7" type="verse">
						And if it be from sixty years old and above; if it be a male, then thy estimation shall be fifteen shekels, and for the female ten shekels.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.27.8" type="verse">
						But if he be poorer than thy estimation, then he shall present himself before the priest, and the priest shall value him; according to his ability that vowed shall the priest value him.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.27.9" type="verse">
						And if it be a beast, whereof men bring an offering unto the LORD, all that any man giveth of such unto the LORD shall be holy.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.27.10" type="verse">
						He shall not alter it, nor change it, a good for a bad, or a bad for a good: and if he shall at all change beast for beast, then it and the exchange thereof shall be holy.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.27.11" type="verse">
						And if it be any unclean beast, of which they do not offer a sacrifice unto the LORD, then he shall present the beast before the priest:
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.27.12" type="verse">
						And the priest shall value it, whether it be good or bad: as thou valuest it, who art the priest, so shall it be.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.27.13" type="verse">
						But if he will at all redeem it, then he shall add a fifth part thereof unto thy estimation.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.27.14" type="verse">
						And when a man shall sanctify his house to be holy unto the LORD, then the priest shall estimate it, whether it be good or bad: as the priest shall estimate it, so shall it stand.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.27.15" type="verse">
						And if he that sanctified it will redeem his house, then he shall add the fifth part of the money of thy estimation unto it, and it shall be his.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.27.16" type="verse">
						And if a man shall sanctify unto the LORD some part of a field of his possession, then thy estimation shall be according to the seed thereof: an homer of barley seed shall be valued at fifty shekels of silver.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.27.17" type="verse">
						If he sanctify his field from the year of jubile, according to thy estimation it shall stand.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.27.18" type="verse">
						But if he sanctify his field after the jubile, then the priest shall reckon unto him the money according to the years that remain, even unto the year of the jubile, and it shall be abated from thy estimation.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.27.19" type="verse">
						And if he that sanctified the field will in any wise redeem it, then he shall add the fifth part of the money of thy estimation unto it, and it shall be assured to him.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.27.20" type="verse">
						And if he will not redeem the field, or if he have sold the field to another man, it shall not be redeemed any more.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.27.21" type="verse">
						But the field, when it goeth out in the jubile, shall be holy unto the LORD, as a field devoted; the possession thereof shall be the priest's.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.27.22" type="verse">
						And if a man sanctify unto the LORD a field which he hath bought, which is not of the fields of his possession;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.27.23" type="verse">
						Then the priest shall reckon unto him the worth of thy estimation, even unto the year of the jubile: and he shall give thine estimation in that day, as a holy thing unto the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.27.24" type="verse">
						In the year of the jubile the field shall return unto him of whom it was bought, even to him to whom the possession of the land did belong.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.27.25" type="verse">
						And all thy estimations shall be according to the shekel of the sanctuary: twenty gerahs shall be the shekel.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.27.26" type="verse">
						Only the firstling of the beasts, which should be the LORD's firstling, no man shall sanctify it; whether it be ox, or sheep: it is the LORD's.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.27.27" type="verse">
						And if it be of an unclean beast, then he shall redeem it according to thine estimation, and shall add a fifth part of it thereto: or if it be not redeemed, then it shall be sold according to thy estimation.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.27.28" type="verse">
						Notwithstanding no devoted thing, that a man shall devote unto the LORD of all that he hath, both of man and beast, and of the field of his possession, shall be sold or redeemed: every devoted thing is most holy unto the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.27.29" type="verse">
						None devoted, which shall be devoted of men, shall be redeemed; but shall surely be put to death.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.27.30" type="verse">
						And all the tithe of the land, whether of the seed of the land, or of the fruit of the tree, is the LORD's: it is holy unto the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.27.31" type="verse">
						And if a man will at all redeem ought of his tithes, he shall add thereto the fifth part thereof.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.27.32" type="verse">
						And concerning the tithe of the herd, or of the flock, even of whatsoever passeth under the rod, the tenth shall be holy unto the LORD.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.27.33" type="verse">
						He shall not search whether it be good or bad, neither shall he change it: and if he change it at all, then both it and the change thereof shall be holy; it shall not be redeemed.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.LEV.27.34" type="verse">
						These are the commandments, which the LORD commanded Moses for the children of Israel in mount Sinai.
					</seg>
				</div>
			</div>

					<seg id="b.NUM.1.1" type="verse">
						And the LORD spake unto Moses in the wilderness of Sinai, in the tabernacle of the congregation, on the first day of the second month, in the second year after they were come out of the land of Egypt, saying,
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.NUM.1.2" type="verse">
						Take ye the sum of all the congregation of the children of Israel, after their families, by the house of their fathers, with the number of their names, every male by their polls;
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.NUM.1.3" type="verse">
						From twenty years old and upward, all that are able to go forth to war in Israel: thou and Aaron shall number them by their armies.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.NUM.1.4" type="verse">
						And with you there shall be a man of every tribe; every one head of the house of his fathers.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.NUM.1.5" type="verse">
						And these are the names of the men that shall stand with you: of the tribe of Reuben; Elizur the son of Shedeur.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.NUM.1.6" type="verse">
						Of Simeon; Shelumiel the son of Zurishaddai.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.NUM.1.7" type="verse">
						Of Judah; Nahshon the son of Amminadab.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.NUM.1.8" type="verse">
						Of Issachar; Nethaneel the son of Zuar.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.NUM.1.9" type="verse">
						Of Zebulun; Eliab the son of Helon.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.NUM.1.10" type="verse">
						Of the children of Joseph: of Ephraim; Elishama the son of Ammihud: of Manasseh; Gamaliel the son of Pedahzur.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.NUM.1.11" type="verse">
						Of Benjamin; Abidan the son of Gideoni.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.NUM.1.12" type="verse">
						Of Dan; Ahiezer the son of Ammishaddai.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.NUM.1.13" type="verse">
						Of Asher; Pagiel the son of Ocran.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.NUM.1.14" type="verse">
						Of Gad; Eliasaph the son of Deuel.
					</seg>
					<seg id="b.NUM.1.15" type="verse">
						Of Naphtali; Ahira the son of Enan.
					</seg>

					</seg>

					</seg>

					</seg>
